**Praise and Chant: The Five Directions’ Guardian Spirits’ Spells.**

「This spell is not originally compiled in the *Praise and Chant* section, yet many afflictions arise from hearsay and oral transmission, with numerous errors and distortions. Hence, it is recorded here, so that from childhood one may be instructed in it, and thus apply it throughout one’s life.

Moreover, examining this spell, all its verses are texts to subdue evil (*制邪*), so each contains the character *wǒ* (我, "I/we"). Some mistakenly alter it to *chén* (臣, "subject"), which is incorrect.

After reciting the spell, igniting the furnace, and focusing one’s mind (*存神*), then comes the moment of invoking the *Upper True* (上真) and sealing the decree. There is no taboo in this sequence; it follows the *Golden Talisman Rites* (*金箓仪*) and cross-references the *Dao藏* (*Dao Canon*) for verification.

**East:**
Nine *Qi* of Azure Heaven, the Great Spirit of Bright Stars,
Illuminating the Eastern Region, piercingly revealing the Nine Gates,
Turning radiant the Yang Light, sweeping away filth and dissipating the *fēn* (氛, malevolent influences).
The *Kāimíng* (开明, "Illuminating") Child, guarding my hall (*我轩*),
Binding demons and subduing *yāo* (妖, spirits),
Standing before the Imperial Lord, offering the True *Dao*.
The *Chìshū* (赤书, "Red Scripture") and *Yùzì* (玉字, "Jade Characters"),
the Nine Heavens’ True Commandments, summoning the *Lóngyì* (龙驿, "Dragon Post") to transmit,
universal peace and stability throughout the heavens—*I* attain flying immortality (*飞仙*).
All in harmony; the remaining verses follow the same pattern.

**South:**
The Southern Region of Vermilion Heaven, where the Three *Qi* flow with radiance,
the Glowing Stars revolve like torches, piercingly illuminating the Great Sun.
Above, the *Chìjīng* (赤精, "Vermilion Refined") and *Kāimíng* (开明) Spirit Child,
commanding the Fire Soldiers, guarding the Three Palaces,
beheading evil and binding *yāo*, severing the *Mówáng* (魔王, "Demon King"),
as decreed by the Northern Emperor.
This spell is entirely for subduing demons and spirits, preventing them from disturbing the *Dao*’s sacred grounds (*道场*).

All who practice the *Dao* must subdue the multitude of demons—all belong to the Northern Emperor.
The Northern Clouds are under the Northern Emperor’s jurisdiction; some mistakenly claim this is a Southern spell, altering it to be recited by the *Chìdì* (赤帝, "Vermilion Lord"), which is incorrect.
This confusion is harmful and must be clarified.
The Eight *Chōng* (冲, "Assaults") of Wind and Fire,
jingling bells in alternating brilliance—dare any resist?
The True *Dao* spreads, *I* reap the rewards, safeguarding Heaven’s eternal preservation,
for countless *jiè* (劫, eons), without end.
The phrase "Severing the Demon King" is derived from the *Dao藏*’s ritual procedures (*科仪*), where "魔" (*Mó*, "Demon") is pronounced *xiān* (凶, "calamitous").

**West:**」

The Seven *Qi* (气) of pristine Heaven,
the *Taìbái* (太白, "Great White") pours forth its essence,
illuminating the Golden Gate, piercingly enlightening the Great Darkness.

Within lies the *Sùhuáng* (素皇, "Pristine Sovereign"), named *Dìlíng* (帝灵, "Imperial Spirit"),
preserving and calming the divine, guarding my form,
severing the source of evil—*Wángdào* (王道, "Sovereign Dao/Way") stands clear,
palaces in solemn order, the Three *Jǐng* (景, "Luminaries") aligned,
the Dao/Way harmonizes naturally, ascending to the Purple Court.

The *Língbǎo* (灵宝, "Numinous Treasure") talisman’s efficacy,
universally benefits all beings,
its merit encompassing all—Heaven and Earth alike are pacified.

**North:** The North’s Mysterious Heaven,
where the Five *Qi* (气) linger in motion,
the *Chénxīng* (辰星, "Star of Destiny") blazes resplendent,
illuminating the *Tàiwēi* (太微, "Great Subtlety").

The *Hēilíng* (黑灵, "Dark Spirit") Venerable Deity,
clad in *Fēixuān* (飞玄, "Ascending Mysterious") robes—
some mistakenly alter this to *Fēixiān* (飞仙, "Ascending Immortal") robes, which is incorrect.
This confusion is harmful and must be avoided.

Defending the Five Gates,
refining essence and capturing transgression—
dare any attempt intrusion?
They shall be shattered and annihilated.

The *Yùfú* (玉符, "Jade Talisman") decrees,
the Deity’s might resounds with the Eight *Wēi* (威, "Awe"),
evil gates sealed shut, the True Dao/Way brightly revealed,
its radiance reflected upon my person—
the Three *Guāng* (光, "Luminaries") shine together.
Some mistakenly alter this to *Sānguān* (三官, "Three Officials") piercingly enlightened, which is incorrect.

Riding the void and mastering the floating,
lifting my form to ascend as an immortal.

**Central:** The Yellow Center gathers all *Qi*,
overseeing the governance of immortal truth,
the *Zhènxīng* (镇星, "Guarding Star") emits its radiance,
illuminating the Nine Heavens.

The *Kāiguāng* (开光, "Awakening Light") *Tóngzǐ* (童子, "Boy/Child"),
twelve in number—
their *yuángqi* (元气, "Original Qi") flares with *fánhuá* (梵华, "Buddha-Light") essence,
and the flame ascends as *zhūyān* (朱烟, "Crimson Mist").
Some mistakenly alter this to *yānshàng* (焰上, "Flame Ascends") or *yánshàng* (炎上, "Heat Ascends"), which is incorrect.

Piercingly enlightening the altar and my form,
vanquishing myriad demons,
repelling ten thousand ghosts—
the *Shāngshān* (中山, "Central Peak") Deity’s spell,
universally compels all under Heaven,
the Five *Líng* (灵, "Spirits") are calmed,
and my form ascends to the immortals.

**North:** The *Kāihuáng* (开皇, "Opening Sovereignty") *Xuānshàng* (玄上, "Mysterious Ascension") Five Yang *Fánhùn* (梵混, "Buddha-Blending") *Qi* Treasure Talisman.

the Heavens blend with the Great Darkness.

The *Shénjīng* (神旌, "Divine Standard") flies with black plumes—
the *Shénjīng* is adorned with black plumes and soars.

The *Xuāntiān* (玄天, "Mysterious Heaven")’s script is stern,
its secrets deeply concealed in the Emperor’s ear.

**Text:**

The *Xuānwén* (玄文, "Mysterious Script") is stern—*Xuāntiān* (玄天, "Mysterious Heaven") and *Xuānfēng* (玄风, "Mysterious Wind") are both erroneous.
Demons in throngs revere the Transformed Virtue,
ten thousand realms secure in peace.

**Central:** The *Shànghuáng Zhōnglíng Yīyáng Fánhùo* (上皇中灵一阳梵宝, "Supreme Sovereign’s Central Essence—One Yang Buddha-Treasure") *Qi* Treasure Talisman.
The Yellow Void generates the One *Qi*,
sensing transformations to form the True Essence.
The *Shàngdé* (上德, "Supreme Virtue") upholds gentleness,
golden light piercing the boundless void.

It establishes the Center, encompassing the Nine Extremes,
grasping the Root to govern the Three Celestial Stems.
Its radiance shines at the Heavenly Summit,
its flying beams dazzle the Jade Spirit.

**External Altar Praises**
The rites beyond the altar—each word rooted in *bádú* (拔度, "Extraction-Transformation"),
no trifling matter, especially at this time of mourning.
The host’s sorrow weighs heavy; chanting hymns is ill-suited.
Now, taking previous verses and newly added ones,
to aid the rites, ensuring elegance and propriety.

**Opening Chant (Zhào Míngjǔ’s *Kāifāng Jì*)**
First recite this verse, then open the talisman.
Four voices respond, extolling with intent.

*The Six Glasses* (六璃) reverse the *Yúquán* (虞泉, "Yu’s Spring")’s flow,
city walls and towers dissolve into evening mist.
When the night-watch’s chime first stirs the stillness,
the *Yīnguān* (阴关, "Dark Pass") reopens, ghosts scattering as dust.

At *Yùlóng* (玉隆) the gathering—how shall it proceed?
The inner realms divide their guardians, firm in defense.
To seek the Great Talisman wherever it may be,
one must rely on the True Edict for its proclamation.

**First Degree: Invocation of the Gods’ Verse (Newly Added, for *Dàshèng Xiānyuán Jiàozhǔ*, "Great Sage, Daoist Patriarch")**
Four-toned chant:
The Dragon Chariot descends with *Zǐqīng* (紫清, "Purple Clarity") in tow,
summoning all noble visions, banners unfurled.
The gods arrive from boundless realms,
cloud-wrapped, following the rhythmic beat of the procession.

**Second Degree: Invocation of the Departed’s Verse**
The Nightly Bureau’s cold seals tormented souls,
the *Nǚqīng Tiānzǔ* (女青天诏, "Celestial Decree of the Green Maiden") warms with mercy.
The *Língshěn* (灵婶, "Spiritual Attendant") opens the Dao’s path for wandering spirits,
the *Fǔlì* (符吏, "Talisman Scribes") hasten like swift steeds.

**Third Degree: Invocation Verse**
The Great Dao’s pity fathoms the Six Realms’ depths,
ferrying across the Sea of Suffering with a vessel of mercy.
The Purple Altar’s night opens its conveniences,
ascending to the Great Balance’s unified *Qi*.

**Bathing Verse**
First, recite the Eight Heavenly *Fànwén* (梵文, "Sanskrit Scripts"),
commanding the master to visualize—
draw the *Sānshíèr Tiān Zhēnqì* (三十二天真气, "True *Qi* of the Thirty-Two Heavens") into the bathing water,
then chant this verse.

When the verse ends, a junior disciple recites the script,
leading into the *Kējì* (科偈, "Structured Verse").

All because the heart’s defilements resist cleansing,
drifted in the Sea of Suffering, the body unclean.
The clinging stains of evil barriers remain unremoved,
the serene radiance of purity cannot be revered.
The *Jīnlóng* (金龙, "Golden Dragon") bears the *Chánggēng* (长庚, "Long Star") waters,
the *Yùnǚ* (玉女, "Jade Maiden") distributes the Imperial Seat’s incense.
Three fumigations, three washings—composing dignity,
ascending the *Yǐng* (景, "Shadow") to ride the Void, paying homage to the *Tàishàng* (太上, "Supreme Sovereign").

**Newly Added: Invitation to the Bathing Rites**
Having answered the summons, the departed—
by your recommendation, they have received the warm decree,
escaped the cold realm.
Following the scribes’ hasty steps, they arrive without walking;
glimpsing the distant banners, they respond to the call.
At the veranda’s threshold, they receive the transmitted talismans.
First, they must bathe their bodies, purify their virtue,
adjust their robes, brush their crowns,
reverently relying on the divine incantations,
the protective talismans—
lantern-waters pour to cleanse them,
the Four Spirits guard in attendance,
the Nine *Qi* weave a dense net.

Now, proclaim the Bathing Rites’ script.

**Law-Bridge Verse**
Universal offerings to the Boundless Sage,
incense smoke dispersing across the Ten Directions.
May I ride the Seven-Treasure Platform,
casting light upon the Five Turbid Worlds.
Forever guiding beings of heaven and earth,
all ascending the Law-Bridge.
Gathered in harmony, witnessing the Effortless,
diligently cultivating without retreat.

**Law-Bridge Scripture**
Assemble the Dao Assembly’s participants,
with sincere devotion, pay homage to
the Holy One of the Ten Extremes, the Five Spirits’ guiding youth.
May you grant compassion, specially descending to save and guide.

Indeed, the Sea of Desire is deep and easy to drown in—
one must trace its origins.
The Dao’s shores are high and difficult to ascend—
who will lend a hand?
Through the nature’s enlightenment and delusion,
one’s fate rises or falls between heaven and earth.
Alas, these beings in the turbid world—
their love flows like an ocean, their cruelty surges like waves,
the tides of greed and wrath churn violently,
habits accumulate like drops into torrents,
chasing after objects, the dead fill the sight—
all are self-inflicted.
Yet those who reach the shore are rare in the world.
Is there no path to draw them out?
To rescue those drowning in suffering.

Only the *Tàishàng* (太上, "Supreme Sovereign") pities all beings drowning together,
establishing the wondrous Law as a bridge,
commanding the Ten Extremes’ Celestial Lords to be the sacred pillars of the Dao’s shore,
instructing the Five Spirits’ children to be the ferry across the Sea of Paths,
pulling the lost from their wanderings,
leading them to the other shore.
Crossing the Weak Waters—three million *lǐ*,
transmitting the *Tuánjiāng Fēng* (团刚风, "Clustered-Firm Wind") five hundred billion *zhòng*,
without delay, ascending in a breath—
immediately reaching the realm of unbounded ease.
It depends on the heart’s source,
reflecting the Law’s power,
ever more—
a single step does not stray from the true cause,
nine prostrations to the Primordial Sovereign,
furthermore, the multitude of saints secretly protect,
so that the suffering sea’s souls
all ascend the Law-Bridge.

**Responding Chant**
*Dàdù Tiānzūn* (大度天尊, "Great Virtue Celestial Venerable")—
guide the departed onto the Law-Bridge.

**Next Step**
**Descending the Bridge Verse**
The Law-Bridge spans the Sea of Suffering as a crossing,
the *Tàishàng*’s compassionate vows are boundless.
In the raging waves, they encounter the *Dǐzhù* (砥柱, "Pillar"),
at the love-river’s broken bank, they meet the immortal’s *Yīnyīn* (音雕, "Echo-Carved") sound.
The *Gōngzǐ Língwén* (公子灵旛, "Noble Prince’s Spirit Banner") dispels stagnation,
the Celestial Venerable extends a hand in mutual invitation.
Taking up the martial arts, they descend the bridge toward the Jade Terrace,
the Great Talisman’s unfettered faith in unbounded ease.

**For the Departed: Taking Refuge in the Three Jewels and Repenting Sins**
The departed’s offenses—having received the summons,
they arrive at the Dao Assembly.
Now, the Golden Mouth’s precepts will be transmitted,
the *Dānwén Jiǎnzhù* (丹文简箓, "Cinnabar Script Talismans") will be bestowed.
Yet lingering obstacles remain unremoved,
fearing they may not awaken to the True Words,
reverently relying on the Three Jewels’ radiance,
repenting the Six Roots’ sins.

For sins arise from the heart—
extinguishing the heart dissolves ten thousand faults;
the will finds peace in the Dao—
seeing the Dao, the single spirit shines through.
It is fitting to purify emotions and thoughts,
cleanse the nature’s purity,
quickly abandon illusion to return to the True,
thus hearing the scriptures and attaining the Dao.

Those who perform meritorious deeds, establish vegetarian offerings,
receive talismans and precepts—
first, they must take refuge in the Supreme, True, Ten-Directional Three Jewels,
relying on the Three Jewels’ holy power,
repenting the departed’s threefold karma and transgressions.

Thus the scripture says:
*If one does not take refuge in the Three Jewels,
then all good deeds have no foundation to depend upon.*

The gathered assembly of the Dao-field,
united in sincere devotion.

**Taking refuge in the Ten-Directional Dao Treasures,**
we prostrate to the Primordial Sovereign of Heaven, the Origin,
who can absolve the departed souls of their **body-karma sins**.
We repent the departed’s boundless **body-karma sins**—
their countless transgressions too vast to measure.
In every movement, coming and going,
they were entangled in dust and defilement.
Adorned with vanity, indulging in idle pleasures,
they scorned and mocked the people of the world.

Now before the Great Compassionate Sage,
with one heart, we confess our sins.
May these **body-karma sins** be erased,
never to arise again.
In purity and stillness, we align with the Immortals,
forever free from the Three Boundaries.

**Taking refuge in the Supreme Clarity Scripture Treasure,**
we prostrate to the Highest Dao Lord,
who can absolve the departed souls of their **mind-karma sins**.
We repent the departed’s boundless **mind-karma sins**—
their countless transgressions too vast to measure.
Anger, joy, and love for the clergy,
delusion arising from the heart.
Lust and emptiness, deceit and envy,
they wronged the people of the world.

Now before the Great Compassionate Sage,
with one heart, we confess our sins.
May these **mind-karma sins** be erased,
never to arise again.
With wisdom and insight, our minds now clear,
penetrating the profound and mysterious principles.

**Taking refuge in the Supreme Purity Teacher Treasure,**
we prostrate to the Highest Old Lord,
who can absolve the departed souls of their **speech-karma sins**.
We repent the departed’s boundless **speech-karma sins**—
their countless transgressions too vast to measure.
Double-tongued and slanderous,
they defamed the sacred scriptures.
Devouring living beings, they humiliated the people of the world.

Now before the Great Compassionate Sage,
with one heart, we confess our sins.
May these **speech-karma sins** be erased,
never to arise again.
Cutting off false speech, we forever recite the True Scriptures.
In past devotion to the Three Treasures,
our repentance was the supreme cause.
May the departed now ascend to the celestial realms—
flower-adorned canopies await,
cloud-bound messengers come to welcome.
Crimson banners and azure banners,
midair guides lead the way.
Beneath the cypress groves, they forever hear the Dao’s teachings.
By the Pearl Moon Pool, only sacred hymns resound.
All sins of their past life,
now forever dissolved.

「After death, the Three Realms are traversed through present explanations.
Ascending on dragons and riding phoenixes, they wander freely through the ten highest heavens;
Realizing the Dao and attaining transcendence, they dwell in the boundless realms of the Three Pure Ones.

Blessings flow and manifest in this life and the next,
with constant fruits of merit arriving—
in this world and the next,
everlasting kinship with the Way is achieved.

The Great Sage of the Highest Path,
in His boundless compassion,
rescues all living beings,
together ascending to the Dao’s shore.

**A Second Hymn on the Inconceivable Virtues**

With humble obeisance, I take refuge in the Dao,
the Venerable Primordial Lord of Great Unity.

In the boundless void of ancestral kalpas,
from the chaos of the primordial root,
I pray You descend the Teachings of Clarity and Tranquility,
to deliver this departed soul.

All the departed,
ascend to the realm of the Immortals—
*(below follows the same for the other two Treasures)*

With humble obeisance, I take refuge in the Scriptures,
the True Words radiant in all eight directions.

Refining gold into phoenix seals,
molding jade into dragon characters,
I pray You open the Golden Mouth to expound,
and deliver this departed soul.

With humble obeisance, I take refuge in the Master,
the Venerable One among the Three Vehicles.

From before the heavens, You show boundless mercy,
through kalpas, You guide the lost and the deluded.
I pray You descend infinite teachings,
to deliver this departed soul.

I repent the sins of the departed’s eyes, ears, nose, tongue, body, and mind—
the six senses, six desires, and six afflictions.
Flutes and strings resound with little true sound,
while ears delight in purple and green hues, not pure colors.

Noses compete in perfumes of orchids and musk,
tongues revel in the clamor of chariots and horses.
The body indulges in spicy excess, harming the spirit,
the mouth speaks in unchecked wrath, only seizing others’ wealth.
The mind clings to the six senses’ sins—
each sense draws the wheel of rebirth,
or even the Three Paths of suffering—
this is an error.

The Three Treasures always open the gates of salvation.
With present sincerity, I confess past transgressions,
and utterly wish for all sinful roots to be extinguished.

Next, I repent the sins of greed, anger, delusion, and ignorance—
of licentiousness, theft, killing, and falsehood.
Of defaming the Scriptures and destroying the Teachings,
not taking refuge in the Dao.
Of blaming the Way and faulting the Master,
breaking solemn vows.
Of restless fantasies in body and mind,
of senses ever stirred by greed.
From past, present, and future lives,
the sins of the Three Worlds are immeasurable.
Today, with heartfelt repentance, I confess,
and pray that all past obstructions and afflictions be removed.

Having now confessed with words to the Dao’s presence,
the multitude of saints, seated in the void,
will surely witness and judge.
The inconceivable virtues are invoked—
each with a finger-snap,
to atone for the departed’s sins.

May the departed’s bodily sins be erased,
their mental sins be erased,
their speech-karma sins be erased,
their six senses be purified,
their grudges be dissolved,
their karmic obstructions be dissolved,
all their sins be dissolved.
May the departed’s countless sins melt like frost and dew,
under the universal rays of grace.

In this life and the next,
their inherent nature remains forever serene and tranquil.
The departed soul emerges from the endless night,
no longer stagnant, now bound for the Immortal Source.

The Northern Capital cleanses the texts of past offenses,
the Southern Palace inscribes the characters of eternal life.
The Immortal hymns echo through the void,
no longer hearing the agonized voices of the underworld.

All present here vow with utmost sincerity—
may the departed ascend to heaven and find joy.

The above two hymns,
both from the *Nine Abysses Rite*,
are attributed to the Venerable Master Guangcheng.

After repentance and the granting of precepts,
the departed are guided back to their proper place—
now follows the consolation:

The departed, [name],
having already taken refuge before the Three Pure Ones,
received the Nine Precepts in person,
now stand in solemn reverence,
listening with awe and accepting with devotion.

Again, prepare the ceremonial feast,
each in their proper order,
partaking of fragrant offerings,
awaiting the completion of the grand auspicious cause.

The host gazes upon the spirit,
with pious sincerity, offering homage.
If [the departed] were fed by incantations,
then do so now.
If not fed by incantations,
then dedicate this feast back to them,
and perform the *Nine Abysses Rite*.

The *Rite for Escorting the Departed* is now complete—
the feast has ended, the law-assembly dispersed.

Receive the blessings of goodness,
and together bathe in extraordinary merit.
Following the radiant wisdom-light,
they behold the Celestial Sage.
Holding the talismans of fate,
they ascend to the Immortal Realm.

The departed, [name],
having now heard the Scriptures and listened to the Teachings,
must surely perceive their true nature and know the heavens,
and in reverence, await the Alchemical Chariot,
then rise upon the Cloud Path,
crossing the Immortal Bridge,
and at this moment, ascend to the **Red Peak Palace**.

Having now attained transcendence in this time,
each carries forth blessings—
the host, with pious sincerity,
will dutifully escort them.

**Verse**

The law-assembly’s grand merit is now fulfilled,
the departed, though distant, are fully delivered.
All together cross the Immortal Bridge,
each bearing virtues to pay homage to the Three Pure Ones.

**For Daoist Communal Teachings**
The Daoist communal teachings must employ the *Three Chapters of the Scripture of Gathering*.
The Daoist communal teachings must employ the *Four Chapters of the Scripture of Gathering*.」

「The Daoist Master Lü Taigu’s *Collection of Petitions*
**Petitionary Verse**
To the Highest Functionary’s Imperial Desk—
Fragrant incense ascends, its prayers like jade flowers blooming,
Nine breaths of *qi* enfolded in mist,
Dense incense clouds weave through the heavens,
Directly piercing the Nine Celestial Realms.

The Golden Boy attends with incense,
The Jade Maiden relays the words,
Before the Celestial Sovereign,
All who hear my humble plea
Grant their favor as I speak.

**Hand-Held Incense Petition**
The Dao/Way arises from heart-mind study,
Mind transmitted through fragrant incense,
Hand clutching the jade burner,
Heart set toward the Nine Celestial Heights.

The True Spirit descends in grace,
Divine adornments attend the court,
My Lord commands me to proclaim—
Directly ascending to the Three Heavens.

**Incense on the Alchemical Altar Petition**
The Crimson Sun soars through the Nine Exalted Realms,
The luminous essence of the Primordial Crystal refined.
The Spirit Phoenix comes to perch,
Ascending to the Celestial Court of Jade.

Karmic bonds dissolve through transformation,
The Daoist Path achieves its triumph.
May this Alchemical Prayer,
Like smoke, swiftly ascend.

**Hand-Held Incense Petition**
A hundred deities arrayed in ritual,
Mind focused on the Cavernous Sun.
To the left, the True Marshal commands,
To the right, the Primordial Sovereign draws near.
Unfolding the Sacred Scroll,
The Great Brahman flourishes.
Purple smoke ascends to the heights,
Ten thousand Dao/Paths expand in splendor.

**Petitionary Verse for the Incense Offering**
Humbly heard, the boundless realm of the **Great Clarity (Taiqing)**,*
Across lifetimes, mere dust;
The august, peerless **Supreme Venerable (Wushang)**,**
Ever distant, no trace among mortals.
With reverent fasting and purification,
I now present my earnest supplication,
Hoping for a private descent of scrutiny,
A slight display of the wondrous transformation of **sentient response (ganhua)**.

Gazing afar upon the Cloud Chariot,
Temporarily departing the **Purple Expanse and Vermilion Gate’s** solemn grandeur,*
Adorned with celestial crowns and stars,
Together revealing the **Jade Treasury and Pearl Banner’s** sacred mysteries.**
With utmost sincerity, I humbly pray—
May the Heavens accept my words, as spoken.

**Altar Petitionary Text**
Humbly heard, the lofty tiers of clouds,
The Heavens do not close the path of **sentient response (ganhua)** and communion;
The human Dao/Way is vast and distant,
Yet the Saints ever descend in private grace.
With solemn reverence in my home,
I now devote myself to the **Pure and Exalted Rites (jingjiao)**.
I present the humble offerings of earthly plants,
I kindle the sacred incense to the heavens,
Daring to reveal my simple thoughts,
Humbly seeking the **Great Construction’s** divine favor.

Now, with respectful devotion to the **Celestial Science (xianke)** of this year,
I pray for the extension of the True Chariot,
Truly marking the beginning of this **fasting assembly (jianzai)**,
The first expression of my sincere service to the **Celestial Sovereign (shidi)**.

Though my offerings are meager,
The Dragon Chariot’s blessings I earnestly await.
Only this turbulent, defiled land,
Fearing to offend the Highest Clarity,
Gazing upon the **Buddha’s** fragmented form,
Increases my trembling awe.

Humbly I hope for the Cloud Chariot and Crane Procession,
Descending through the **Ninefold Celestial Gate (tiantian)**;
Vermilion banners and rainbow flags,
Halting in the **Five Impurities of the Human Realm (wuzhu)**.
The **Three Realms of Jade Emptiness (Yuxu)**,**
The **Ten Thousand Spirits of the Golden Gate (wanzhu)**,
Temporarily leaving the distant heavens,
Descending to fulfill my devout and earnest prayers.

I command the **Spirit Official of the Realm (Lingguan)**,
To solemnly oversee this **rite of purification (jiao)**.
I decree the **Guardian Officers of the Altar (weitanjiangli)**,
To drive away all malevolent influences.
May my sincere intentions resonate in **sentient response (ganhua)**,
And my fasting rites achieve their purpose,
So that I may immediately receive the **Highest Saint’s** descending grace.

**The Petitioner’s Words**
The **Altar Petitionary Text** is thus universally employed.»

The Petitioner’s Humble Words

I have heard that the **Supreme Immortal of Tranquil Stillness** acts without doing yet responds perfectly; the **Mysterious Void Dao** ever subtly communicates through attunement. Without sincere invocation of the **Numinous Methods**, how could one aspire to the **Sacred Workings**?

Now that the **Sacred Altar** has been established and the **Rite of Purification** is about to commence, I first humbly pray to the **Celestial Spirit**, then unfold the **Dao’s Precepts**. May it penetrate the **Nine Heavens above**, so all may hear and know; may it illuminate the **Three Realms below**, so all may be moved and respond. May the **Supreme Virtue** be broadly bestowed, encompassing all sentient beings.

**The Yellow Register Rite’s Sacred Petitionary Text**
The **Yellow Register Sacred Rite**, the **Purple Yang Secret Pattern**, above can **stabilize Heaven and pacify Earth**, below can **protect the nation and bring peace to the home**. It rescues the living and saves the dying, extends life and delivers from peril—held in reverence by the **Ten Thousand Heavens**, followed by the **Thousand Saints**. Its teachings unfold across the **Nine Periods**, drawing from the **Nine Yang Numbers**; its altar is structured in **Three Levels**, branching into the **Three Qi Blossoms**. It aligns the **Eight Trigrams** with the **Eight Directions**, fixes the **Ten Celestial Stems** in their **Ten Positions**. It opens the **Heaven Gate** and the **Earth Portal**, the **Ghostly Path** and the **Human Way**. The **bows and flags**, **mirrors and swords** are arrayed in solemn order; the **trays and vessels**, **earthen jars and gourds** are offered in humble simplicity. Thus does it **model Heaven and mirror Earth**, **communicate with the True and summon the Spirits**.

We, the petitioners, now begin our **first reverence**, our **initial homage**. Before the **Jade Stair’s** infinitesimal space, we dare not be disrespectful; beneath the **Celestial Countenance’s** near presence, we stand as if already above. We humbly pray that the **Three Pure Ones and Ten Extremes**, the **Ten Thousand Saints and Thousand Immortals**, temporarily leave the **Golden Gate’s** lofty heights, descending to survey the **dusty world’s** confined depths. May this humble abode become the **Pure Capital’s** celestial residence, awaiting Your gracious descent—our reverence and longing know no bounds.

**The Petitioner’s Words on the Rite’s Sacred Petitionary Text**
Thus, when the altar is first opened, the **Heavenly Gates** stand wide, the assembly is solemn and silent, our hearts pure and sincere. We emulate Heaven’s grandeur and Earth’s humility, arranging the **Heavenly and Earthly** in order; we gaze left to the **Ceremonial Standards**, right to the **Jade Carvings**, the gates aligning with **Sun and Moon**. We focus our intent within the **elaborate scriptures and ritual systems**, attuning to the **dim, elusive** yet **manifest** Spirits. With **seven days of abstinence** and **three days of fasting**, we honor the ancients’ devotion to the **Celestial Sovereign**; with **inner resolve and outward sincerity**, we pledge today’s unyielding honesty. We open the **Treasure Altar of All Marvels**, fulfilling the **past year’s and present wishes**, inviting the **feathered sages** to chant the **Deep Chapters**. The **Celestial Procession** ascends with thunderous might, the **Sacred Waters** flow like clouds and rain.

We humbly pray to the **Star Palaces and Moon Halls**, the **Vermilion Gates and Pure Capitals**, the **Deepest Mysteries**, the **Saints of the Triple Profound**. From the **Heaven of Heavens**, descending from the **Symbol Beyond Symbols**, You traverse the void with flying steps—**Zhi-Tong children** bearing **feathered banners** lead the way; **dragon chariots** and **wind-riding steeds** bring You swiftly down. You deign to observe the **fragrant offerings**, to accept the **humblest sincerity**, bestowing blessings on the living and the dead, extending mercy to the hidden and the manifest. We have already received the **Highest Spirit’s** oversight—how could we forget the **Great Response’s** omen? We await Your descent with reverent longing.

**The Petitioner’s Words on the Altar’s Sacred Petitionary Text**
All **Three Realms’ responsive Spirits**, all **True Essences**, may You hear our petitions and descend to the **fragrant altar**. Having bathed in Your radiance, we now humbly present our earnest prayers. We envision the **celestial melodies**, the **feathered retinues** standing in solemn ranks. The **wind-blown canopy** and **cloud-borne palanquin** drift near; the **rainbow banners** and **vermilion flags** appear and vanish. The **Supreme Truth** descends to this mortal realm—the **Purple Palace’s** and **Cinnabar Sky’s** processions arrive. You pause at the **changing world**, the **Jade Pool’s** and **Moon Gate’s** splendor, temporarily halting the **phoenix carriage** to survey our sincere hearts, revealing our hidden devotion, and ascending to the **Great Workings**.

I have heard that the **Dao ever responds to humanity**, Heaven ever listens below. With our **sincere devotion**, how could we neglect the **solemn beginning**? We exhaust our **inner sincerity** and **outer offerings**—the altar follows the **law’s measurements**, the **earthen jars** prioritize **substance over ornament**. The **sacrificial tokens** are arranged, each symbolizing the **Five Directions’ colors**; the **headgear and robes** are arrayed, dividing the **multitude’s ranks**. The **Dragon-Torch** flickers in **divine light**, the **incense beasts** congeal in **auspicious mist**. The **willow branches** are purified, the **flower petals** scatter in profusion. When the **high and low** take their positions, it is the moment of **Heaven and humanity’s mutual response**—**Heaven’s威** is near, the **clouds** rest in serene stillness, the **Spirits descend**, demanding utmost solemnity.

We humbly pray that the **Celestial Countenance** grant favor, the **Heavenly Gates** open wide, the **Ten Thousand Chariots** begin their journey, the **Hundred Spirits** guard the path. The **Lion and White Crane** bear the **Heavenly Standards** forward; the **Responding Dragon and Azure Qiu** guide the **Imperial Chariot** swiftly. May You not reject our **mortal sincerity**, so that the **rite’s purpose** may be fulfilled, and we may receive the **Saints’ descending grace**.

**The Petitioner’s Words on the Sacred Petitionary Text for Inviting the True**
Furthermore, we pray that the **Xiao-Shao melodies** lead the way, the **canopied carriages** follow behind. The **mist wraps the rainbow robes**, the **clouds float above the moon veils**; the **Wind Lord** clears the path, the **Rain Master** washes the dust. The **Celestial Procession** moves through the **Heavenly Roads**, scattering **treasure flowers** across the **Dharma Realm**. The **swift-flying retinues** descend to the **Dao Field**. We hope to glimpse You through the **dissipating mists**, to bare our hearts in **sincere entreaty**.

Now, as the evening’s **sincere devotion** begins and our **earnest prayers** are presented, the **rites of welcome** are complete, and our **attunement** is without flaw. The **round altar** is arranged, the **ranks of High Immortals** take their places. The **group of Spirits** departs from the **Emerald Caverns and Jade Palaces**, the **assembly of Saints** descends from the **Golden and Jade Halls**. They bear **banners and canopies**, **treasure umbrellas** following the **celestial carriages**, their **clouds** ascending like **jade**, their **light** gleaming like **stars**. The **Celestial Countenance** is solemn, **dark robes** held in readiness to listen to mortal pleas; the **Tai Mountain’s** grandeur stands firm, **golden tablets** presented to inspect the **rite’s solemnity**. The **Southern Bureau** takes up the brush to record the **virtuous** for **rebirth**; the **Northern Bureau** awaits to inscribe the **meritorious** for **salvation**.

At this very moment, even a fragment of virtue shall not fear the Three Realms’ ignorance;
With this resolve, even a slight merit shall not be surprised if the multitude of Immortals fail to record it.

How much more so when one’s devotion is profound and the assembly is sublime—
When the incense altar is solemnly arranged,
And one cultivates the twelvefold mind of virtue,
Following the three-nine gradations of fasting discipline—
Who would dare say the Saints and Worthies do not respond to mortals?
Why doubt that the hidden and manifest alike are not touched by their grace?

It is not the Dao that expands humanity—
Humanity that expands the Dao.

Now, we invite the Immortals’ passing gaze,
Follow the ritual protocols to seal the covenant,
Unfold our sincere pleadings,
And humbly appeal to the Great Work.

We humbly pray that the Three Pure Ones of the Three Realms,
The Ten Directions and Ten Glories,
The Marvelous Conducted Immortals,
The True Great Saints,
The Nine-Heavenly Star Manifestations,
And the Three Realms’ Awe-Inspiring Spirits—
May they emit the five-colored auspicious light,
Cast the Nine-Peak treasure canopy,
Descend upon this sacred assembly,
Accomplish our virtuous deeds,
All as we supplicate—
And thus, the response shall be immediate and resonant.

Your servants, in reverence, declare:

Previously, we submitted a white petition to the Five Masters.
Now, the ritual feast begins, the fasting rites commence.

We gaze upon the Three Realms’ idyllic groves,
Concentrating our hearts in silent contemplation;
We summon the Nine Pure Ones’ swift celestial chariots,
Raising our hands in earnest devotion.

The array of crowned and adorned Immortals stands majestic,
Their awe-inspiring presence hovering in ethereal form—
Yet how can we reach the Jade Capital’s golden gates,
The Purple Palace’s alchemical platform,
The Celestial Palaces of Sun and Moon,
The Azure Sky’s starry halls and the Pole Star’s domain?
They soar beyond all earthly symbols,
Far beyond mortal reach—
How can we convey the sincerity of the humble,
Or offer the modest rites of the lowly?

The Masters’ treasures have long encompassed the Dao’s grace.
Now, this ritual fasting is established—
Its sincerity must be spread, its devotion must reach.

Your servant, [name], humbly reflects:
For long have I partaken in the Mysterious Transformation,
Long basked in the True Wind’s breath.
Today, I choose this auspicious hour,
Reverently fulfilling my heart’s wish.
Whether fortune or misfortune, I offer rites with utmost reverence and respect,
Speaking truth, not empty words.
Yet, alas, my understanding of the Dao’s worth is unheard,
And I am ignorant of the True Methods.
By mistake, I have been entrusted with this proclamation.

We humbly beseech the Five Masters of the Numinous Treasures,
The Moral and Daoist Saints—
Do not reject our earnest plea,
And grant us the boundless embrace of the Great Virtue.

We request that the Four Departments and Five Imperial Officials,
Along with their attendants,
Attest to this fasting ritual,
Ascend our sincere wishes,
Examine our petitions,
And in secret bestow their blessings.
May they ensure that at each moment, our prayers are relayed,
Our supplications answered,
Our wishes fulfilled,
Our virtuous deeds made manifest,
Our oaths steadfast and sincere—
So that we may, in reverence, repay their grace.

Your servants, in devotion, declare:

The altar is erected, the furnace ignited.

The **prayer** is earnestly offered to the lofty heavens,
The **heart** devotes itself to serving the **Celestial Sovereign**;

The **Purple Clouds** descend to this humble earth,
And the **Method** of summoning the **True One** is solemnly observed.
At the moment when the **Sage** first responds through **spiritual resonance**,
When the **ritual platform** is established and the **auspicious rites** commence,
We uphold **sincerity** and **earnestness**,
And dare to invoke the **Celestial Majesty**.

This **servant of the Dao**, by virtue of past **karmic causes**,
Was born in the **Land of the Five Directions**,
Possessing the **Four Great Virtues** of the realm,
And sharing in the **numinous essence** of all ten thousand things.

Our **fleshly bodies** are frail as silk,
Yet we endure the **sufferings** of the **hunted hare**;
Our **forms** are human, yet our **Daoic countenance** remains,
Fortunate to retain the **compassionate grace** of the **Sage**.

The **recompense** has not yet appeared in the **smallest particle**,
Nor has the **gratitude** faded from **day and night**.

On this **auspicious day** of **good fortune**,
With **reverence** and **resolve** in our initial **vows**,
As the **water clock’s arrow** first begins its passage,
And the **ritual bell’s tone** is newly struck,
We light the **Nine Veiled Lamps**,
Burn the **sublime incense** of myriad wonders—
Cleansing the **dusty tumult** so that the **celestial breeze** is pure,
Raising the **yin-qi** so that the **night’s luminosity** grows cold.

All the **three or four nights** of **devoted practice**,
Are fulfilled in **one step** of **sincere observance**.

May our **humble supplications** ascend and be heard,
May the **Celestial Sovereign’s** wisdom pierce through the **distant void**,
Temporarily leaving the **Primordial Chaos**,
And descending to this **jewel-pure ritual field**.

The **Celestial Maidens** and **Golden Boys**,
Dispense **heavenly fragrance** in **dense clouds**;
The **rainbow banners** and **crimson flags**,
Mingle with the **flowering rain** in **splendid array**.

Not neglecting the **lowliest blade of grass**,
Nor failing to **slightly comfort** the **long-held wishes** of the years.

Thus do we humbly address the **Five Masters of the Daoic Rituals**,
At the **forefront of the fasting assembly**.

...your humble servant hears that the **Primordial Dao** established its teachings first,
And the **Great Unity** (*Hunyuan*) already receded into **non-action** (*Wuwei*).

Across countless **kalpas** (*eons*), the **Sage** dispenses salvation to all beings,
And the **treasure of the Teacher** (*Shifu*) rests upon the **favor of the Celestial Sovereign** (*Jianming*).

Thus, in the **Mysterious Core** (*Xuanzhong*), the **Celestial Master** (*Xuanzhong*) assumes his sacred office,
Overseeing the **fasting assembly** (*Zhai*) with solemn vigilance—
Transmitting the **canon** (*Jingji*) through successive generations,
Relying upon the **Three Realms** (*Heaven, Earth, and Humanity*) for shared support,
Responding to each **spontaneous impulse** (*Suijin*) as it arises,
Granting every **sincere wish** (*Yuan*) without fail.

Now we establish this **Treasure Fasting Hall** (*Baozhai*),
Uniting the **visible and invisible** (*Youming*) to bring benefit and deliverance.
We pray that the **Celestial Sovereign** may descend upon the **dusty world** (*Chenjie*),
Bestowing grace and blessings to **pervade and extend**.

With utmost reverence, we lay bare all **common sentiments** (*Fanqing*),
And humbly beseech the **Teacher’s craft** (*Shizao*).

**At dawn** (*Qingdan*), when **Great Clarity** (*Daming*) arises from the **eastern quarter** (*Shufang*), free of all **dusty veils** (*Chenyi*),
Even as **night qi** lingers in the **level dawn** (*Pingdan*), how could **illness** (*Juezhuang*) perish?
The **Cloud Chariot** and **Crane-Drawn Vessel** hover in **leisurely flight** (*Paihuai*),
While the **wild horses** of **earthly turbidity** remain **unmoved** (*Buzheng*).

If we **entrust our fate** (*Chenming*) to the **Celestial Master’s** decrees as **disaster dissolves** (*Xiaozai*),
And **renew our stored blessings** (*Zai’chu*) with **sincere devotion** (*Qing*),
His **pity for all life** (*Haosheng*) shall be our guiding virtue—
Entering our **intentions**, may the **pure dawn** (*Jingdan*) now **practice the Dao** (*Xingdao*),
Sealing the **ritual petitions** (*Guanzou*) to the **Highest Spirit** (*Shangling*),
Humbly awaiting the **Teacher’s True Essence** (*Shizhen*), that he may **descend and grant his blessings** (*Chui’ao*).

May our **sincere devotion** (*Daocheng*) be **guided and perfected** (*Daocheng*) as the **radiant sun** (*Rao*) ascends,
And our **hidden faults** (*Qianxia*) be **subtly cleansed** (*Qianxue*) like **thin ice** melting away.
So that each **fragment of virtue** (*Pianshan*) may **prevail** (*Kexu*) beyond **demonic obstacles** (*Mozhang*),
And the **vast Teacher’s blessings** (*Hong’en*) may **pervade** (*Tian*) both **visible and invisible** (*Youming*),
Our **grateful hearts** (*Gandai*) ever **present in our thoughts** (*Shizai*).

**At noon** (*Linwu*), the **fasting rites** are **strict** (*Zhiyou*),
Beginning and ending with solemn reverence—
The **Sage’s heart** (*Shengxin*) is **unimpeachable** (*Gezhong*), neither **partial** nor **biased**.
See how the **Sage** reveals the **Great Centrality** (*Dazhong*) to all,
Like the **sun’s chariot** (*Yijiu*) driving **true and upright** (*Zhengli*), beneath the **midday sun** (*Zhongri*).
No **hidden darkness** escapes its light,
All **ten thousand things** draw upon it for their **formation and growth** (*Shengcheng*).
Every **sentiment** finds its way through,
A **single thought** strikes at it and **resonates** (*Koudazhou*).
Thus, when we now **stand at noon** (*Linwu*),
We **again approach** (*Zai*) to **offer our sincerity** (*Shucheng*),
Unveiling our **heartfelt words** (*Ciqing*),
And **daring to petition** (*Maogan*) the **Teacher’s ear** (*Shitong*).

As it has been spoken above (*Yuruyun*).
**In the still night** (*Jingye*).

The **Four Seasons** resound with clarity,
The sky is free of haze and filth,
The **Divine Wind** stirs in silence,
The earth is cleansed of all malevolent dust.

The **Big Dipper’s handle** stretches across the void,
Lifting **heartfelt words** to the celestial expanse;
The **moonlight** washes the night,
Chilling the **qi** in bone and hair.

Trembling with reverence, we **diligently** extend our offerings;
With **lofty sincerity and depth**, we humbly await the **Teacher’s** gracious hearing.

We **press upon** the **True One’s** essence,
Hoping to fulfill all that should be done.

As it has been spoken above (*Yunyun*).

**The Original Command Scripture**

Above, it mirrors the **Heavenly Vault** (*Huntian*),
Dividing the **Three Celestial Exaltations** (*Sanxing*) along the **Lunar Lodges** (*Jingwei*) and **Solar Paths** (*Wei*).

**Great Clarity** establishes its teachings,
Spreading the **Two Dipper Stars** (*Erdou*) across the **Water** (*Kan*) and **Fire** (*Li*) constellations.

It proclaims the **Original Command’s** grand framework,
Unfolding the **Mysterious Spirit’s** essential keys.

For **humanity’s foundation** lies in the **Seven Elements** (*Qi Yuan*).
Heaven’s **Dipper’s Crown** (*Doubei*) measures the **Original Qi**,
Binding **life and fate** to the **Five Bodies** (*Wuti*).
It governs **longevity and early death**,
Determining a life’s rise or fall.

Thus, when the **cosmic cycles** unfold,
One must **contemplate the Six Degrees** (*Liu Du*),
To descend blessings upon the mortal realm,
Extending the **fragrance and light** for all to **return and invest**.

Therefore, those who attain **three lifetimes’ merit** as **sons of the Dao**,
Should **observe fasts and establish rituals** (*Zhai Jiao*),
Contribute according to their means,
Offer water and flowers in gratitude,
Repaying **karmic roots** as circumstances allow.

At the **Boar Hour** (*Jianchen*), they must not let the moment pass in vain,
But **ascend in reverence**, extending **longevity’s blessings**—
Their voices should rise like **grain’s resonance**,
Their light should answer like **reflections**.

**Entering the Mind**

**The True Martial Scripture**

---

**Entering the Mind**

**The True Martial Scripture**

In the **Pure Celestial Domain** (*Ta Qing*), the **forms and colors** (*se xiang*) are not absent but **serene and still** (*zhan ji*). Descending to the **Northern Pole** (*Bei Ji*), its **awe and authority** (*wei quan*) are **fierce yet benevolent** (*he her yi ci ren*).

It **views the people as wounded** (*shi min ru shang*), **grinding its teeth** (*qie chi*) against the **proliferation of demons** (*qun mo zhi si kuo*). **Compassion for life** (*hao sheng wei zhong*) is paramount, **pushing forth its heart** (*tui xin*) to stir the **sorrow of all beings** (*zhao shu zhi xing ai*).

It **assists the upright and crushes the perverse** (*fu zheng cui xie*), **dissipating calamities and bestowing blessings** (*xiao zai jiang fu*). Though **forty-two years of Daoist cultivation** (*sui shi er jian chen xiu dao*) and **thousands of rituals’ fulfillment** (*san qian yu hang zhi cheng gong*) may be required, the **origin from the Golden Gate’s transformation** (*ben cong jin que zhi hua shen*) and the **manifestation of all beings’ proof of enlightenment** (*ming shi zhong sheng zhi zheng guo*) are what enable it to **circulate through the six directions** (*zhou xing liu he*), **commanding awe in all beings** (*wei she wan ling*).

**All five pestilences** (*wu wen*)—**minor demons** (*xiao mo*)—
and the **six heavens’ malevolent qi** (*liu tian zhi gu qi*), **ensnared in white dragon shadows** (*zhong bai hong ying guo*), **dissolve into dust** (*hua zuo chen ai*).

With **dual eyes flashing like lightning** (*shuang jing dian zhong*), **it exterminates all remaining evil** (*chao wu yu lei*).
Thus, **demonic evils are annihilated** (*de yi mo ying mie*), **and households and states alike are at peace** (*jia guo xian ning*).

On the **seventh day of each month** (*mei yue san qi zhi chen*), the **True Lord descends to the mortal realm** (*shi zhen jun jiang fan zhi ri*), one should **extend offerings of fragrance and light** (*yin xian huo zhi gong fu*), **to repay favors and rest** (*yi da en xiu*).

**The Scripture for Pacifying the Dwelling**
Hearken to the **age of Youxiao** (*You Chao Shi zhi shi*), when people **ate acorns and chestnuts** (*shi xiang li zhi*) and **lived in trees, nesting** (*qi mu ju chao*).
In the **time of Xuanyuan** (*Xuan Yuan Shi zhi shi*), they **changed their homes** (*yi dong yu*) to **shelter from wind and rain** (*dai feng zhi yu*).

Thus, the **old and young among the people** (*shi min ren zhi lao you*) may **rest securely** (*an zuo xi*) in **dawn and dusk** (*xiao hun*).

Only the **Sage** (*Sheng Ren*) **adapts to the needs of things** (*qi wu zhi yi*), **for the greatest benefit of all under heaven** (*wei tian xia suo li zhi da*).

Yet, **Yin and Yang have shifts of ascendance and decline** (*yin yang you yi fu zhi bian*), **cold and heat bear pestilential evils** (*han shu you ci li zhi xie*). When people **transgress these** (*ren huo mo zhi*), **calamities are unavoidable** (*zai suo bu mian*).

Thus, the **Highest Sovereign** (*Tai Shang*) **commands the spirits and assigns duties** (*ming shen ling er shou zhi*), **to guard the dwellings of common folk** (*wei fan fu wei zhe yu*). **Dividing their roles** (*yi fen si*), **the Grandfather Star** (*Tai Sui*) is held in **highest reverence** (*wei zun*), **and one year is taken as the standard law** (*yi yi nian wei zhun fa*). **Compassion for life** (*hao sheng wei zhong*) is their **primary duty** (*zhu yu*), **and banishing evil comes first** (*qu e zhi ju xian li*).

The **spirits of the Heavenly Pit and Magua Mouth** (*tian keng ma kou zhi shen*), **swallowing demons and devouring ghosts** (*tun mo shi gui*).
The **clan of Yellow Grinding Wheels** (*huang mi zhi shu*), **with leopard tails** (*bao wei*), **protect the righteous and crush the perverse** (*hu zhe cui xie*).

**In their proper positions, they discern directions** (*zheng wei bian fang*), **securely maintaining their duties** (*tuo ling shou zhi*).
They **declare the Highest Sovereign’s awe and authority** (*xuan tai shang wei quan zhi hua*), **warding off all beings’ potential for harm** (*fang zhong sheng heng hai zhi yu*).

Who would have thought that **people vary in wisdom and folly** (*shi ren you xian yu mo*), **ignoring prohibitions and warnings** (*wang ming jin ji*)?
The **spirits are bold and fierce** (*shen wei yong han*), **knowing no distinction between light and dark** (*mo jian you ming*).

To **offend them** (*fan zhi*) is to **invite calamity without cause** (*wu gu mo zhi fen*).
To **provoke them** (*gan zhi*) is to **ensure disasters and misfortune** (*bi shi zai xiong zhi bian*).

Fortunately, the **Highest Sovereign** (*Tai Shang*) **twice pities common folk** (*cai min fan fu*), **issuing talismans** (*chu fen wen*) **to bring peace** (*an ning*), **proclaiming incantations** (*xuan zhou fa*) **to serve as warnings** (*jing jie*). All **hundreds of spirits obey its commands** (*bai shen ting qi ling*), **and hidden ghosts submit to its oaths** (*you gui qing qi meng*). Thus, **those who transgress in ignorance** (*mo fan zhe zhuan huo wei xiang*) **turn misfortune to good fortune** (*huan zai zhi fu*), **and those who return and invest** (*gui tou zhe que zai zhi fu*) **avoid disasters and attain blessings** (*xu zai zhi fu*). **Humans and deities alike benefit** (*ren tian meng li*), **and households and states share its grace** (*jia guo zhan en*).

The **Daoist Gate’s universal teachings** (*dao men tong jiao*) **must employ the four final volumes** (*bi yong ji juan zhi si jing*)—
**The Yellow Arrow Talisman** (*Huang Que Dao Shi Lü Tai Gu Ji*), **Volume One: For the State’s Scripture** (*Guo Zhi Tan Jing Wen*).

The **Scripture of the Dao and Its Virtue** (*De Dao Jing*) is **the text of non-action** (*wu wei zhi wen*), **the transformation of nature** (*zi ran zhi hua*). It stands **unbounded beyond the Great Desert** (*luo luo tai mo zhi biao*), **towering before the August Emperor’s image** (*wei wei xiang di zhi xian*). **The two qi** (*er qi*) **rely upon it to establish their roots** (*zi zhi yi li gen*), **the three luminaries** (*san guang*) **hold it to form their manifestations** (*chi zhi yi cheng xiang*). **Subtle yet all-pervasive** (*xi wu bu ru*), **vast yet all-encompassing** (*da wu bu bao*), its **true essence** (*qi zhen*) **governs the self** (*yi zhi yi shen*), **and its practice** (*qi tu*) **extends to all under heaven** (*yi xing jia qie yu shen zhi yi cheng xiang*). Its **function** (*qi gong*) **elevates all beings** (*du qun pin*), **and its profound subtlety** (*qi wei miao*) **can attain immortals** (*zhi shen xian*).

In ancient times, **Laozi passed through Hanguang Pass** (*Lao Zi zhi guo Han Guan*), **bestowing eighty-one chapters** (*shou ba shi yi zhang*) **before departing**. **Emperor Wen of Han** (*Han Wen zhi cong*) **followed the Yellow River’s teachings** (*cong he shang zhi jiao*), **and though seventeen centuries passed**, **the transmission remained** (*gai qian qi bai nian er jin chuan*). **Exhausting the inexhaustible** (*qiong hu wu qiong*), **reaching the limitless** (*ji hu wang ji*), it **proclaims the essentials of the Dao and Virtue** (*xuan dao de zhi yao*), **serving as the teacher of emperors** (*wei di wang zhi shi*).

As for **ascending to the Mysterious** (*sheng xuan*), **it expounds the sounds of purity** (*yan qing jing zhi yin*), **entering the gates of myriad marvels** (*ru zhong miao men*), **while transcending all defilements** (*li zhu ran zhe*). It **expiates calamities and lists the ranks of repentance** (*rang zai lie chui hui zhi pin*), **delivering all beings from adversity** (*du yi qie e*). **Whatever it treads upon is secure and at peace** (*suo li ping an*).

**The Yellow Emperor composed the Scripture of the Dark Symbol** (*Huang Di zhuo yin fu zhi shu*), **which can be employed as a teacher against ten thousandfold adversaries** (*ke yong shi yu wan bei*).
**The Green Silk robe transmitted the incantations of celestial luminaries** (*qing luo chuan xing yao zhi zhou*), **which can manipulate the cycles of the Five Phases** (*ke tui yun yu wu xing*).

All these **unlock the singular decision** (*jie yi jue*), **revealing the mysteries of the Dao** (*shen dao zhi yu wei*), **and expound the hidden profundities of the Mysterious Pivot** (*yan xuan zong zhi yin ao*). **Reciting it makes one’s voice resonate with the Supreme Ultimate** (*song zhi ze sheng can tai ji*), **studying it elevates governance to peace and harmony** (*yan zhi ze zhi hua sheng ping*). **Disasters vanish from the Nine Yin** (*huo mie jiu yin*), **and blessings permeate all ten thousand realms** (*ze han wan yu*).

**The blessings flow to the lineage and community** (*qing liu zong she*), **and sitting in meditation, one faces boundless rest** (*zuo dui wu jiang zhi xiu*).
**The incantations align with the Sage and the Deity** (*qing ge shen ren*), **silently dissolving the insoluble adversities** (*qian xiao nan jie zhi e*).

Again, **offering hymns of praise** (*zai yin ji zong*), **to complete the eulogy** (*yi jin zan yang*).

---
**First Scripture: The Scripture of the Dao and Its Virtue** (*De Dao Jing*)
*Establishing the Primordial Extremes to Govern Difficulties* (*Xian Tian Li Ji Zhi Nan Ming*), **vague and indistinct** (*huang huo*), **rare and elusive** (*xi yi*)—**this is the root of the true** (*zhi ben gen*).
**The celestial steps eternally clear** (*tian bu yong qing xuan ri yue*), **the Dao’s pivot unmoving** (*dao shu bu dong zhuan qian kun*).
**The spiritual source directly severs all paths of delusion** (*ling yuan zhi duan qun mi jing*), **the immortal path broadly opens myriad gates of marvel** (*xian lu hong kai zhong miao men*).
**The Sage’s longevity matches the August Extremes** (*sheng shou mian chang huang ji jian*), **may my words align with the Lord of the Primordial Hour** (*yuan yan chen ji yu qi zun*).

---
**Second Scripture: The Scripture of Transcending and Elevating** (*Qian Ba Tan Jing Wen*)
The **Scripture of Delivering Beings** (*Du Ren Jing*) is **the highest of the Three Caverns** (*san dong shang pin*), **the profound speech of the One Vehicle** (*yi cheng miao yan*). It **harmonizes with the songs of myriad demons** (*can zhong mo zhi ge yin*), **and proclaims the hidden melodies of all spirits** (*xuan bai ling zhi yin yun*).

In ancient times, **it was bestowed upon the soil of the Jade Decline** (*bei yu bi luo zhi tu*), **and hidden within the Purple Micro’s Palace** (*cang yu zi wei zhi gong*).
**The Brahma’s breath** (*fan qi*) **permeates all realms** (*mi luo*), **encompassing the ten directions’ boundless expanse** (*zhou shi fang wu ji zhi jie*).
**The Golden Essence’s brilliance** (*jin zhen lang yu*) **radiates**, **illuminating the eight heavens’ empty caverns** (*huan ba tian kong dong zhi zhang*).

**Its words flow freely yet without ornamentation** (*wen chang er qu bu hua*), **its depth profound yet its meaning ever more subtle** (*qu you er yi yi ao*).
It **reaches the marvelous intent within the Mysterious** (*ji xuan zhong zhi miao zhi*), **far beyond the common speech of the world** (*fei shi shang zhi chang ci*).
Those who **chant it** (*yong zhi zhe*) are **listed among the Jade Chamber’s ranks** (*ming lie yu fang*).
Those who **hear it** (*wen zhi zhe*) **have their spirits soar to the Golden Gate** (*shen fei jin que*).

**All ten thousand emperors set forth their rites** (*wan di she li*), **all demons bind their forms** (*qun yao shu xing*).
Even **those who attain celestial birth** (*sheng tian tong wei ao zhi yan*) **and comprehend the profound mysteries** (*qing jing kai zhen chang zhi xing*), **are cleansed by the tranquil initiation of true constancy** (*shi sheng jing zhi zhen chang zhi xing*).
**The ten directions reverently uphold the sacred treasure of salvation** (*shi fang yan jiu ku zhi bao jun*), **and the Nine Abysses receive the spiritual scripture of the seal of the heart** (*jiu you shou xin yin zhi ling pian*). **All beings are universally delivered** (*pu du tian ren*), **the ferry across life and death** (*jin liang sheng si*). Thus, **those who face the long night of suffering** (*ba dui zhi chang ye*) **are all listed among the ranks of the Highest Purity** (*xian lie ming yu shang qing*).

Again, **reciting verses** (*zai yin ji zhang*), **to extend salvation and deliverance** (*yi jin ji du*).
**The Jade Book and Golden Tablet deeply deliver beings** (*yu shu jin jian du ren shen*), **flowing from the boundless compassion of the Benevolent Lord** (*liu chu ci zun guang da xin*).
**The Brahma’s breath forms the boundless expanse** (*fan qi jie cheng wu ji jie*), **and the natural sounds of the celestial winds drift** (*tian feng piao fan zi ran yin*).
**The Nine Abysses break their shackles, ice melting like spears** (*jiu you po jie bing xiao ji*), **the Eight Extremes ascend with fragrance, the moon full upon the sleeves** (*ba ji fei xiang yue man jin*).
**Bowing with reverence, none can match the Sage’s guidance** (*qi shou wu ying qi jie yin*), **the divine light shatters the deepest darkness** (*shen guang yi dao po zhong yin*).

「以实坎，画于朔易之都；
**With the solid and receptive** (*kàn*), **its form is inscribed upon the realm of the Dark Beginning and the Great Simplicity** (*shuò yì*).

虚之以离，焕乎文明之位。
**With the empty and luminous** (*lí*), **it shines upon the station of refined clarity** (*wén míng*).

陶铸万品，统御三元；
**It molds the myriad things** (*wàn pǐn*), **governing the Three Primordial Powers** (*sǒng yǔ sān yuán*).
五行得之以成，七政得之以运。
**The Five Phases** (*wǔ xíng*) **find their completion through it, the Seven Celestial Officials** (*qī zhèng*) **move in accordance with it.**

道生於一，而着於水火之用；
**The Dao** (*Way*) **arises from the One, yet manifests in the functions of Water and Fire.**
物散於万，而极於水火之功。
**Things disperse into the myriad, yet reach their utmost in the operations of Water and Fire.**

南北二经，盖尽兹蕴。
**The Two Great Canons of the South and North** (*nán běi èr jīng*) **comprehensively exhaust this profound essence.**

昔太上之下降，命天师之密传。
**In ancient times, the Most High** (*Tài Shàng*) **descended and commissioned the Celestial Master** (*Tiān Shī*) **to secretly transmit** (*mì chuán*) **its teachings.**

浮玉局於地中，敷扬秘诀；
**The Floating Jade Array** (*Fú Yù Jú*) **was established within the earth, and the profound secrets were expounded.**
化鹤鸣之山上，亲授灵文。
**Upon the Mount of the Transformed Crane’s Resonance** (*Huà Hè Míng*), **the Most High personally bestowed the numinous texts** (*líng wén*).

可以荐福消灾，可以注生削死；
**It can present blessings and dispel calamities** (*jiàn fú xiāo zāi*), **it can bestow life and diminish death** (*zhù shēng xuē sǐ*).
永除业障，渐入仙宗。
**It eternally removes karmic obstructions** (*yǒng chú yè zhàng*), **and gradually leads one into the Daoist lineage of transcendence** (*jiàn rù xiān zōng*).

且天童开护命之符，而真武有降福之愿。
**Moreover, the Celestial Youth** (*Tiān Tóng*) **unfurls the talisman of protection for life, while the True Martial One** (*Zhēn Wǔ*) **holds the aspiration to bestow blessings.**

上智广真一之训，报劬劳恩；
**The highest wisdom expounds the precepts of the True One** (*Zhēn Yī*), **repaying the laborious merits of devotion.**
静观达智慧之门，明解脱义。
**Through tranquil contemplation, one attains the gate of wisdom** (*zhì huì*), **and clearly comprehends the meaning of liberation** (*jiě tuō yì*).

功德甚重，不可具陈。
**The merits and virtues are profound** (*gōng dé shèn zhòng*), **too vast to fully recount.**

辄引偈章，以伸赞叹。
**Thus, verses of praise are invoked to further extol and celebrate.**

芝坛香霭露华稀，云际风高鹤盖飞；
**Upon the mushroom dais** (*zhī tán*), **incense vapors rise while dew-laden blossoms scatter thin; at the cloud’s edge, winds surge high as the crane’s canopy takes flight.**

玉宇寥寥鸣警跸，金光奕奕下丹墀；
**In the vast jade heavens** (*yù yǔ*), **the solemn toll resounds, and golden radiance** (*jīn guāng*) **shimmers upon the vermilion steps** (*dān tí*).

愿倾法雨除尘垢，更乞仙丹造道微；
**May we pour forth the Daoist teachings as rain to cleanse the dust of delusion, and further seek the elixir of transcendence to refine the subtle path of the Way.**

两卷真经香一瓣，自兹根极欲知归；
**With two volumes of the true scriptures and the scent of a single incense offering, from this moment onward, we earnestly desire to return to the roots and extremes of the Dao.**

忏悔 道家仪文，至於巢先生，号为大备。
**The rites and texts of Daoist repentance** (*chàn huǐ*), **as perfected by Master Niao** (*Cháo Xiānsheng*), **are called the Great Completion** (*Dà Bèi*).

文字皆有所出，或儒书，或道书；
**All texts have their origins—some from Confucian writings** (*rú shū*), **others from Daoist scriptures** (*dào shū*).
剸裁铺张，自有体制，一字不可移易。
**They are meticulously edited and expansively arranged** (*chuǎn cái pū zhāng*), **possessing their own systematic structure; not a single character can be altered or transposed.**

惟忏悔文，消灾、迁拔两篇，又多取庄子；
**Yet the texts of repentance** (*chàn huǐ wén*), **particularly the two chapters on *Dispelling Calamities* and *Ascending and Extracting*** (*xiāo zāi, qiān bá*), **draw extensively from the *Zhuangzi*.**
使人闻之，洗濯疏瀹，有清心向道之意。
**When heard, they purify and clarify the mind, inspiring one to cultivate a pure heart and turn toward the Dao.**

未烛厥理者，或有改易，增加书字，殊为可笑。
**Those who fail to penetrate their meaning may attempt alterations or additions, which is most laughable.**

故书之，以告将来。
**Thus, they are recorded to instruct future generations.**

黄箓启坛忏悔
**Repentance with the Yellow Talisman** (*Huáng Luó*) **at the Initiated Altar:**

臣法众等，至心归身、归神、归命十方无极太上灵宝天尊；
**Your devoted subjects, the Lawful Assembly** (*Fǎ Zhòng*), **with utmost sincerity, dedicate our bodies, our spirits, and our lives to the Most High, the Lord of Supreme Treasure** (*Líng Bǎo Tiān Zūn*), **boundless in all directions, the One Beyond Extremes.**

圆穹列曜星辰，厚地洞天、海岳醮筵；
**Under the domed heavens adorned with luminous constellations** (*yuán qióng liè yào xīng chén*), **and upon the vast earth of cavernous purity, the altar of mountains and seas** (*hǎi yuè jiào yàn*).
感降一切真灵。
**We humbly pray for the descent of all true numinous beings** (*qǐng jiàng yīqiè zhēn líng*).

伏愿大慈，洞回昭鉴，同垂巨泽，普降洪恩。
**We earnestly wish that the Great Compassion** (*Dà Cí*) **penetrate our hearts with clear discernment, equally bestow vast blessings, and universally grant abundant grace.**

臣闻天无亲，而所辅在德；
**We have heard that Heaven has no favorites, yet it aids those who possess *virtue/power* (***dé***).**
福无门，而所召在人。
**Blessings have no fixed gate, yet they are summoned by human aspiration.**

仰归众妙之门，必应群心之用。
**We turn toward the gate of myriad wonders, and it must surely respond to the collective intent of all hearts.**

宝笈箸度人之法，独步玉京；
**The methods of salvation through the Precious Talismans and Golden Tablets** (*Bǎo Jiǎo Zhù*) **are unparalleled in the Celestial Capital** (*Yù Jīng*).
驿龙驰奏善之章，上朝金阙。
**The Dragon of the Celestial Relay gallops to present the chapters of virtuous deeds at the golden gates of the Celestial Court** (*Shàng Cháo Jīn Kuò*).

每灵心之丕应，见天意之孔昭；
**Whenever the numinous heart responds profoundly, the will of Heaven becomes manifestly clear.**
皆太上垂慈济拔之科，而天下奉道修为之路，□蛮如答，神明罔违。
**All are the Most High’s decrees of compassionate salvation and extraction** (*Cí Jì Bá*), **and the paths by which all under Heaven revere the Dao and cultivate their practices—obedient as the wild tribes, with no deviation from the divine will.**

伏念臣法众等，暨斋官某等；
**We humbly reflect upon Your devoted subjects, the Lawful Assembly, and the officials of the fast** (*zhāi guān*).
生逢盛明，志慕虚静；
**Born in this age of radiant clarity** (*shèng míng*), **we aspire to emulate the void and tranquil** (*xū jìng*).
清天君而疏瀹，断业障以皈依，
**We purify the Celestial Sovereign** (*Tiān Jūn*) **and clarify our hearts, severing karmic obstructions to take refuge.**
谒欵在辰，斋明有翼，
**Our offerings are presented in the auspicious hour, and our fasts are illuminated with wings of virtue.**
将以交三灵於恍惚，祷百顺以延长。
**We seek to commune with the Three Numinous Ones** (*Sān Líng*) **in the realm of the ineffable, and pray with a hundred virtues to prolong our lives.**

尚虑宿运功微，前缘德薄；
**Yet we fear that our past destinies are weak in merit, and our former karmic roots are thin in virtue.**
今生往劫，多纵罪根；
**In this present life and past kalpas, we have repeatedly indulged in the roots of transgression.**
俗骨凡胎，未阶真品；
**With mundane bones and ordinary flesh, we have not yet attained the true essence.**
虽道心之甚固，恐天听之难闻。
**Though our hearts for the Dao are steadfast, we fear that our supplications may not be heard by Heaven.**

伏愿上圣哀怜，洪恩荡宥；
**We humbly pray that the Most Holy** (*Shàng Shèng*) **take pity upon us, and that the vast grace sweep away our offenses.**
拔九祖之魂於既往，贷三世之罪於将来；
**May we extract the souls of the Nine Ancestors from the past, and be pardoned for the sins of the Three Worlds in the future.**
洗六根以一新，秉纯诚而无贰。
**May we purify the Six Senses to renew them anew, and uphold absolute sincerity without doubt.**

庶几寡过，仰格上真；
**Thus, we may hope to have few transgressions, and be accepted by the Most High.**
用修黄箓之科，延召紫清之福。
**Through the practice of the Yellow Talisman** (*Huáng Luó*), **we seek to invite the blessings of the Purple Clarity** (*Zǐ Qīng*).

臣等稽首礼谢无上至真三宝。
**We prostrate ourselves in reverence and gratitude to the Three Treasures of the Most High and Supreme Truth.**

散坛忏悔
**Repentance at the Dispersed Altar:**

臣闻强名曰道，本清静以无为；
**We have heard that the Dao** (*Way*) **is called the "Strong Name"** (*Qiáng Míng*), **its essence being the void and tranquil with non-action.**
不测者神，有感通而必应。
**The unfathomable is the numinous** (*Shén*), **which responds when there is feeling and communication.**

再荡涤於尸秽，终对越於灵真。
**Again, we purify ourselves from the defilements of the mortal body** (*shī huì*), **and ultimately transcend to meet the numinous and true.**

伏念臣等，仙品未充，业根尚在；
**We humbly reflect that our transcendent nature is yet incomplete, and our karmic roots remain.**
虽稽参於宝箓，常讽诵於真经，
**Though we kneel and study the Precious Talismans, and frequently recite the true scriptures** (*Zhēn Jīng*),**
宣举教科，修行斋直；
**We proclaim the teachings and their precepts, and practice the rites of fasting and purity.**
虑有违於道范，曾未沃於灵心，
**We fear that we may have strayed from the Dao’s norms, and have yet to nourish our numinous hearts.**
辄更澄练身形，洗除尘染，
**Thus, we further refine our physical forms, cleansing away the dust of defilement.**
扩性天而一毫莫翳，拂心鉴而内境圆明；
**We expand our nature to match the heavens, with not a single hair obstructing clarity, and we brush away the mirror of our hearts so that our inner realms are perfectly luminous.**
萝此修持，用祈感格。
**With this cultivation, we seek to invite the numinous response of Heaven.**

伏愿众真□略，上圣涵容；
**We humbly pray that the myriad numinous beings** (*Zhòng Zhēn*) **overlook our shortcomings, and that the Most Holy embrace our sincerity.**
凡朝谒非仪，坛壝不肃；
**Our ordinary offerings and visits are not in accordance with ritual, and our altars are not solemn.**
千愆万过，并乞贷原。
**With myriad faults and countless offenses, we earnestly seek pardon and forgiveness.**

臣等稽首礼谢无上至真三宝。
**We prostrate ourselves in reverence and gratitude to the Three Treasures of the Most High and Supreme Truth.**

消灾忏悔
**Repentance for Dispelling Calamities:**

臣闻尽天下之物，不足以交神明；
**We have heard that all things under Heaven are insufficient to commune with the divine and luminous** (*Shén Míng*).**
修胸中之诚，斯可以应天地。
**Yet cultivating sincerity within the heart can respond to Heaven and Earth.**

矧乃玄元之教，莫非清静之门。
**How much more so with the teachings of the Primordial Mystery** (*Xuán Yuán*), **which are all gates of void and tranquil.**

傥三业六根之过存，岂一精二纯之能格。
**If the transgressions of the Three Activities and Six Senses persist, how could the single essence and dual purity suffice to overcome them?**

当斋科之谨始，欲尘累以先除；
**At the solemn beginning of fasting and ritual practice, we first seek to eliminate the accumulated dust of defilement.**
庶藉宣扬，以伸昭格。
**Thus, through proclamation and exposition, we may further manifest the clear response of Heaven.**

臣今忏悔奉道某等；
**We, the certain ones who serve the Dao, now repent.**
因从旷功，逮及今生；
**From the beginning of our vast merits, extending to this present life,**
有妙湛之体，而为情所昏；
**we possess the profound and luminous essence, yet are obscured by passions.**
有虚明之用，而为物所蔽。
**We possess the void and clarity of function, yet are veiled by things.**

欲恶盛而性有雈音完苇；
**The passions for desire and aversion are rampant, yet our nature resounds with the harmonious sounds of *Zuo* and *Yin* (symbols of purity and truth).**
闻见疏而智亦聋盲。
**Our perceptions are coarse, and our wisdom is deaf and blind.**

不能外身而多身殃，不能缄口而多口过。
**We cannot transcend the body, thus incurring many bodily afflictions; we cannot seal our mouths, thus accumulating many verbal transgressions.**

意有所至，爱有所忘；
**Our thoughts reach far, yet our affections are lost in forgetfulness.**
积其有涯之生，造徧无边之罪。
**We accumulate the finite life of existence, and create widespread, boundless offenses.**

今则对列真而忏悔；
**Now, we stand before the numinous and true, and repent.**
体妙道以修为。
**We embody the profound Dao to cultivate our practices.**

诸业生於诸根，尘尘是妄；
**All activities arise from the Six Senses, and each particle of dust is illusory.**
有身孰不有患，物物迷真。
**With a body, who does not have afflictions? Each thing veils the true.**

爰即灵坛

**The flattering deceits of insincerity are all removed,
the clinging evils of greed are utterly purged.
Past deeds already wrought shall never again tread the wheel of retribution;
future calamities yet to befall shall never be cast into the abyss.

Thus may we preserve the body whole and keep harm at bay,
never chasing profit while forsaking the True.

With humble devotion, we pray to the Radiant Saints:
May their luminous insight pierce through all darkness,
and with the waters of the Jade Pool,
purify the hearts of all;
with the blossoms of Ambrosial Dew,
cleanse away all defilements.

May the roots of guilt wither and vanish,
and the luminous wisdom-nature shine perfectly round.
With reverence, we follow the rites of storing virtue,
to fulfill the pattern of prolonging life.

If not the birthday of the Sage,
then let us instead cultivate a steadfast heart for goodness,
awaiting the blessings of benevolent grace.

May misfortune sink into the Nine Abysses,
and blessings spread across the Ten Directions.

We, the humble servants, prostrate and offer thanks to the Supreme Triple Jewel of the Most High True One.

**On Repentance:**
This repentance is for living beings still in existence,
to purify the mind and still the thoughts,
to serve the Celestial Sage with clarity—
not for the departed, lest there be misunderstanding of intent,
and names of the dead be mistakenly invoked,
for human affairs and the Dao are utterly distinct.

I have heard:
To seek the True Essence beyond form,
the Dao is pure and boundless;
To awaken vast aspirations within the world,
its principle returns to purity and stillness.

「To purge the external afflictions is not enough—
only then may one behold the Celestial Sage’s luminous presence.

To repent and cleanse the dust of worldly attachments—
only then may one properly fulfill the rites of the **sacrificial hall (斋直)**.

Now, we humble servants repent and dedicate ourselves to the Dao,
from the distant past through countless **kalpas (劫)**, down to this very life.
All deeds of body, speech, and mind,
witnessed by Heaven, Earth, and humanity—**the Six Perceptions (六见)**.

Where there is a body, there is great affliction,
long-accumulated sins and transgressions;
all actions arise from the **Six Senses (六根)**, yet the **evil obstructions (恶障)** remain unremoved.

To indulge in **sensual pleasures (声色)**, to abandon oneself in licentiousness,
when **vital energy (血气)** is strong, the calamity of strife arises;
when **desires (嗜欲)** overflow, the sickness of life and death beckons,
ever turning from the True to the False,
struggling to free the mind while binding the spirit.

At the commencement of these **sacrificial rites (斋事)**, we fear the **Nine Heavens (九霄)** may remain distant.
We wish to bathe in the **Great Mysterious Waters (太玄之水)**,
to wash away the **Six Evil Roots (六恶根)**;
to seek the **Six Perfections (六度)** as a vessel,
to reach the **Dao’s shore (道岸)**.

To cultivate the **fruit of non-outflow (无漏果)**,
to block the **pathways of all malevolent forces (众邪门)**;
to cleanse the **Five Poisons (五菔)** and **Six Dusts (六尘)**,
to sever the **Ten Fetters (十缠)** and **Nine Bonds (九结)**.

With one heart enlightened,
all sins dissolved into emptiness.

We vow from this day until the next life,
never again to ensnare ourselves in the **net of karma (业网)**.

May the **Pure Celestial Court (清都)** observe our sincere devotion,
and the **Supreme Polarity (紫极)** return its boundless grace,
acknowledging our earnest striving,
and bestowing its vast benevolence generously.

For **past sins (阴愆)** and **present transgressions (阳过)**,
whether **retribution from former lives (上世流注之殃)**,
or **entanglements with the Six Relatives (六亲)**—
these ties, whether **fated in past incarnations (宿世所造)** or **slandered by enemies (仇家所诬)**,
the **poisonous winds and malevolent qi (毒风恶气)**,
the **torment of demons and malevolent beings (魔鬼凶人)**—
we pray that the **Dao’s wind (道风)** may sweep them all away,
cleansing and purifying the **form and spirit (气形)**,
so that at the **sacrificial altar (坛枪)**,
we may stand upright before the **Nine Ancestral Spirits (九祖)**,
and attain the **fruit of the Celestial Sage (上仙)** in the future.

May we ascend to the **Everlasting Spring of the Nine Heavens (九天不夜之长春)**,
and reach the **Realm of the Celestial Caverns (洞阳)**;
with **Three Kinds of Karma (三业)** unrooted, we depart forever
from the **host of malevolent ghosts (万鬼)**.

Blessings spread across the **Ten Directions (十方)**,
misfortune sinks into the **Nine Abysses (九夜)** forever.

We, the humble servants, prostrate and offer thanks to the **Supreme Triple Jewel of the Most High True One (无上至真三宝)**.

**On the Opening of the Way (外坛开方):**
The texts for opening the way are not singular;
the most fitting originates from **Master Chao (巢先生)**’s cultivation of goodness.
Others may recount the **virtues of the Five Phases (五行之德)**,
or explain the **origins of ghosts and gods (鬼神之由)**—
these too are appropriate, yet none surpass the efficacy of this text alone.

The **Nine Dragons (九龙)** bear the decree,
ascending the spirits accumulated in darkness;
the **Six Ghosts (六鬼)** clash in battle,
cutting off the path to rebirth.

The **Most High (太上)** manifests through the **illuminated teachings (明训)**,
and the **Divine Official (神公)** sweeps away the inauspicious.
With reverence, we present the **sacred rites (典彝)**,
and humbly extend our **petitions (关告)**.

To hope for the **Bright Spirits (明灵)** to respond,
we first rely on the **chanting of the Daoist hymns (梵呗)** to exalt their names.
We invoke the **Universal Compassion (众慈)**,
and all voices resonate in harmony.

We take refuge in the **Eastern Lord (东方主)、Jade Treasure Emperor of Heaven (玉宝皇上天尊)**,
the **Southern Lord (南方主)、Heavenly Emperor of Supreme Truth and Ten Thousand Blessings (玄真万福天尊)**,
the **Western Lord (西方主)、Heavenly Emperor of Ultimate Marvel and Supreme Polarity (太妙至极天尊)**,
the **Northern Lord (北方主)、Heavenly Emperor of Supreme Mystery and Jade Purity (玄上玉宸天尊)**,
and the **Central Lord (中央主)、Heavenly Emperor of Supreme Unity and Rescue from Suffering (太乙救苦天尊)**,
whose **inconceivable merits (不可思议功德)** are vast.

With incense now burning,
we earnestly invoke the **Five Directions’ Open Path Great Gods (五方开路大神)**,
the **Earthly Sovereigns (地界主)**.

May the **Divine Benevolence (神慈)** descend and accept,
the **sacrificial altar (香坛)** bear witness,
and our **sincere prayers (虔祷)** enter their hearts.

Indeed, the **unfathomable interplay of yin and yang (阴阳不测)** is the **Divine Mystery (神之妙)**;
the **limitless transformations (变化无方)** are the **True Dao (道之真)**.

Only the **Most High (太上)** encompasses the **Divine Mystery of yin and yang (阴阳不测之神)**,
and exhausts the **True Dao of endless transformations (变化无方之道)**.

With **Six Penetrations (六通)** and **Four Liberations (四辟)**,
its power endures eternally;
instantaneous departures and sudden arrivals,
piercing all obstructions with clarity.

Descending as spirits to fulfill **manifestations (赴感)**,
embodying the Dao to respond to humanity.

Those who receive **transmission (受度)** are not divided by life or death,
and those who return to the **True Dao (皈真)** are not bound by distance or proximity.

Let it be so that a thousand years may pass in an instant,
and ten thousand miles become as near as a hand’s span.
At the **sacrificial rites (醮席)**, we listen to the **lawful sounds (法音)**,
and in the **Celestial Court’s morning (朝上帝)**, we ascend to the **True Dao (登真)**,
hearing the **song of the void (空歌)** while awakening to the **Way (悟道)**.

Should any **pursued spirit (灵识)** fail to arrive at the altar,
or if **all earthly officials (地司)** dare to obstruct with deceit,
hindering the **wandering souls (幽魂)** or blocking the **path to rebirth (生路)**,
the **Heavenly Decrees (天宪)** are stern,
and the **True Dao’s rites (真科)** will not be forgiven.
