Now, the **sacrificial official (斋官)** of this household
commences these **extraordinary rites (殊常之斋范)**,
inviting all **high Daoists (高真)** of the **Three Realms (三界)**.
Lanterns and stars stretch across the **Jade Slip (玉绳)**,
and incense smoke ascends to the **Golden Gate (金阙)**.

Hearing the **hidden melody of the Celestial Courts (诸天一声之隐韵)**,
all **karma of a hundred lives (百生之业障)** dissolves;
listening to the **piercing chapter of the Nine Judgments (司马九过之洞章)**,
the **forms and spirits of the Three Thousand (三万之形神)** are fully manifested.

The **departed ascend, the living are transformed (前亡后化)**—
at every moment, spirits rise.
Yet we still fear the **three worlds’ lost souls (三世幽魂)**,
and **nine springs’ trapped spirits (九泉滞魄)**,
those who have not yet been **offered salvation (荐拔)**,
suffering the utmost **pity and lamentation (悲酸)**.

Thus, we request the **talisman of eternal life and rescue from suffering (长生救苦之符)**,
and humbly accept the **precepts of earnest devotion (克勤之戒)**,
to proclaim within the **Yellow Talisman Altar (黄箓坛内)**,
and present before the **Most High’s Court (太上御前)**.

First, we admonish the **spirits and deities (神祇)**,
and open the **Five Pathways’ messengers (开辟五路使者)**,
like an **unstoppable boat (不击之舟)**,
coming and going without obstruction.

Like **cranes freed from their cage (出笼之鹤)**,
soaring unrestrained in the sky.
Oh, you **multitude of spirits (众灵)**,
clear the path!
All **petitions and records (文牒)** are solemnly declared.

Once declared,
present the **petitions and records (文牒)** above,
and instruct all **gentle deities (柔祇)** broadly.
If there are no records,
descend from the path below,
and ascend to report,
instructing all **gentle deities (柔祇)** broadly.

Oh, **responsible deities (神司)**,
swiftly follow the **Dao’s teachings (道训)**!

To the **local deities (界土地)**,
the **village and city spirits (里社城隍)**,
the **guardians of boundaries and protectors of realms (守疆护界)**,
and all **upright spirits (正神)**—
we command you to **clear the path (辟道路)**,
and **guide the departed (接引亡人)**.

Where there are **barriers (关者)**, swiftly open them;
where there are **ferries (津者)**, swiftly transport them.
Do not **block or hinder (勿壅勿遏)**,
do not **delay or pause (勿稽勿停)**.
To those **entangled in litigation (阴讼者)**,
do not **detain or imprison (勿得拘留)**.
To those **bound by grievances (冤对者)**,
do not **entangle or bind (勿得缠缚)**.

For those coming from the **East (东来)**,
the **Green Cavalry General (青骑将军)** shall escort them;
from the **West (西来)**,
the **Great God of the Gui Trigram (兑卦大神)** shall protect them;
from the **South (南来)**,
the **Red Bird’s (朱雀)** earthly pathways are made smooth;
from the **North (北来)**,
the **Dark Tortoise’s (玄武)** realm is opened wide.

Without **far or near (无远无近)**,
without **affinity or estrangement (无亲无疏)**,
we follow the **Green Decree’s (依女青)** command,
and review the **names and surnames of the ancestral spirits (先灵之名姓)**.

「沿路关报，逐界申闻，
along the way, announce to the officials,
and in each domain, proclaim the message.

拨发前来，斯须无滞，
dispatch them forthwith—
no delay shall hinder their passage.

即使亡过某等，
Even if they have committed grave offenses,
如晨风之趋林，
like the morning wind rushing toward the forests,
如夜蛾之赴火，
like the night moths drawn to flames,
如水之东注，
like water flowing eastward,
如马之出奔，
like horses breaking free from their bonds,
径赴道场，
they shall proceed directly to the Daoist ritual hall,
领沾功德。
to partake in the merit and virtue of the rites.

若有六天故气，
If there are lingering resentments from the Six Heavens (*liùtiān*—六天),
孽鬼妖神，
or malevolent spirits and demonic deities,
妄肆猖狂，
acting recklessly and without restraint,
敢生邀阻，
who dare to obstruct or hinder,
请戮路左，
let them be slaughtered by the wayside—
以明天诛。
to make manifest the Heavenly punishment.

道法甚严，
The Daoist laws are strict,
天威难犯，
and Heaven’s wrath is not to be provoked.
度人功大，
the merit of guiding souls is vast,
风火不停，
and the winds and flames shall not cease.
道路山川，
Let all paths and rivers
急急传命，
swiftly convey this command:
载伸偈颂，
carrying forth hymns of praise,
感格神灵。
to move and honor the divine spirits.

举不可思议功德。
All these inconceivable merits are invoked.

大圣玄元教主：
The Great Sage, the Primordial Daoist Master of Mysterious Origin:

元始有命，
At the Primordial Beginning (*yuánshǐ*—元始),
上开八门、
Heaven opened the Eight Gates (*bāmén*—八门),
死魂受炼，
and the departed souls undergo purification.

无量度人。
Endless is the power to guide souls.

天关一转，
With the turning of the Heavenly Gate,
飞天法轮。
the flying Heavenly Wheel of Law is set in motion.

咨尔东方，
Address now the deities of the East,
震上诸神。
the august spirits of the *Zhen* Trigram (*zhèn*—震).

咨尔南方，
Address now the deities of the South,
离上诸神。
the august spirits of the *Li* Trigram (*lí*—离).

咨尔西方，
Address now the deities of the West,
兑上诸神。
the august spirits of the *Dui* Trigram (*duì*—兑).

咨尔北方，
Address now the deities of the North,
坎上诸神.
the august spirits of the *Kan* Trigram (*kǎn*—坎).

东北艮方，
The northeast, the *Gen* Trigram (*gèn*—艮),
号曰鬼门。
is called the Ghostly Gate.

东南巽方，
The southeast, the *Xun* Trigram (*xùn*—巽),
地户所存。
is where the Earthly Portal resides.

西南坤方，
The southwest, the *Kun* Trigram (*kūn*—坤),
号曰人门。
is called the Human Gate.

西北乾方，
The northwest, the *Qian* Trigram (*qián*—乾),
天门所经。
is where the Heavenly Gate passes through.

地界主者，
The earthly domain’s sovereigns,
八方之灵。
the spirits of the eight directions—

请辟道路，
I pray that they clear the paths,
接引亡人。
and guide the departed souls.

使诣灵坛，
Let them proceed to the Sacred Altars (*língtán*—灵坛),
听法闻经。
to hear the Dao and recite the scriptures.

领沾功德，
Partaking in the merit and virtue,
保命生根。
and securing their life’s foundation.

敢有拒逆，
Whoever dares to resist,
逼合鬼群。
shall be forced into the ranks of the malevolent spirits.

翦形截首，
Their forms shall be severed,
their heads cut off—
风火无停.
the winds and flames shall not relent.

今法众等，
Now, all who gather in this ritual,
合道场人，
united with those in the Daoist hall,
稽首皈依，
bowing in reverence and taking refuge,
至心奉请东方青帝、
with utmost sincerity invoking:
the Green Sovereign of the East (*qīngdì*—青帝),
南方赤帝、
the Red Sovereign of the South (*chìdì*—赤帝),
西方白帝、
the White Sovereign of the West (*báidì*—白帝),
北方黑帝、
the Black Sovereign of the North (*hēidì*—黑帝),
中央黄帝、
and the Yellow Sovereign of the Center (*huángdì*—黄帝),
开路将军，
as well as the Generals who Open the Paths (*kāilù jiāngjūn*—开路将军),
鉴察弟子丹诚，
may they witness the disciples’ earnest devotion,
开辟五方道路。
and clear the five directional paths.

偈日：
The hymn declares:

上来仪范戒柔祇，
The ritual precedents and prohibitions of the *Rouqi* (柔祇)
are now invoked from above.
想尔八方尽遍知，
Know that all eight directions are fully aware.

应有关津蒙济度，
Whoever encounters barriers or crossings
shall be granted swift passage.
更无道路敢稽迟，
No path shall dare to delay or obstruct them.

亡魂已出寒庭狱，
The departed souls have left the Cold Prison of the *Hanting* (寒庭).
丹霍行升火炼池，
They proceed through the Vermilion and Azure paths,
ascending to the Fire-Purification Pool (*huǒliànchí*—火炼池).
空洞谣歌齐赞咏，
Let all empty and resonant hymns unite in praise,
敢凭道力拯灵仪。
and let them rely on the Dao’s power to rescue the sacred souls.

黄箓大斋第一度：
The First Degree of the Grand Fast of the Yellow Offerings (*huánglù dàzhāi*—黄箓大斋):

召请祀典神祇，
I summon and invite the deities of the ritual traditions,
泬寥戒夜，
on nights of solemn purity (*pǒngliáo jièyè*—泬寥戒夜),
沆瀣澄空，
when the *Hángxiè* (沆瀣) clears the heavens,
伫神听之格思，
awaiting the divine response with reverent contemplation,
控忱诚而惕若。
holding my sincere devotion in check with utmost vigilance.

入意以今恭率法众，
With this solemn intent,
I lead the assembled ritualists (*fǎzhòng*—法众)
in the First Degree’s invocation—

召请古先帝王、
I summon the ancient sovereigns of old:
the *Moral Dao* (*dàodé*—道德) and the august saints,
忠贞勋烈、
the loyal and virtuous ministers of merit and valor,
历朝文武重臣，
and the civil and martial officials of past dynasties,
凡该祀典诸庙福德灵享，
all deities enshrined in temples of ritual tradition,
伏愿暂迂飙驭，
I humbly pray that they temporarily abandon their swift celestial chariots (*biàoyù*—飙驭),
降赴道场，
and descend to this Daoist hall,
领录斋功，
to receive the merit of this fast,
证明修奉。
and witness its observance.

伏以大道弘化，
I humbly submit that the Great Dao/Way (*dàdào*—大道)
has spread its vast teachings,
真一播灵，
and the *True Unity* (*zhēnyī*—真一) has disseminated its sacred influence.
三清为众圣之先，
The Three Pure Ones (*sānqīng*—三清) are the foremost of all saints,
弥罗冠万天之首。
and *Mile* (*mílúo*—弥罗) is the crown of all heavens.

旁分九气，
They govern the nine breaths of *Qi* (*jiǔqì*—九气),
复品四人，
and embody the four cardinal virtues.
踰劫历之先，
Before the eons of the past,
出阴阳之表，
they transcended the realms of *Yin* and *Yang* (*yīnyáng*—阴阳).
三界为超凡之始，
The Three Realms (*sānjiè*—三界) mark the beginning of their transcendence,
八梵为元阳之初。
and the Eight *Brahmins* (*bāfàn*—八梵) are the origin of the Primordial Yang.

上辟清圆，
Above, they clear the Pure and Rounded,
下凝方浊。
below, they condense the Square and Turbid.
玄黄交感，
The Mysterious Yellow (*Xuánhuáng*—玄黄) intermingles in resonance,
太素流形。
and the Great Primordial Essence (*tàisù*—太素) manifests its forms.

对越在天，
They face each other in the heavens,
准尊元首。
and align with the august Primordial Sovereigns.

於是冬居营室，
Thus, in winter they dwell in *Yingshi* (营室),
夏处层巢，
and in summer they reside in *Cencháo* (层巢).
饮血茹毛，
They consume blood and raw flesh,
结绳识事。
and use knotted cords to record matters.

迨及燧人钻火，
When the time came for *Suirén* (燧人) to drill fire,
伏牺画爻，
and *Fuxi* (伏牺) to inscribe the *Yao* (爻),
炎帝肇基，
*Yandi* (炎帝) established the foundations,
有熊御世，
and *Youxiong* (有熊) ruled the age.
帝誉顺天而行义，
The Sovereign *Yuyu* (帝誉) followed Heaven’s will
and practiced righteous governance,
高阳任地以依神，
*Sovereign Gaoyang* (高阳) entrusted himself to the Earth
and relied upon the divine.
夏后祖于唐虞，
The *Xia* sovereigns (*Xiàhòu*—夏后) succeeded the *Tang* and *Yu* (唐虞) eras,
殷命法乎三圣，
and the *Shang* dynasty (*Yīn*—殷) took its mandate
from the Three Saints (*sāshèng*—三圣).
文武为继代之主，
The *Wen* and *Wu* (文武) sovereigns were the successors of their age,
汉唐宗拨乱之君，
and the *Han* and *Tang* (汉唐) emperors were the ancestral lords
who calmed the chaos.
莫不龙虎勃兴，
None failed to rise like dragons and tigers,
风云际会。
or gather the winds and clouds in auspicious confluence.

又况世分治乱，
Moreover, in an age divided between governance and chaos,
臣有忠良，
there were loyal and virtuous ministers,
莫非理国以辑民，
who did not fail to govern the realm
and bring order to the people.
皆务积功而累行，
All strove to accumulate merit
and refine their conduct.

故在天为星象，
Thus, in the heavens they became stars and constellations,
在地为神明，
and on Earth they became divine luminaries.
德被群生，
Their virtue extends to all living beings,
泽流万世，
and their blessings flow through countless ages.
膺上帝之休命，
They received the Heavenly Mandate of auspicious fate,
授列职之仙班。
and were appointed to the ranks of the celestial immortals.

故《混元图翼》所载云：
Thus, the *Hunyuan Tu* (混元图) records:

伏牺为太一真君，
*Fuxi* (伏牺) is the True Sovereign of the *Taiyi* (太一),
神农为南极真君，
*Shennong* (神农) is the True Sovereign of the Southern Pole,
轩辕为中黄太帝，
*Xuanyuan* (轩辕) is the Great Sovereign of the Central Yellow,
少昊为太虚真君，
*Shaohao* (少昊) is the True Sovereign of the *Tai xu* (太虚),
帝誉为太玄真君，
*Sovereign Yuyu* (帝誉) is the True Sovereign of the *Tai xuan* (太玄),
颛顼为北宫真君，
*Zhuanyu* (颛顼) is the True Sovereign of the Northern Palace,
帝尧为太微真君，
*Emperor Yao* (帝尧) is the True Sovereign of the *Taiwei* (太微),
帝舜为太极真君，
*Emperor Shun* (帝舜) is the True Sovereign of the *Taiji* (太极),
夏禹为紫庭真君，
*Yu the Great* (夏禹) is the True Sovereign of the Purple Enclosure,
殷汤为北玄真君，
*Tang of Shang* (殷汤) is the True Sovereign of the Northern Mysterious,
武丁为紫微真君，
*Emperor Wuding* (武丁) is the True Sovereign of the Purple Forbidden,
阳甲为苍元真君，
*Yangjia* (阳甲) is the True Sovereign of the Azure Primordial,
文王为太虚真君，
*King Wen of Zhou* (文王) is the True Sovereign of the *Tai xu* (太虚),
武王为太平真君，
*King Wu of Zhou* (武王) is the True Sovereign of the *Tai ping* (太平),
康王为太华真君，
*King Kang of Zhou* (康王) is the True Sovereign of the *Tai hua* (太华),
穆王为九元真君，
*King Mu of Zhou* (穆王) is the True Sovereign of the Nine Primordials,
汉高皇为北帝宾友，
*Emperor Gaozu of Han* (汉高皇) is the guest of the Northern Sovereign,
文帝为通玄真君，
*Emperor Wen of Han* (文帝) is the True Sovereign of the *Tongxuan* (通玄),
景帝为太一真君，
*Emperor Jing of Han* (景帝) is the True Sovereign of the *Taiyi* (太一),
宣帝为紫华仙伯，
*Emperor Xuan of Han* (宣帝) is the Celestial Lord of the Purple Splendor,
武帝为玄成真人。
*Emperor Wu of Han* (武帝) is the True Person of Mysterious Perfection.

凡诸神圣睿哲之君，
All these divine, sagely, and enlightened sovereigns
皆证清高崇峻之位，
have attained the lofty and pure ranks,
曳裾八极，
their robes trailing through the eight cardinal directions,
腾景九天。
and their radiance ascending to the Nine Heavens.

经若不传，
Had the scriptures not been transmitted,
世莫能显。
the world would not have known their glory.

复有忠臣贤佐、良辅元勋，
There are also loyal ministers, virtuous counselors,
and meritorious aides and great officials of merit—
位列仙阶，
their ranks listed among the celestial immortals,
名垂信史，
their names recorded in trustworthy histories.
或享世间庙食之盛，
Some enjoy the grand offerings of mortal temples,
或主岳渎鬼神之权。
others hold authority over the mountain altars and waterways of spirits.

故风后为太华真人，
Thus, *Feng Hu* (风后) is the True Person of the *Tai hua* (太华),
力牧为玄山真人，
*Li Mu* (力牧) is the True Person of the Mysterious Mountains,
太山稽为洞庭真人，
*Tai Shan Ji* (太山稽) is the True Person of the *Dongting* (洞庭),
苍颉为九华真人，
*Cangjie* (苍颉) is the True Person of the Nine Splendors,
容成为应化真人，
*Rong Zhen* (容成) is the True Person of Adaptive Transformation,
大挠为玄光真人，
*Dayao* (大挠) is the True Person of Mysterious Radiance,
奚仲为太成真人，
*Xizhong* (奚仲) is the True Person of Great Perfection,
传说为左言上相，
*Zhuanshuo* (传说) is the Supreme Counselor of the Left Utterance,
叔齐为金阙仆射，
*Shuqi* (叔齐) is the Vice-Director of the Golden Portal,
伯夷为太微侍郎，
*Boyi* (伯夷) is the Attendant Officer of the *Taiwei* (太微),
周公为紫微都护

---

...and those who govern the authority over the mountain altars and waterways of spirits.

Thus, *Zhao Gong* (召公) and *Ji Zi* (季子) are both the Lords of *Southern Brightness* (南明) and *Northern Brightness* (北明);
*Qi Heng* (齐恒) and *Jin Wen* (晋文) hold the office of *Director of the Celestial Command* (司命都禁).

*Yuan Gui* (元规) and *You Yu* (幼舆) serve as *Left Celestial Guards* (左司禁);
*Yuan Zhi* (元直) and *Shen Yuan* (深源) are the *Morning Attendants of the Sovereign* (侍帝晨).

*Tao Shiheng* (陶士衡) is the *Marquis of the Western River* (河西侯),
*Wen Tai Zhen* (温太真) is the *Duke of the Supervised Sea* (监海伯).

All these virtuous sages have their appointed duties,
Their advancement is reckoned by years of service,
Their promotion is determined by merit and diligence.

Thus, the *Northern Sovereign* (北帝) changes every three thousand years,
The mountain altars and waterways are relocated every six hundred years.
*Wu Jie* (武解) is the *Ghost King beneath the Earth* (地下鬼王),
*Wen Jie* (文解) is the *Master beneath the Earth* (地下主者).

Those of utmost loyalty and filial piety,
Of utmost chastity and integrity,
Initially serve as *Ghost Officials* (鬼官),
Then ascend to the *Caverns of the Dao* (洞府).

Most are promoted every one hundred and forty years,
Entering the feast at *Eastern Hua* (东华);
Their ranks advance through *twenty-seven grades* (二十七品),
Only then escaping the *Great Calamity* (大劫).

The *Heavenly Court’s* (上天) promotions and demotions are profound and mysterious,
Not discernible by the limited senses of the mortal realm.

Only through accumulated merit and virtue do they gradually attain *Daoist immortality* (仙位).
How much more so in this land of *Sichuan’s* (兹庸蜀) *abundant Daoist networks* (井络之地),
Which truly rests upon the auspicious foundation of *Zeng Chang* (曾昌)!

The *divine horses of gold and green birds* (金马碧鸡) are revered by imperial decree,
The *copper gates and jade ramparts* (铜关玉垒) of their temples protect the *Earthly Foundation* (坤维).

The *group of celestial lords* (群望) governs in appointed roles,
While the *mild and virtuous* (柔示) are stationed in their places.

From *Sichuan* (蜀郡), this system is extended by analogy,
Covering all lands—each has its *Daoist framework* (纲维).

Mountains and rivers, the nine regions,
Jade and silk offerings from myriad lands,
All are governed by spirits.

The *hidden and distant temples* (幽隐庙貌) are everywhere,
From near to far—those who benefit the people
Are honored by all spirits.

Now, there is a family dedicated to the Dao,
Who follows the *Nine Altars’* (九坛) traditions and rituals,
Who observes the *Three Arrow* (三箓) rites of the Dao,
Ascending to the *Idyllic Heaven* (郁罗之天),
Encompassing the *Heavenly and Earthly Realms* (乾坤之界),
Descending to the *Abyssal Daoist Caverns* (洞渊之府),
And reaching into the *Remote Northern Lands* (朔都之乡).

With a single thought, they resonate with the *True and Authentic* (真灵),
And all spirits gather in response.

To the *Heavenly, Earthly, Watery, and Land-based* (天地水陆),
They pray and make offerings in all directions;
The spirits of mountains and rivers, of all lands,
Assemble in the *boundless* (无方).

I humbly pray that the *One True Spirit* (大恢得一之灵)
May come from the *boundless* (无方),
To fulfill the command of *summoning the True Person with the Jade Tablet* (碧简招真),
And to join the ranks of *those who attend the Golden Portal* (金阙朝真),
To exalt the *Heavenly Auspices* (天休),
And to safeguard the *imperial lineage* (国祚).

May they *seal the powers of life and death* (封掌生死),
And open the *path of ease and convenience* (方便之门);
May they *grasp the balance of yin and yang* (把握阴阳),
And ascend to the *Age of the Sovereign’s Supreme Dao* (皇极之世).

I humbly pray that they may *temporarily dwell in the celestial chariot* (暂驻风云之驭),
And *descend to partake in the offerings of the Daoist community* (俯歆苹藻之羞),
To *bestow blessings upon the solemn rites* (阴佑斋功),
And to *fulfill the harmonious aspirations* (克谐愿望).
May they *extend their praise again* (再伸偈颂),
And *touch the hearts of the mighty and numinous* (感格威灵).

The *emperors and kings* (帝王) study ancient traditions and emulate the *Heavenly Craft* (代天工),
Different teachings converge in the *Great Central Dao* (建大中).

The *sovereign’s loyal ministers* (元首股肱) serve with unwavering devotion,
And the *spirits and Daoist saints* (鬼神贤圣) are revered in equal measure.

In mortal rites, they honor the *ancestors and sages* (祀典思遗列),
While in the celestial ranks, they *respond to the swift and mighty* (仙班答骏功).
With incense and fire offerings, they strictly adhere to the *broad Daoist precepts* (溥告),
And pray to *align the celestial chariot with their sincere intentions* (愿驱云驭格精衷).

**Second Degree: Inviting the Departed Souls**
The *wandering soul* (游魂) is restless, and the *Great Night* (大夜) never brightens.
They must *lean upon the Nine-Colored Golden Light* (必倾九色之金光),
And *use the Iron Locks of Darkness* (用掣重阴之铁锁).

The *Great Dao is without obstruction* (大方无碍),
And the *myriad laws are illuminated* (万法昭融).
The *Celestially Revered* (举天尊) proclaims:

There is a *formless substance* (有物混成),
From which the *Sovereign* (皇) gives birth to *Heaven and Earth* (生天地).
The *round and clear* (圆清) and the *square and turbid* (方浊)
Within it give rise to humanity.
This is called the *Three Talents* (三才),
Each possessing its *Daoist nature* (道性).

*Heaven endures, Earth lasts* (天长地久),
Without beginning or end,
They *propel the flow of yin and yang* (推荡阴阳),
And *divide the cycles of darkness and light* (裁割昏晓).
The *uninterrupted breath of qi* (一气不息)
Gives birth to all forms (万形以生),
Distinctly manifesting as *divinity* (卓然有神),
Known as the *Creative Transformation* (造化).

Humans dwell within it,
Above, aligned with the *Two Principles* (两仪) of Heaven and Earth,
Though noble and humble differ,
The *virtuous and the foolish* (贤愚) are distinguished.

What they receive from this source,
Is the *same initial essence* (一初).
They *embrace yin and hold yang* (负阴抱阳),
With *round heads and square feet* (圆首方趾).

From infancy, they *preserve their pure spirit* (精守神全),
Their *Heavenly Truth* (天真) untainted,
Their *mixed and primordial state* (混沌) unbroken,
They do not covet wealth and nobility,
Nor do they scorn poverty and lowliness,
Though they possess *sentience and knowledge* (含识知),
Their essence remains *pure and untainted* (纯粹精白).
This is the *True and Authentic Nature* (真实性),
Without *deceit or falsehood* (无邪伪心),
And to be born as a human is what is most precious.

As they grow older,
Their bodies interact with the world,
Gradually losing their *Heavenly Truth* (天真),
And being *corrupted by human desires* (熏煎人欲).
The *innocence of childhood* (赤子之性) diminishes day by day, month by month,
Endless beings arise,
Endless streams of existence flow,
Yet they only *pursue worldly attachments* (务逐物),
And do not *know the love of origin* (爱缘).

How few recognize that this body,
Above, is aligned with *Heaven and Earth* (配天地),
That it *originates from the womb* (始从胎育),
And *descends from the Nine Heavens* (降气九天).
When the *ten months are complete* (十月既圆),
All *ten thousand spirits* (万神) guard it.
Once the form is born,
The *seven orifices* (七窍) open,
The *nine palaces* (九宫) are arranged upon the head,
Where the *Nine True Spirits* (九真) reside,
The *five viscera* (五藏) are divided within,
Each with its own *spirit* (神).

The *Three Souls* (三魂) dwell in the liver,
Desiring that humans act virtuously.
The *Seven Spirits* (七魄) reside in the lungs,
Desiring that humans act wickedly.
The *Twenty-Four True Spirits* (二十四真),
Are divided among the *three departments* (三部):
The *Purple Gates and Jade Pavilions* (紫户玉阁),
The *Crimson Palaces and Vermilion Fields* (绛宫丹田),
And within, the *True Person* (真人),
Known as the *Innocent Child* (赤子),
Where *ten thousand Heavenly Spirits* (天地神气) and *thirty-six thousand* (三万六千)
Converge—every *joint and subtle mechanism* (关节机微)
Is under their control.

How noble is the human body!
Most noble is the *One True Spirit* (一真),
The *original essence* (初生),
Pure and untainted,
And humans, in their worldly existence,
Each know how to *preserve their own* (自存).

The *divine spirits within the body* (周身中神) rejoice and surge.
The *stars upon the crown* (顶戴之星)
Shine brightly and radiate.

The **refined essence** (精炼),
Can attain the **Daoist Sage** (神仙).

The **true and genuine compassion and benevolence** (真正慈仁),
Also allow one to **long endure** (久视).

If one **contrary to this** (反此),
No **evil fate** (恶缘) will fail to befall them.

The **Heavenly Spirits and vital qi** (神气) daily **degenerate** (日衮),
The **stellar lights** (星光) grow dim each day.
The **original nature of the One True Spirit** (一真之性),
Even unto death remains **unrecognized** (不知).

They **betray the Great Dao** (上辜大道),
The **fate of transformation** (混成之缘),
And **fail the dual principles** (下负两仪),
The **path of equilibrium** (受中之道).

In **endless darkness** (冥冥),
They journey ever onward,
And **consort with ghosts** (与鬼为徒).
The **ten thousand spirits** (万神) mourn in sorrow,
Each **abandoning their mortal form** (各去其体).

Some **sink into eternal night** (沦幽夜),
Others **fall under the jurisdiction of ghosts** (属鬼官).
To **seek rebirth beyond** (超生),
Is **utterly without hope** (渺无涯涘).

Only **my Supreme Lord** (太上),
Through **countless kalpas** (历劫) **proclaims compassion** (宣慈),
In the **stream of life and death** (生死流),
**Clears the path** (辟津梁路).

The **divine banner** (神旛) **opens the Dao** (启道),
The **Golden Edict** (黄诏) **summons the spirits** (招魂),
The **fragrant waters** (香水) **purify defilements** (荡瑕),
The **Law Bridge** (法桥) **rescues the drowning** (拯溺),
The **sacred talisman** (灵符) **revives the dead** (起死),
The **wondrous precepts** (妙戒) **return one to the True** (归真),
The **cloud-inscribed charms** (云篆) **translocate the spirits** (迁神),
The **Law Lamp** (法灯) **dispels darkness** (破暗),
**Illuminating the Dao’s mysteries** (昭垂道妙),
And **restoring the True Nature** (还复性真).

Thus, **all beings** (诸众生),
From **post-mortem annihilation** (死灭后),
In the **various realms of suffering** (苦趣),
May **arouse the mind of repentance** (发回向心),
And **acknowledge the Heavenly True Self** (认处天真),
**Repenting evil deeds** (忏悔恶业),
**Riding the Six Powers** (乘六通惠),
To **escape the myriad ghosts** (出万鬼群),
And **behold the Heavenly Sovereign** (得睹天尊),
**Proclaiming the Supreme Dao** (说无上道),
**Refining the form in the Fire Palace** (炼形火府),
And **crossing to the Southern Celestial Realm** (度品南宫).

Each **follows their own inherent nature** (随本人),
With **roots and capacities deep or shallow** (根品深浅),
If **sudden enlightenment** (顿悟) is achieved,
They **transcend the human and celestial realms** (超人天).
Through **gradual cultivation** (渐进修),
They **reclaim their original nature** (复生正性).

As **previously expounded** (上所说),
**Fully recorded in the True Scriptures** (具载真经).

**Perilous is the single mind** (危哉一心),
Bound in the **wheel of life and death** (生死轮转).
Yet **my Supreme Lord** (太上),
**Vows unceasingly** (弘誓不忘),
That **all beings may awaken to the Dao** (皆得悟道).

Now, **a certain family** (某家),
Through **incense and refined offerings** (熏修妙供),
**Awakens the living** (启迪生方),
And **respectfully invokes the distant** (谨即长途),
To **extend their summoning** (以伸告召).

May the **departed** (亡者)
**Each recognize their Heavenly True Self** (各识天真),
With **their original spiritual essence** (以本性灵),
**Uniting all their vital spirits and qi** (合诸魂气).

**Loudly calling forth** (大声疾呼),
Their **names and lineages unconfused** (名姓不迷).
**Widely opening the paths of salvation** (广进康衢),
No **mountains or rivers shall obstruct** (山川不隔).
A **single thought spans a thousand miles** (一念千里),
With **a finger-snap across three lifetimes** (弹指三生).
**Arriving at the Dao’s threshold** (即到道前),
**No hindrance remains** (了无壅滞).

Again, **raising the Daoist hymn** (再伸仙偈),
To **invoke and guide the departed spirits** (招引亡魂).

---
*The Dao penetrates Heaven and Earth, unique among humanity’s paths*,
*A single gathering of Heavenly True Self yields a body of ten thousand treasures*.
*Chasing after worldly things brings one to sink in the sea of life and death*,
*Observing the body—who then becomes a Sage or Holy One?*
*The essence of gold, even refined a hundred times, still retains its nature*,
*Flame repeatedly kindled returns to its original True Self*.
**Hoisting the divine banner dispels all obstructions**,
**Summoning all spirits to emerge from the misty crossing**.

---
**Third Degree: The Night of Deep Obscurity** (沉阴戒夜),
Even **ghostly officials may be called forth** (鬼正可呼).
**Spirits lost in confusion** (滞爽迷方),
The **Dao always brings salvation** (道常善救).

**Invitation to the Mind:**
**Raise the Holy Name** (举圣号).

**The Origin of the Supreme Polarity**,
the Two Principles are thus divided.
The light and clear become Heaven, the Three Celestial Luminaries arrayed in order,
the heavy and turbid become Earth, myriad beings springing forth in clusters.
Between the Six Extremes, there is inner and outer,
in the movement of **One Qi** (One Breath), there is upright and perverse.
Within, there is harmony and balance—**virtue/power** (德) is the nature of humanity.
The accumulation of **One Qi** (One Breath) in moderation gives rise to Sages and Holy Ones.
Dwelling in the common crowd, they merge as ordinary folk.
Gathering in rebellion and inversion, they become ghosts and demons.
The remainder, mixed and confused, descend to beasts.
The world is thus created, and all beings are distinguished by their kind.

In the age of **grass and dimness** (primordial chaos), when life was unstable,
the ancient Sages arose and established these teachings.
Nobility and humility, honor and lowliness,
the refined and the uncivilized, human and beast—
each found its proper place,
so none would be overturned and inverted.

Where the **Kunlun Mountains** stand,
below lies **China** (the Central Realm),
and the Sages transmitted the **Dao/Way**,
steadfastly upholding its center.
With **virtue/power** (德) and righteousness established,
loyalty and filial piety emerging together,
through sincerity and reverence,
through propriety and law,
they ordained many ways to prevent even a single stray thought.

A thought aligned with uprightness,
not crossing into the improper—
this is to be Heaven, to be humanity,
to be divine, to be a Sage.

But if one turns to rebellion and inversion,
to ferocity and cruelty, to violence and retribution,
willing to join the demonic ranks and battle the heavens—
within the **Dao/Way of humanity** (人道),
to violate the fundamental principles,
is to lose one’s human form and fall into the earthly hells,
where iron cities encircle flames,
and copper pillars are slick with blood.
Endless debts of karmic recompense,
endless cycles of vengeance and suffering,
where specters question their shadows,
and skulls lament their solitude.
In the boundless void, without reliance,
they sigh and groan in endless despair.

**Greed, anger, and delusion** (三毒) fuel the karmic fire,
with no way to escape its burning.
Hungry ghosts wander beside,
receiving punishment for their deeds.
All realms rise and fall—
all originate from humanity.

**Beware, the heart’s smallest inch—**
its strength rivals creation.
A single awakening suffices to dispel all accumulation,
and the **Primordial Dao/Way** (先天) will not be obstructed.
A single delusion, once lost, cannot be retrieved—
even all the Buddhas cannot save.

Within the heart’s measure,
the Six Realms cycle endlessly.
Through the Three Realms,
one traverses countless kalpas.

The **karmic fire** blazes fiercely,
consuming the **Great Thousand Worlds** (大千).
Like fleeting water, it vanishes into the boundless,
and one drifts through the Eight Extremes.

At this juncture,
in frantic flight and haste,
they cry out in sorrow—
who then can rescue them?

Only our **Great Compassionate and Merciful Father, the Primordial Sovereign of Heaven** (元始天尊),
emits boundless radiance,
illuminating all without exclusion.
In the **sea of karmic forces** (业力海),
He steers the **compassionate vessel** (慈航).
In the **city of tormenting flames** (虐焰城),
He pours the **lawful rain** (法雨).
With **jade-like mercy** (玉颜恻隐),
His **golden hands** (金手) lift and guide.

Through His **Great Spiritual Penetration** (大神通),
He awakens their true nature.
In the blink of an eye,
they escape the wheel of suffering.
In the span of a closed breath,
each recognizes their past destinies.

While living beings remain undelivered,
His compassionate vow endures.
For all future beings,
He grants universal liberation.

Now, this humble household,
relying on His sacred oath,
proclaims the **auspicious cause** (良因),
for kin and kindred alike,
all may be elevated and saved.

From the **realm of desire** (色欲界) to the **abyssal depths** (洞渊泉),
from **China’s domain** (中华区) to lands without measure,
for **heavenly beings, humans, ghosts, and those in hell** (天人鬼狱),
of varied realms and ranks—
we turn the **Great Vehicle’s chariot** (大乘辕),
and all ascend together.

We humbly vow:
May each, through the **law’s power** (法力),
arrive at the **Dao/Way’s threshold** (道前),
and behold the **Heavenly Sovereign** (天尊),
receiving equal deliverance.

A single resonant void,
cleansing the sincerity of those entangled in filth;
all sentient beings,
entering the **suspended pearl’s aperture** (悬珠之窍).

Again, we recite the **verses of the Dao** (偈颂),
to gather wandering souls.

From the **uppermost darkness** (昙誓) to the **abyssal depths** (渊泉),
the Six Extremes are traversed, the **Great Thousand Worlds** (大千) all reached.
The enlightened dwell beyond form and vessel,
while the deluded cannot escape the bonds of life and death.
The **karmic wheel** ceases to turn with grasping,
who then knows the **transformation of the Dao’s essence** (体悟迁)?

The **void’s treasure-pearl aperture** (空际宝珠通窍道),
the **darkened heart** (冥心) pleads to the **Primordial Sovereign** (元始) for mercy.

Baptized in the **rites of deliverance** (度魂仪),
we humbly confess:
In the **yellow underworld’s abyss** (黄泉溟漠),
the **turbulent and impure qi** (凝浊滞染) clings to the spirit;
in the **black soil’s obscurity** (黑壤幽阴),
the **accumulated filth** (积秽) sinks deep into the **vital essence** (灵爽).
Through the endless night of darkness,
ascension is difficult to achieve.

Thus, the **Supreme Most High** (太上) in compassion,
the **Primordial Emperor** (元皇) in sorrow,
descends with the **law of cleansing toil** (洗涤尘劳之法),
and proclaims the **rites of baptism and purification** (沐浴炼度之仪).
Even if the **karmic net** is severed,
and the **roots of sin** (罪根) are absolved—
today, we solemnly prepare the **treasure-chamber** (宝室),
and purify the **fragrant bath** (兰汤).
We establish the **five-scented ablution rites** (五香澡盥之仪),
and follow the **three registers of exorcism** (三箓拯拔之格).

We invite the **departed souls** (亡过某等),
to attend the chamber and be cleansed,
to dispel the turbid and flow the pure,
and after the rites, to return to their place and listen to the **law**.

We humbly confess:
The **paths of the underworld** (泉路) are deep and dark,
the **cold halls** (寒庭) accumulate filth,
so the **spirit** (神魂) grows obscured,
and the **vital essence** (灵爽) is clouded by ignorance.
Without the **merit of recommendation** (资荐之功),
ascension is impossible to hope for.

We, the assembly of the **law**, (请法众等),
offer this for the **departed souls** (亡灵),
to aid their passage into the **immortal realm** (往生仙界).

We recite the **Bath of Purification Incantation** (沐浴荡秽咒):
*The skies are clear, the qi refined, five colors radiant and bright.*
*The sun and moon emit their splendor,*
*to wash and purify the body’s form.*
*The divine ford is dissolved,*
*fragrant waters flow with clarity.*
*The light shines forth in brilliance,*
*illuminating the Uppermost Purity.*
*The qi does not receive impurity,*
*the Five Palaces accept the essence.*
*Guilt vanishes from the Three Abysses,*
*calamity fades from the Nine Underworlds.*
*The roots of evil are severed,*
*blessings naturally arise.*
*Today’s great vow,*
*all is now declared.*
*The body receives liberation,*
*ascending to the Imperial Court.*

We humbly confess:
For the **spirit to fly into the Dao’s realm** (神飞仙境),
it must rely on the **merit of purification** (炼度之功);
for the **vital essence to depart from obscurity** (魄离幽阴),
it may attain the **fruit of ascension** (升真之果).
To sever earthly filth,
and swiftly gain passage—
to gather harmonious **qi** (气) in the **body-field** (身田),
and to resolve past grievances in the **karmic net** (业网).

We, the assembly of the **law**, (请法众等),
offer this for the **departed souls** (亡灵),
to aid their passage into the **immortal realm** (往生仙界).

We recite the **Bath of Purification Incantation for the Dao’s True Nature** (沐浴炼真咒):
*The Supreme Most High and True, the essence of the Nine Spirits.*
*May the spirit fly into the Dao,*
*and ascend to the Purple Court.*
*Baptized in the Pool of Splendor,*
*the body and spirit become clear.*
*The essence penetrates the Great Emptiness,*
*and ten thousand breaths arise anew.*

We humbly confess:
The **yellow register** (黄箓) descends with its teachings,
the **Purple Court** (紫清) establishes its doctrine,
to save the living and deliver the dead—
all enter the **law’s gate** (法门).
*We open the divine court of flowing fire,*
*to purify and remove obscurity;*
*We stir the lawful waters of radiant clarity,*
*to wash away the toil of the earthly.*
*One may ascend to the land of purity,*
*and behold the Sages of the Void.*

We, the assembly of the **law**, (请法众等),
offer this for the **departed souls** (亡灵),
to aid their passage into the **immortal realm** (往生仙界).

We recite the **Dan Yang Incantation for the Purification of Departed Souls** (丹阳炼度亡魂咒):

The Dragon Han flows boundless, formless, nameless.
Through countless eons, the Imperial Dao shines bright.
Divine clarity radiates—nine souls exhale their essence.
Jade Emptiness glows pure, the Great Vermilion ascends sublime.

The Primordial Origin opens cultivation;
All celestial hosts gather in attendance.
The Three Primordials nourish the Way,
The Two Symbols govern life’s transformation.
The unenlightened are enlightened,
The unformed are perfected.
The dead are transformed, the withered bloom anew.
All sentient souls—stirring, breathing—
Conceived in wombs, all receive rebirth.
This auspicious day, all attain radiance.
The Five Emperors gaze upon them,
Proclaiming to ten thousand souls.

Heaven and Earth’s deities,
And the rivers’ sources,
The Five Peaks and Four Seas,
And all named mountains,
The Cavernous Primordial, Cavernous Void,
Cavernous Emptiness, Cavernous Immortal,
The Boundless Great Sage, the Most True and Noble Deity,
The Boundless and Limitless—all compassionately oversee and deliver life.

When the earthly roots are severed,
The Primordial Register records their names.
All the True Ones respond,
All obey.

For the stagnant souls trapped in the springs,
By the law’s power, they ascend;
The suffering souls in the bitter sea,
Hear the immortal’s voice and attain liberation.
Swiftly depart the turbid waves,
Directly ascend the Pure Capital,
Transformed among mortals,
Forever dwelling in blessings and longevity.

We, the assembly of the law,
Offer this for the departed souls,
To aid their passage into the immortal realm.

We recite the **Bathing at the Eastern Well Incantation**:
The Heavenly River washes the Eastern Well,
Where the Stone Mirror’s water spirit resides.
Round light sweeps the luminous soul,
Dark radiance gleams high and clear.
The Primordial Origin sustains the heavy night,
Heavenly beings follow the moon’s birth.
Bathing in the Orchid Pool above,
A dragon bears the Long Star’s vessel.
The Golden Boy scatters fragrant waters,
The Jade Maiden flows the Five Stars.
Crowns and sashes are cleansed in jade dew,
Five immortals are refined in form.
Fragrance descends upon all gods,
Ascending the luminous heights on their shadows.

For the compassionate heart saves beings,
The scriptures deliver people,
Opening the path for all to return.
First, they are cleansed in purity,
Then their souls attain boundless freedom.

We, the assembly of the law,
Offer this for the departed souls,
To aid their passage into the immortal realm.

We recite the **Pure Water Soul-Delivery Incantation**:
Majestic is the Dao’s noble virtue,
Its merits already complete.
Descending to guide and lead,
The teacher and protector come together.
The compassionate, wondrous law-water
Washes away folly and delusion.
Forever crossing to the Three Pure’s shores,
Long farewell to the Five Turbidities’ mire.

For stirring the turbid and uplifting the pure,
Their ranks are already perfected;
Ascending the True and escaping calamity,
Their aid extends to both the living and the dead.
Now the bathing is complete,
Foulness has been dispelled,
The spirit and mind are pure,
Suffering and torment are removed.

We respectfully invite the departed,
Now adorned in new crowns and sashes,
To come before the Dao and pay homage to the compassionate sage,
To receive the seals and precepts.

We, the assembly of the law,
Offer this for the departed souls,
To aid their passage into the immortal realm.

We recite the **Incantation for Donning Robes and Sashes**:
The Five Turbidities are cleansed,
The Eight Sceneries are bright.
Today they undergo refinement,
Guilt is destroyed, blessings arise.
Forever equal to the Five Emperors,
They join the ranks of the Highest Spirits.
Form and spirit are both wondrous,
Ascending to be reborn in the Southern Court.

Now the bathing is complete,
Their purity is perfected,
Their rainbow robes flutter fragrant,
Their cloud-steps depart the chamber.
Respectfully facing the Three Pure’s throne,
They proclaim the Nine Keys’ true teachings,
Receive the seals and precepts,
Transcend the mundane to attain sainthood,
And surely achieve the wondrous fruit,
Swiftly realizing the immortal realm.

The spirit and soul abide,
Bowing to the summons.

**The Sweet Dew Law-Food Rite is invoked.**
The master sits and recites the **Primordial Lord’s Invocation for Invitation**:
The Primordial Lord issues the teachings,
Highest among all the Ways.
Through countless eons, He delivers beings,
Propagating the Heavy Darkness’ meaning.
To broaden the ferry’s path,
One must first perform the invocation ritual.
Hoping to observe the Great Construction’s wisdom,
To serve as the dependent refuge for the departed souls.
Where heavenly light illuminates,
The sweet dew is imbued with spirit.
Each must firmly grasp the sincere sincerity,
Ascending to the Void’s saints.

We recite the **Jade Purity’s Wise Command Invocation**:
With bowed head, we honor the Dark-Wisdom Void-Worthy,
With bowed head, we return to the Heavy Darkness Master.
The Heavenly Earth’s virtue is beyond measure,
All beings rely on You as their refuge.
With compassion, You turn the Five Paths’ wheel of souls,
With pity, You rescue the Three Realms’ hellish sufferings.
We return to the Golden Gate’s Heavenly Worthy,
We return to the Six Perfections’ compassionate father.
We return to the Supreme Jade Purity,
Forever free from birth and death’s endless cycle.
Exiting to enter the Void—no dependence remains,
Able to transform decay into immortality.
Encounters in countless eons are rare,
For all beings, You expound on karma’s causes and conditions.
Reviving the corpse, eternal life is raised,
Ensuring form and spirit suffer no change.

When gathered, they are life—
The four limbs rely on nourishment and drink;
When dispersed, they are qi—
A single soul needs no food to sustain it.
Knowing the truth of death,
The form becomes empty space;
Understanding life’s essence,
The qi encompasses ten thousand forms.
If the spiritual nature remains unenlightened,
Then karmic consciousness brings delusion—
Where does the soul’s qi not wander?
It binds itself to the decaying body,
Transforming with all things,
Ever more entangled.
When thoughts arise, calamities follow.
Bearing karmic obstacles,
The wind of karma blows harshly,
Enduring bitter suffering;
Craving food and drink,
The fire of hunger burns fiercely,
Never sated.

Such inversion makes transcendence difficult.
Thus, the Most High, in compassion,
The Primordial Lord, in pity,
Reveals the Dao’s wonders through fragrant offerings,
And washes away folly with law-water’s coolness.
They scatter the darkness of the underworld’s heavy gloom,
And moisten the inner heat of all beings.
The merits are profound, the benefits boundless.

Now, the officiant of this ritual, [Name]’s family,
Offers this for the departed [Name],
Who has departed the dusty world,
Fearing to sink into the dark night.
With sincere devotion, they revere and elevate them.
Purifying the world’s delicacies,
Relying on the Heavenly Lord’s law-bestowal.

You all should now sever the sound of withered hearts,
Taste the richness of the Dao,
Drink the elixir of the Heavenly and Immortal’s mingled essence,
Feast on the Supreme Ultimate’s harmonious qi.

Those who delight in the Southern teachings
Follow accordingly, taking Heaven and Earth as their spring and autumn;

---

They who return their heads to the Dao are born anew,
Standing tall as they see death and life as night and day.

A single word of insight unlocks boundless liberation—
They lean upon the *Ganlu*[1] scripture’s radiance,
To awaken the self-luminous nature of their hearts.

Reciting the *Open Business-Dao and Unlock True Paths*[2] incantation:
Its golden-lighted merits open the dim gates—
Subtle yet vast, dispelling the deepest obscurity.

From the *Hua Chi*[3] flows the scent of truth,
Lotus canopies drift with clouds.
A thousand spirits rejoice in the Primordial Harmony,
Dwelling eternally in the Twelve Palaces.

Swiftly proclaiming the *Lingbao*[4] essence,
They roam at will through the Heavenly Realm.

The *Lingquan*[5] enfolds the Five Phases,[6]
Nourishing all things yet preserving the Dao’s subtlety;
The *Fashui*[7] flows through the Hundred Valleys,[8]
Receiving all impurities yet containing none.

Bearing Heaven’s singular essence as their Sovereign,
They generate the Supreme Benevolence as their Virtue,
Conforming to the conditions to manifest as crooked or straight,
Adapting to the vessel to become square or round.

By reason tracing its origin—
The more exhausted the inquiry, the deeper the mystery;
By the Dao revealing its function—
The more refined the clarity, the more profound the unrest.

Externally, they purge the Six Senses and Ten Evils,[9]
Freeing them from heat and torment, from weariness and suffering;
Externally, they irrigate the Nine Orifices and Hundred Bones,[10]
Achieving the elixir of golden nectar and jade essence.

The Heavenly Lord establishes teachings,
To rescue the lost in the netherworld.
By this praise and offering, they extend boundless support.

For the departed, they recite the *Open Throat and Universal Moistening*[11] incantation of nourishment:

Alas, the endless night of suffering,
Tormented by the Three Paths of heat.
Fierce flames enter the throat—
The longing for eternal life, for quenchless thirst.

A single sprinkle of *Ganlu* nectar,
Cools the burning as the cold of clarity.

The spirit-soul ascends to the Great Luo,[12]
Moistening all things.

The scent of scentless fragrance is priceless—
Burn it, and it returns sevenfold in misty abundance;
The Dao permeates Nature—
Invoke it, and nine luminous rays radiate in splendor.

Thus, the Dao is learned through the heart,
Yet the heart relies on fragrance to transmit it.
Such is its use—
Neither fire nor smoke;
Such is its observation—
Neither millet nor barley.

Within it, no delusion remains,
Its fragrance drifts far.

Ascending to the Three Realms and Ten Heavens,[13]
Descending through the Nine Abysses and Five Paths,[14]
Revealing its profound mysteries,
They offer the departed soul,
Burning it toward the furnace,
Extending boundless support.

They present the scentless, priceless fragrances of the Heavens:
*Return-Soul Fragrance*,
*Reverse-Wind Fragrance*,
*Inverted-Wind Fragrance*,
*Seven-Colored Fragrance*,
*Heavenly Treasure Fragrance*—
Their scent misty and pervasive,
Radiating through the Ten Directions,
Extending boundless support.

The flowers:
Upon the *Yujing Mountain*[15], naturally arise the Seven Treasures Forest;
Within the *Dahai Courtyard*[16], spread the Eight *Qian*[17] Trees.
Lush and vibrant, their verdure unfolds in emerald splendor.
Feasting on the *Qian* Tree’s leaves,
They become the Jade Immortals—
Their bodies transparent as jade, luminous within;
Consuming the Seven Treasures Forest’s blossoms,
They transform into golden bones—
Their Five Viscera[18] like polished gems, round and clear.

Only the Heavenly Unadulterated remains unstained and unattached,
A single petal—how could it soil a robe?
Thus, in the mortal world, it neither grows nor is sown,
How could its five leaves bear fruit?

Golden flowers, jade petals,
*Huachi*[19] yellow sprouts—
No marvel blooms from a common body,
Yet through refining, it becomes the bone of the Immortal.
Three flowers converge at the crown,
Nine breaths[20] coalesce into form—
By this praise and offering, they extend boundless support.

They present the Heavenly wonders of strange realms’ flowers:
*Nine Spirits Supreme Marvelous True Flowers*,
*Five Spirits Minor Marvelous Strange Flowers*,
*Emerald Petals Golden Glow Flowers*,
*Golden Petals Purple-Gold Radiant Flowers*,
*Languan Gardens Azure Jade Orchid Flowers*,
*Jade Forest Flowing Light Treasure Flowers*—
Their light dazzling, illuminating the Ten Directions,
Extending boundless support.

The waters:
Before chaos was divided,
The Primordial Essence was but a single pitcher of sacred elixir—

The divine marvel is already complete,
Dispersed as nine refined elixirs of pure essence.
How few discern the sages’ wisdom,
To save the world, one must know depth and measure.

If one can taste the taste of flavors,
Only then does one perceive the pure of the pure.
Should one drink three cups,
Necessarily, the Great Dao will be understood.

With reverence, I present this offering,
Wishing its fragrance to be savored,
Gathering as the *yangchun*[21] of a full belly,
Scattering as the sweet dew of the heavens—
Penetrating the Three Realms in speechless, laughterless harmony,
Merging all things in one drunkenness, one awakening,
Striking the *Bai Xue Huang E*[22] on the zither,
Raising the cup to invite the Clear Wind and Bright Moon,
Rejoicing in the celestial realm within the vessel,
Roaming the misty peaks beyond the world,
Emulating *Dao Hongkai* in the pursuit of the Way,
Seeking *Bai Yunzi* in the quest for True Reality—
Divine elixirs of immortal alchemy,
The Great Saint’s Sacred Pill,
Holding this sacred nectar,
Extending boundless support.

I present the Seven Heavenly Sacred Elixirs:
*Solar Essence Elixir*,
*Lunar Luster Elixir*,
*Stellar Radiance Elixir*,
*Sweet Dew Elixir*,
*Golden Fluid Elixir*,
*Spirit Light Elixir*,
*Jade Vault Elixir*—
Drinking them brings endlessness,
Circulating through the Ten Directions,
Extending boundless support.

**Fruits:**
Fruits arise from flowers,
Their cultivation must be nurtured by planting.

The stillness of the heart gives birth to the Dao/Way,
Yet it must rely on the strength of cultivation and planting.
Thus there are the coiled peaches of *Zi Xiang*,
And the fire dates of mingled hues,
Nearly taken from the self, distantly drawn from things.

If the heart-field’s purity is clear and bright,
Then fruits flourish in abundance;
Or if thorns and brambles grow thickly,
Then roots and shoots wither away.

Their color like citrus, yet sweet as honey,
Some ripen after years, others at their appointed time,
Some take three thousand years to form,
Some mature in an instant’s flash—
Chewing them, the spirit feels invigorated,
Savoring them, the mind becomes lucid and clear.

If the fruit arises from its cause,
Then one must discard the flower and focus on the essence.
At this moment, the mind is fully illuminated.
Through this praise, boundless support is extended.

I offer the Seven Heavenly Sacred Fruits of *Qiónglín*:
The *Kōngdòng* spirit-gourd,
The *Wànsuì* immortal peach,
The *Jīnzhǐ* golden dates,
The *Yuánguāng* primal essence fruits,
The *Chìlíng* crimson spirit dates,
The *Fēidān* flying alchemy pomegranates—
Their fragrance thick and pervasive,
Eating them brings endlessness,
Circulating through the Ten Directions,
Extending boundless support.

**Food:**
Heavenly and human sustenance, bland and flavorless,
Recorded in the *Huángtíng* scriptures;
The *Shūmǐ* millet grains,
Refined without remainder, their merit marked in *Língbǎo*.
Thus the highest sages,
Only savor the *Chōnghé* balanced taste;
While those descending to the mortal realm,
Indulge in rich delicacies to repel demons.

The Four Heavenly Fragrant Rice of the celestial kitchen,
Born from the common folk’s grains;
Yet the world’s hundred varieties of rice and millet,
Each kernel earned through toil and suffering.

Those who enjoy blessings without laboring to eat,
Should reflect on their origins;
Those who have abundance yet know contentment,
Must not cast it away lightly.

In this *Fǎhuì* assembly of sacred practice,
I prepare the *Huìxiāo* fine offerings.
Thus I present these fragrant feasts,
To nourish the departed spirits.

Through this praise, boundless support is extended.

I offer the Four Heavenly Fragrant Rices:
*Fēngshān* Abundant Mountain Rice,
*Lóngshān* Dragon Mountain Rice,
*Qīngjīng* Verdant Essence Rice,
*Tàihé* Grand Harmony Rice—
Their fragrance thick and pervasive,
Eating them brings endlessness,
Circulating through the Ten Directions,
Extending boundless support.

The *heart-flower* of wisdom’s fruit,
The *golden rice* and *jade nectar*,
The *Língbǎo* spirit’s fragrant wisdom,
The *pífēn* subtle dharma-flavors—
All rely on things to manifest the Dao/Way,
Yet one should perceive the mind through their form.

Each should offer sincere and expansive devotion,
Turning it into boundless merit.
May all beings on the great earth attain fullness,
No creature left unnourished by its essence.

Further, through fitting praise,
To complete the awakening.

Hearing the *Fǎnwèi* wisdom’s radiance in the *Tàiwú* boundless void,
The *round penetration* of all mysteries;
Refining the true light within the dharma-body,
Savoring the *Chōnghé* balanced taste.

Able to draw sufficiency from all forms,
Initially not dependent on external things.

After the *spirit-food* incantation,
I hope for your departed soul,
To absorb the *Língmáng* luminous essence of the inner landscape,
To steady the central *zhōngzhuàng* true position,
To drink the *Qióngguì* dewdrops of the spirit-tree,
To eat the *Huánghuá* golden petals’ jade-like tenderness,
To grasp the Dao’s profound mysteries,
To congeal the spirit in the boundless expanse,
To rest in the *yuánfáng* primal chamber and lie at ease,
To aid the true transformation in its boundless circulation.

Offered to the departed,
To merit their rebirth in the heavenly realms.
Recite the *Yùqīng Dàcí* Great Compassionate Sovereign’s *Gānlù* Nectar Law-Food Incantation:

Turn back and gaze upon the *Yuánluó* round canopy,
Uniting the scene and drawing the luminous essence.
Confining the soul, restraining the seven *pò*,
Focusing the mind, centering the *zhōngzhuàng*.
Moving, dwelling, walking in the boundless void,
Sleeping, resting in the *yuánfáng* primal chamber.
Hunger, feast on the *Huángbì* golden petals;
Thirst, drink the *Qiónggēn* dewdrop nectar.
The spirit-banners command the *tiān mó* heavenly demons,
Uniting the body, refining the true light.
Once more illuminating the *Tàiwú* boundless void,
Endlessly dwelling in the mid-air realm.
Round penetration fades at the *bōjí* wave’s edge,
True transformation knows no final limit.
Profound mysteries without beginning or end,
The practitioner must clearly understand.
Silent and vast, forgetting teachings and precepts,
Responding to the *yùn* cosmic flow, vast and unconstrained.
The Dao’s mirror does not shine by itself,
It must first be polished by what is offered.
Union finds no duality,
Separation follows the heart’s will.

Now mingled in the *mángwèi* murky and luminous,
Transformation not yet riding the single *qì* breath.

To reverse their original knowledge,
Form must arise from the *sān guāng* Three Lights.
Appropriate to sing and chant in the *qīngyáo* clear melodies,
To unfold the path of birth and rebirth.

After the *spirit-food* incantation,
I hope for your departed soul,
To embrace the *yīn* and cradle the *yáng*,
To draw the *rìyuè* sun-moon’s ascending *bēn* vital qi,
To mold the soul and cast the spirit,
To store the *kǎnlí* water-fire’s constructed essence.
The Three Palaces full and replete,
The Ten Aspects complete—
Early ascending to the *tōngdá* realm of boundless passage,
Endlessly roaming the *zhìhuì* gate of wisdom.

Offered to the departed,
To merit their rebirth in the heavenly realms.
Recite the *Sānguāng* Three Lights Illuminating the Nectar Law-Food Incantation:

Vast and crystalline, the *yuángì* primal qi is born,
Perfusing the *tàikōng* great void.
The two *yào* luminaries shine together,
The five *wéi* constellations harmonize in turn.
The Three Lights radiant, their brilliance complete,
Sacred qi fills the Three Palaces.
The imperial domain gathers the *jiǔlǎo* Nine Elders,
Feasting on the *bǎitǐ* hundred forms of abundance.
The *Jīnhuá* golden petals illuminate the scene,
Body aligned with the sun and moon.
In thought of the Dao, before the highest sages,
Endless life through ten thousand kalpas.
Heavenly beings nurture the people,
Accumulating the *sānwānliùqiān* thirty-six thousand divine qi;
The world abandons the Great Dao/Way,
Destroying the *yībǎiliùshí* one hundred and eighty spirit-gates.
Self-corruption damages the true roots,
No nourishment blooms in the jade tree.
The spirit does not grant itself,
The shadow wanders with demons.

To reverse the source of life,
One must rely on the *fàn* sacred chant.
After the *spirit-food* incantation,
I hope for your departed soul,
To obtain the *zhònghuà* myriad transformations’ primal essence,
To restore the five *shén* spirits’ true dwelling,
The *Bái Yuán* White Sovereign on the right as guardian,
The *Gōngzǐ* Prince on the left as support,
The crown adorned with the *fēicùi* floating emerald canopy,
The feet encircled by the *jīnlián* golden lotus.
Fragrant clouds enfold the body,
Sweet nectar sprinkles the heart,
The *zhànhuǎng* profound and elusive primal spirit,
Nourishing the *xīyí* subtle true qi.

Offered to the departed,
To merit their rebirth in the heavenly realms.
Recite the *Yùqīng Dàbēi* Great Compassion Cloud Palace’s *Yīnshēng* Dark Birth Incantation for the *Fànchàng* Sacred Chant and *Shēnghún* Soul-Bathing:

The cloud-root boundless, the myriad transformations’ essence,
The seven *pò* spirits congealed within,
The three *hún* souls inwardly knotted.
The *èrshí sì zhēn* Twenty-Four True Ones,
Enter and exit without gate.
The profound and elusive essence,
The profound and elusive primal spirit.
Following the *jié* kalpa’s rise and fall,
Born with the *qì* breath.
Internally congealed in the *hùnpò* mixed simplicity,
Externally nurtured by the seven *jīng* channels.
The five *shén* spirits planted in the *huá* petals,
The three *tái* platforms spread with luster.
The *zǐquè* purple gate and pristine *sùtóng* youth,
Returning the soul to its *yuán* origin.
Ascending on clouds to become immortal,
Ranging through mists, floating in the void.
Within lies the *Yùjīng* Jade Capital,
Called the *shén gōng* Divine Palace.
On the right, the *wúyīng* peerless guardian,
On the left, the *Bái Yuán* White Sovereign’s support.

The dark beasts block the rear, the vermilion birds guard the front.
Above, they float beneath the emerald canopy, below, they tread the golden lotus.
Fragrant clouds condense in the void, sweet dew flows endlessly.
Using it, it is never exhausted; seeking it, it is never found.

The Nine Abysses of black darkness, where the Six Bandits are confined in iron prisons;
A single thought of clarity, the Great Void knows no boundary.

To leisurely dwell in the True Realm,
One must savor the Great Harmony.

Further wield the **Treasure Scrolls** (*bǎozhāng*),
To uphold the strict **Dharma flavors** (*fǎwèi*).

After the **spiritual meal** (*zòushí*), I hope for your departed soul (*wánglíng*),
To drink the sweet dew’s **falling mist** (*língmèng*), eternally purifying the heart’s defilements (*xīngòu*);
To ride the **Jade Sound’s** (*Yùyīn*) song and call, seated in divine wandering (*shényóu*).

While the **feast and wine** (*yáojiǔ*) remain,
The Eight Extremes are traversed.

Offered for the departed (*wángzhě*),
To ascend and nourish the **Pure Land of the Heavens** (*wǎngshēng tiānjiè*).

Recite the **Nine Abysses Transcendent Sweet Dew Dharma-Meal Spell** (*Jiǔyōu chāoshēng gānlù fǎshí zhòu*):

Cold and flowing, the sweet dew nourishes,
Its **Dharma flavor** (*fǎwèi*) beyond measure.
Like **cyan-lined forests** (*piānlín*), it flows with seven treasures,
Forever banishing hunger and thirst.

To receive this **Dharma offering of food** (*fǎshí*),
Ascend to the heavens, entering the **Purple Chamber** (*Zǐfáng*).

Its lingering essence brings cool relief,
Reaching all beings.

The **underworld’s** depths are iron-walled,
Bound by the **Iron Enclosure** (*tiěwéi*) of its firmness;
The **heavenly realm’s** vastness knows no ascent,
No **stages of rank** (*jiējí*) to climb.

Relying on the **golden light of ten thousand Dao** (*wàndào jīnguāng*),
Breaking the **Nine Yin paths** (*jiǔyīn quánlù*).

After the **spiritual meal** (*zòushí*), I hope for your departed soul (*wánglíng*),
That **Great Stability** (*Tàidìng*) arises from heavenly light (*tiānguāng*),
And **auspiciousness** (*jíxiáng*) is born in the **Void Chamber** (*xūshì*).

The **Jade Terrace’s** Twelve Residences (*Yùlóu shíèr*),
Clearing the **sore throat** (*sǎoyàn*) in the **Flower Pool** (*Huápíng*);
The **Earthly Pivot’s** Nine True Ones (*Níhuán jiǔzhēn*),
Silently attending the **Supreme Deity** (*Shàngdì*).

This is the **path to ascension** (*shēngtiān jìnglù*),
Stretching the **auspicious light of breaking prison** (*pòyù zhāngshū*),
Reaching the **Extreme Heights of Bright Clarity** (*jǐ gāomíng*),
Attaining **Great Freedom** (*Dàzìrài*).

Offered for the departed (*wángzhě*),
To ascend and nourish the **Pure Land of the Heavens** (*wǎngshēng tiānjiè*).

Recite the **Breaking Prison, Ascending to Heaven Spell** (*Pòyù shēngtiān zhòu*):

Vast and boundless within **Dingdu** (*Chéngdū*),
Layered **Golden Mountain** (*Jīngāngshān*).
The **Spiritual Treasure’s** boundless light (*Língbǎo wúliàng guāng*),
Piercingly illuminates the **Fiery Pool** (*Yánchí fán*).

The **Seven Ancestors’** departed souls (*Qīzǔ zhū yōuhún*),
Their bodies borne aloft by fragrant clouds.

The **Flowers of Green Lotus** (*Qīngliánhuā*) for **Stability** (*Dìnghuì*) and **Blessing** (*Yì*),
Ascending to eternal safety.

The **Three Lights** (*Sānguāng*) flow their essence,
Congealing into the **Pierced True Body** (*Dòngzhēn tǐ*), returning to the **Great Void** (*Tàimáng*).

Descending to the **Abyssal Palace** (*Yuāndiān gōng*),
Ascending to the **Peerless Realm** (*Wúhé xiāng*).

Though the body may wander back,
The traces are forgotten in an instant.

The **Seven Treasures** congeal in purity,
The **Mixed Chaos** (*Hùndùn*) blooms with fragrant splendor.

Swallowing the **Nine Qi of Clouds** (*Jiǔqì yún*),
This joy knows no end.

Previously proclaimed were the **Spiritual Treasure Scrolls** (*Língbǎo zhāngbào*),
All are the **Original Sovereign’s** divine spells (*Yuánzūn shénzhòu*),
The **True Explanations** (*Zhēngshèng zhēnquán*) of the saints,
The **Nine Elixirs’** wondrous secrets (*Jiǔdān miàojié*),
The **Sweet Dew’s** Dharma utterances (*Gānlù fǎyán*).
Mysteries profound and causes unfathomable,
All used in **sacrificial offerings** (*zījiàn*).

The departed, having passed through my hands,
Enjoy the **Pure Land’s** simple, correct flavors (*dànpō zhèngwèi*),
All beauties following in suit;
Obtain the **Pierced True Essence** (*Huǎnghuò yuánjīng*),
Eternal life without death.

Still, I pass on the remaining blessings (*yúqìng*),
Bestowing **longevity’s** lingering traces (*chóngshōu miǎocún*),
Ascending to the **Round Canopy** (*Yuángǎi*),
Descending to the **Square Realm** (*Fāngyú*),
All bathed in **auspicious connections** (*liángyuán*),
Together climbing the **Dao’s shores** (*dào’àn*).

**Offerings to all fields of merit** (*fúdìan*),
**Offerings first** (*shīshí*).
In the **future Pure Land** (*xiànglái jìngtǔ*),
Clothing and food arise naturally.

Thus, the **supplications** (*gòngyǎng*),
Are universally presented to all the heavens.

**Dharma-Meal Offerings** (*Fǎshí xiāngchú miàogòng*),
To the **Heavenly Sovereign** (*Tiānzūn*) above,
To the **True Saints** (*Zhēnshèng*) in the middle,
And to all ten thousand kinds of **sentient beings** (*wànlèi hánshēng*) below,
All equally share in the **supplication** (*gòngyǎng*).

**Offerings for the departed** (*Wángrén shí*):
The remaining **vegetarian meals** (*zàizhāi*),
Are returned to the **underworld paths** (*mínglù*).
Those who eat are sated,
Free from all hardships.

The **Great Dao’s** compassion,
Guides them back to the **Immortal Path** (*xiānlù*).

**Dao Gate’s** universal teachings—
Must use **Volume Five** of the **Collected Scrolls** (*jíjuàn*).
