**Master Lü Taigu of the Crane Forest Daoist School’s *Reading and Guidance* Section**
*Preface to the *Praise of the Guidance Rites* by Master Guangcheng*

The scriptures refer to **"fasting officials"** (*zhāiguān*) within the **ritual assembly**—those who practice the Dao of fasting. Today, this is mistakenly called the **"fasting master."**

Those of highest **virtue/power** (*dé*) and **Dao** are called **Lawmasters** (*Fǎshī*), equivalent to **High Functionaries** (*gāogōng*). Those well-versed in **ritual precepts** (*fǎdù*) serve as **Chief Lecturers** (*dūjiǎng*), responsible for chanting, guiding, and upholding the **rites and regulations**. To ensure the **officers** stand in order and the **ritual formations** stand solemn, the **drum and bell** must first be struck. Only then may the assembly gather, and the **Chief Lecturer** ascend the platform to chant.

If the **Chief Lecturer**’s years of **virtue/power** are slightly greater and they wish to avoid excessive labor, one may be appointed from among the officers to strike the bell and lead the rites. Though this practice arose from necessity, it is not the ancient custom. Now that the bell is established as fixed ritual, it has endured for long.

Ancient rites were simple, but modern rituals have grown elaborate. The **High Functionary** and **Lawmaster** lead the **supplications**, their bows and movements setting the example for the assembly. If they are aged or infirm, they may retire of their own accord—never should they be replaced by another, lest it appear as redundant office.

The **Supervisor of the Fasting** (*Jiānzhāi*) upholds the **ritual statutes** (*kēxiàn*) and corrects transgressions. If any offense occurs, they must first warn with a **penalty register**. Those punished must accept their guilt without grumbling, lest disputes arise during **ritual admonition**, bringing shame upon the assembly.

The **Divine Sage’s Attendant** (*Xuánshèng shìjīng*) oversees the **platform** (*tánchǎng*), arranging the **ritual seating** and ensuring all **offerings** are properly prepared. According to ancient practice, within the **fasting hall**—today’s **platform**—two high seats are placed for **morning, noon, and evening lectures**. Those who have mastered the scriptures below the **Lawmaster** may request to ascend the **Law Seat**.

When the **scripture recitation** begins, once the officers are seated, one performs **purification**, while the **Incense Attendant** tends the incense and the **Scripture Attendant** holds the scripture. After recitation, the scripture must be carefully stored in the **fasting hall**, held in strict **veneration**, lest the tables be left disordered, the platform defiled, or outsiders trespass, lightly profaning the **Divine Worthies**.

The **Incense Attendant’s** duties are detailed in the **ritual register**, yet many today neglect them through laxity. The **Lamp Attendant** must diligently maintain the lamps—extinguishing and relighting them as needed—this alone fulfills their role. Recently, some unqualified individuals have excluded the **Scripture Attendant** from arranging the **platform**, instead establishing a **"Direct Platform"** (*zhítán*) title. Today’s **Direct Platform** is what was once the **Scripture Attendant’s** duty.

Beyond the **six primary roles**, there are many redundant positions. This stems from **Sichuan’s** addition of **external platform rituals** beyond the ancient rites, which the officers did not originally perform. Due to neglect, the **three attendants** were made to also **recite repentance verses** and serve the **external platform**, leaving the **Scripture Attendant, Incense Attendant, and Lamp Attendant** unfulfilled in their own duties. Though divided among them, they must still wear **ritual attire** when performing **ritual duties**. This should be examined to align with proper **rites and regulations**.

According to the **Golden Register’s** ancient rites and the **Yellow Register’s** old laws, on the **night of the vigil** and during **meritorious recitation**, one first performs the **Natural Morning Rites**—that is, **paying homage to the Ten Directions** and offering **three repentances**. Only then does the ritual proceed.

Thus, the **fasting ritual sequence** begins at **hour *xū*** (7–9 PM), when the officers are summoned before the **Mysterious Teacher** (*Xuánshī*). One reads the **office statement**, then casts the **petition** onto the **main platform**, offers incense to the **Ten Directions**, ascends to the **inner altar**, offers incense, pays homage to the **Teacher**, lights the **incense burner**, and bows in **morning reverence**. Next, the **fasting petition** is read, followed by the **Great Thanksgiving** and the **proclamation of precepts**. The **Chief Lecturer**, having received their office, recites the **scriptural prohibitions**, makes a **vow**, relights the burner, and returns to stand before the **Mysterious Teacher** once more.

Hence it is said: *"At dawn’s first light, proceed according to the Dao’s law."* This method, transmitted from **Zhang Daoling**, **Lu Jianji**, **Kou Qingzhi**, and **Zhang Qingdu**, has endured through the ages, always maintaining that the **fasting rites** originate from the **Natural Morning Rites**, lest the source be forgotten.

Recently, some mediocre scholars, failing to grasp the intent of the ancients, have **prematurely appointed the six offices** before the **Mysterious Teacher**, proclaiming the **scriptural prohibitions** before ascending the platform, then claiming that **Lu Jianji’s fasting rites** are erroneous. Their false praise and slander only serve to confuse—how little they know! Even their followers imitate this, not only disrupting the **ritual order** but also slandering the **worthy teachers**. Those who understand the **Dao’s teachings** should reject them.

**Du Guangting of the Eastern Isles** writes: Examining ancient rites, there is no **"incense blessing"** (*zhùxiāng*), **"courtly attendance"** (*tíngcān*), or **"proclamation of supplications."** When **Yang Xue**, the **Master of Letters**, revised the **Golden Register rites**, he included an **"incense blessing"**—this was the **official Daoist assembly’s** fixed order. After offering incense and bowing, a **declared Daoist** would state the **fasting intent**, then retire to stand before the **Mysterious Teacher** to assume their office. Today, during **ritual exorcisms**, the **High Functionary** performs the **incense blessing**.

Ancient rites were not without **spirit invocation**—this was the **vigil night**. Hence, **Master Guangcheng** repeatedly expounds upon it. Therefore, the **appointment of offices** and **proclamation of precepts** must follow the **recitation of petitions**, first informing the **Highest Truths** of the **fasting intent**—this is not the time for **descending blessings** or **offering libations**.

Since **Master Wu Ruo** composed the *Critique of Errors*, he favored his own views, claiming: *"How could one appoint offices and proclaim precepts only after the sacrificial rites conclude?"* **Yang Xue**, following **Wu Ruo’s** mistake, moved the **appointment of offices** and **proclamation of precepts** to before the **ritual invocation**, greatly deviating from the intent of all past **lineage masters**.

Now we have **spirit invocation**, **vigil night rites**, and **initial platform announcements** outside the platform—this is like **building a house beneath a house and a roof above a roof**. Though practiced for long, it is difficult to alter. At least, one might eliminate the **vigil night invocation** and the **three-day morning announcements**, which would be somewhat acceptable.

「With reverence, I adopt the ritual sequences established by **Master Guangcheng**, **Yang Xue the Scholar**, and **Master Sun the Teacher**, cross-referencing them with ancient rites, compiling the *Praise of the Dao*, and adapting past traditions to present needs—all to aid the Dao’s transformation.

For the **Daoist common teachings**, the sixth and seventh volumes of the *Collected Scriptures* must be used.
The **Daoist common teachings** also require the *Crane Forest Collection* of **Lü Taigu the Daoist**, particularly the **"Wēiyí Rites"** (*Wēiyí Yì*) and **"Ordinating the Platform Rites"** (*Qìngtán Yì*), alongside the three concordant editions of **Du the Celestial Master**, **Yang Zigong** (次公), and **Zhang Wujin** (无尽).

In general, when the platform faces due north, the **Grand Invocation** (*Dūjiǎng*) should be performed at the **door of the platform** (*dìhù*), meaning the **platform exterior**—this is the **platform’s outer precinct** (*tánwài*). **Celestial Master Zhang Wanfu**’s preface to the *Ritual Procedures* (*Xùshì Yì*) includes a diagram of the platform, designating the **Grand Invocation** (*Dūjiǎng*) as the **Wēiyí Invocation** (*Wēiyí Jiǎng*), implying that all **Wēiyí rites** within a single platform are led by the **Grand Invocation**. Thus, the **ordination of the platform** should be conducted by the **Grand Invocation** alone.

However, **Yang Zigong** (杨杰次公) states: *"Appoint a Daoist of Wēiyí rank to ordain the platform."* This fails to recognize that the **Grand Invocation** itself is the **Wēiyí**. He further says: *"Place the **Jian Water** (*Jiànshuǐ*) at the **door of the platform** (*dìhù*)."* This overlooks the fact that the **Grand Invocation**’s designated position is already the **door of the platform**. If the platform does not face due north, it should be relocated accordingly.

**White Invocation** (*Bái Shì*) and **spirit contemplation** (*Cúnxiǎng*) are to be performed.

**Celestial Master Du** states: *"The Wēiyí Master, wearing the **mystic cap** (*Xuánguān*) and **crimson robe** (*Zhànghè*), stands at the **door of the platform**, and the **White Invocation** (*Bái Shì*) is performed to present the received **scriptures and ordination credentials** (*Jīngzhuó*) for the **appointment of offices** (*Zhìzhí*)."*

I, **Subject [Name]**, humbly hear that none surpasses the **hundred spirits** (*bǎilíng*) in harmonizing **yin and yang** (*Yùnyáng*); yet none can equal the **Great Dao** (*Dàdào*) in **saving the realm and the family** (*Jìjiāguó*) or **communing with the luminous and the dark** (*Yōumíng*).

Thus, the **Jade Hall** (*Bìluò*) undergoes transformations of calamity and fortune, which may be dispelled; the **Yellow Register** (*Huánglù*) contains rites of deliverance, permitting their observance and practice. Your subjects, humbly emulating the **True Transformation** (*Zhēnhuà*), though unworthy, hold official rank. In all places traversed, how dare we forget to repay with devotion?

Now, we petition to construct a certain **ritual hall** (*zhāi*) at [location], for a span of [number] days and nights, performing **Dao rituals** (*xíngdào*) and **scripture-turning** (*zhuǎnjīng*), in accordance with the prescribed rites. Your subjects, refining our **form and qi** (*xíngqì*), purifying our **spirit and vitality** (*jīngshén*), shall diligently execute this, daring not to fail in reporting upward.

We humbly await the **Most High’s** (*Tàishàng*) proclamation of new decrees, the boundless grace of **covering and nurturing** (*fùyù*), commanding the **True Officials** (*Zhēnguān*) to oversee and descend in judgment. May the mists and clouds briefly cease at the **Three Canopies** (*Sānjǐng*), and winds and rains not assail the **Four Seas** (*Sìméng*). Our **confessions** (*chuànxiè*) shall surely be heard, and our petitions transmitted without obstruction. Your subjects, overwhelmed by such boundless grace, focus our thoughts on the **True One** (*Zhēn*), awaiting the response.

As **Master Yang** originally stated: Before the **White Invocation** (*Bái Shì*), first contemplate the **Three Masters** (*Sānshī*) in the west—then the **Three True Lords of Tang, Ge, and Zhou** (*Táng-Gě-Zhōu Sān Zhēnjūn*) before you. **Lord Tang** (*Tángjūn*), of **Júyáng**, with **celestial-crown** (*Tiānguān*) and **red scripture-register** (*Zhàngzhāng dān yī*), wields the **Dragon-Headed Treasure Sword** (*Lóngtóu Bǎojiàn*), his left hand holding a **talisman**. **Lord Ge** (*Gējūn*), clad in ritual attire, holds a **jade spear**. **Lord Zhou** (*Zhōujūn*), in his **crown and robes**, wields the **Jade Yang Node**. Next, contemplate the **True Official** (*Zhēnguān*) in **crimson robes**, riding the **Nine-Phoenix Chariot** (*Jiǔfèng Chéng*) and the **Big Dipper**, descending to purify the defilements at the altar. Then, contemplate the **Seven Stars** covering your head with their handles pointing forward, lest they obstruct your vision.

Only then proceed with the **White Invocation**—though it is better to first contemplate the **Four Spirits** (*Sìlíng*) at your left, right, front, and rear, with the **Sun, Moon, and Five Stars** (*Rìyuè Wǔxīng*) above your head. This is from **Du Yi’s** method.

Upon completing contemplation, pass the **tablet** (*jiǎn*) to the attendant. Next, **clasp the fist** (*wògù*), hands hanging naturally, and summon the **Four Spirits**.

**Clasping the fist**: With the **thumb pressing the middle finger’s middle joint**, the other four fingers drawn into the palm.

**Eastern Azure Dragon** (*Dōngfāng Qīnglóng*), essence of the **Horn and Kneecap** (*Jiǎo-Kàng*), exhales **clouds and suppressed qi**, roars with **thunderous voice**. Soaring through the **Eight Extremes** (*Bājí*), circling the **Four Seas**, come stand at my left.

**Western White Tiger** (*Xīfāng Báihǔ*), corresponding to **Zīshēn**, its **pure essence** and **solemn tones** awe birds and beasts, its howls stirring mountains and forests—come stand at my right.

**Southern Vermilion Bird** (*Nánfāng Zhūquè*), leader of all birds, born from the **Crimson Cavern**, its **azure sky echoes** resounding with **five-colored splendor** and **six symbolic forms**—come guide me before.

**Northern Dark Tortoise** (*Běifāng Xuánwǔ*), born of **Great Yin**, its **void and perilous essence**, **turtle and serpent** merged—circling the **Nine Terrains**, commanding all spirits—come follow me behind.

Next, **both hands pressed to the heart**, feet stepping into the **Ding-character stance**. Having summoned the Four Spirits, they shall now **circle like a belt**, the **Sun clasped by the Moon** in motion.

The **Sixteen Divine Generals of the Nine Regions** (*Jiǔzhōu Shíliù Shénjiāng*) serve as my emissaries. Under the **Great Unity Star Lord** (*Tàiyī Xīngjūn*), there are sixteen divine generals who know the **calamities and blessings of the world**. Some, unacquainted with this, mistakenly alter it to **sixty divine generals**. The **Heaven, Earth, and Water Officials** (*Tiāndì Shuǐguān*) share their auspiciousness.

The characters **Heaven, Earth, Water** (*Tiān-Dì-Shuǐ*) are stepped as **Ding, Gāng, and Sān Cái** (*Sāncái bù*), at the **sword-water** (*jiànshuǐ*), invoking **Yang Yi’s** method. The old rites speak of **Heaven, Earth, and Water Officials**, but **Yang’s** version is superior.

Next, the **right hand grasps the sword**. The **Five Phases** (*Wǔxíng*)—**Fire, Wood, Water, Earth, Metal**—are in motion. My **rigid sword** commands and restrains **ghosts and spirits**. The **Twenty-Eight Constellations** (*Èrshíbāxiù*) array before my will. The **Seven Stars of the Big Dipper** (*Běidǒu Qīxīng*) flank and assist the **Numinous True One**. Circling the ten thousand directions, all blessings converge.

Next, the **left hand holds the water vessel** (*shuǐkuàng*). The **Yangtze, Yellow, Huai, and Sea rivers** are not **Divine Water** (*Shénshuǐ*); **Divine Water** refers to **cauldron-water** (*zhuóshuǐ*), while those rivers are **mundane**. Some mistakenly alter this to **mundane water**, an error in their sight.

The **Five Dragons** exhale to purify **Heaven and Earth**. The **Great Emperor** (*Dàdì*) has worn it for ten thousand years; today, I shall cleanse the **demonic qi**.

Facing the **sword and water**, chant the incantation:
*"With reverence, I summon the **Eastern Azure Dragon** (*Dōngfāng Qīnglóng*), bearing talisman and sword, descending **True Qi** into my water. The **Southern Vermilion Dragon** (*Nánfāng Zhīlóng*), bearing talisman and sword, descending **True Qi** into my water. The **Western White Dragon** (*Xīfāng Báihǔ*), bearing talisman and sword, descending **True Qi** into my water. The **Northern Black Dragon** (*Běifāng Hēilóng*), bearing talisman and sword, descending **True Qi** into my water. The **Central Yellow Dragon** (*Zhōngyāng Huánglóng*), bearing talisman and sword, descending **True Qi** into my water.*

*My water is no ordinary water—it is the **Five Dragons’ and Five Stars’ True Qi Water**. My sword is no ordinary blade—**nine-fold refined**, its rigidity unyielding, the **Seven Stars** flanking it, **treading the Big Dipper**, **straddling the Arc of the General** (*Kuaì Gāng*). The **Great Unity** (*Tàiyī*) forms the **water character**; the **crossbar** (*gāng*) is also written as **‘action’** (*zuò*). **Yang’s** version uses **‘in’** (*zài*), which is superior.*

*Circling the ten thousand directions—three versions omit the lines ‘spraying water upon Heaven’ and ‘sprinkling water upon Earth.’ Water cleanses beyond measure; filth cannot surpass impurity. With purity, impurity is dispelled; with water, defilement is governed. There are no lines about ‘hurrying to depart ten thousand li’ or ‘not stopping.’*

*Urgent, as the **Law decrees** (*Lǜlìng*), commanding restraint.*

*Facing the **Break** (*Pò*)—as in **Yang’s** version—when the **Dipper’s Handle** (*Dǒugǎng*) points straight, its direction is **Break**. Though the altar’s orientation may be inconvenient, mental contemplation suffices.*

Next, proceed to the **southwest**, reciting the **Purification of Heaven and Earth Cauldron** (*Jìng Tiāndì Zhòu*):
*"The **Void of the Cavern** (*Dòngzhōng Xuánxū*), the **Gleaming Primordial** (*Huàngyào Tàiyuán*). The **Eight Directions’ Mighty Spirits**, making me naturally authoritative. The **Numinous Treasure Talismans**, universally proclaimed to the **Nine Heavens**. **Buyan Luo** (*Buyan Luo*), **Cavernous Polar Primordial** (*Dònggāng Tàixuán*), slaying demons, binding evils, killing ten thousand ghosts. The **Central Mountain God’s Cauldron** (*Zhōngshān Shén Zhòu*), **Primordial Beginning’s Jade Text** (*Yuánshǐ Yùwén*), when I recite once, ghosts retreat and years extend. Treading the **Five Sacred Peaks**, the **Eight Seas** know my voice. The **Demon King** bows eastward, guarding my **True Person**. Malignant defilements dispersed, **Dao-Qi** eternally preserved.*

*Urgent, as the **Law decrees**.*

Next, proceed to the **west-north**, reciting the **Pacification of the Land Cauldron** (*Ān Tǔdì Zhòu*):
*"The **Primordial Pacification** (*Yuánshǐ Ānzhèn*), universally proclaimed to all spirits. **Mountain and Water True Officials**, **Land Spirits**—left **Community**, right **Grain**—let none disturb in vain. Returning to the **True Path**, inner and outer purified, each in their proper place, guarding the **Imperial Court**. The **Most High commands**: ‘Hunt and capture evil essences.’"*

---

**To the Dao/Way’s Protector God-King, safeguarding the Dao/Way’s Hall:**
*"I take refuge in the Great Dao/Way, eternally honoring chastity and rectitude.*
*Urgent, as the Law decrees.*

**Next, to the northeast quadrant, recite the Purification of the Altar Cauldron** (*Jìng Tán Zhòu*):
*"I am the **Primordial Sovereign** (*Dòngzhōng Tài-Yī Zhēn*), the **Four Spirits** beneath my celestial step.*
*My head bears the **Heavenly Cauldron** (*Tiān Gāng*), my feet tread the **Four Sacred Beasts**.*
*With **Dragon-Qi** (*Lóng lì*) at the **Xun** position, I turn and march until I reach **Kun**.*
*Seal the **Earthly Portal** (*Dìhù*), guard the **Guan Palace** (*Bǐng Gōng*), and bind the **Five Sacred Steps** (*Yǔ bù*).*
*Let no malevolent **Yao-Qi** (*yāo-fēn*) linger beyond.*
*Rightly aligned, the **Sacred Steps** (*Yǔ bù*) and **Heavenly Cauldron** (*Gāng*) face **Qian** and **Hai**—*
*until I reach the **Heavenly Gate** (*Tiān mén*) to pay homage to the **Celestial Sovereign** (*Dì Jūn*).*
*Urgent, as the Law decrees.*

**Next, to the southeast, call upon the **Heavenly Blue General** (*Tiān Péng Yuànshuài*) and recite the incantation:**
*"This is the **Five Sovereigns’ Invocation of the Northern Spirits** (*Běidì Wǔlíng Yuànlǎo Zhòu*),*
*issued from the **True One’s** (*Zhèngyī*) examination and summoning to sever evil and guide the righteous.*
*Heavenly Blue! Heavenly Blue!*
*The **Nine Mysteries** (*Jiǔ Xuán*) slay the **Young Mages** (*shì tóng*).*
*The **Five Ding** (*Wǔ Dīng*) command, **High Sly** (*Gāo Diāo*) and **Northern Public** (*Běi Gōng*),*
*the **Seven Stars** (*Qī Zhèng*) and **Eight Spirits** (*Bā Líng*),*
*the **Most High’s** (*Tài Shàng*) radiant and brutal might.*
*Long-necked beasts, grasping the **Imperial Bell** (*Dì Zhōng*).*
*The **White Phoenix** (*Sù Xiāo*) of the **Three Celestial Marks** (*Sān Chén*),*
*strictly harnessed with the **Kui Dragon** (*Qúi Lóng*).*
*The **Sword-Wielding Deity-King** (*Wēi Jiàn Shénwáng*) beheads evil, erasing its traces.*
*Purple-Qi ascends to Heaven, crimson clouds surge forth.*
*Devouring demons, consuming ghosts,*
*crossing bodies to drink the wind.*
*The **Pale-Tongued, Green-Toothed** (*Cāngshé Lǜchǐ*) **Four-Eyed Elder** (*Lǎo Gōng*),*
*the **Heavenly Ding** (*Tiān Dīng*) **Force-Mage** (*Lìshì*),*
*commanding the South, subduing the brutal.*
*The **Heavenly Steed** (*Tiān Zú*) strikes fiercely,*
*commanding the North, bearing the blade.*
*Thirty myriads of soldiers,*
*guard my **Ninefold Enclosure** (*Jiǔ Chóng*).*
*Dispelling corpses a thousand *lǐ* distant,*
*clearing away all inauspicious signs.*
*Should any minor ghost dare to approach,*
*to witness my form—*
*the **Heaven-Cleaving Axe** (*Biāo Tiān Dà Fǔ*) splits its **Fivefold Shape** (*Wǔ Xíng*).*
*The **Flame Emperor** (*Yán Dì*) rips its blood,*
*the **Northern Dipper** (*Běi Dǒu*) shatters its bones.*
*The **Four Ming** (*Sì Míng*) break its remains,*
*the **Heavenly Ding** (*Tiān Yóu*) annihilates its kind.*
*One stroke of the **Divine Blade** (*Shén Dāo*),*
*and ten thousand ghosts dissolve in ruin.*
*Urgent, as the Law decrees.*

**Next, to the southwest, call upon the **Heavenly Ding** (*Tiān Péng*) **Vice-General** (*Fù Yuànshuài*) and recite the incantation:**
*"The **Heavenly Ding** (*Tiān Péng*) **Divine General** (*Shén Jiāng*) commands all demons.*
*My head bears the **Celestial Circle** (*Tiān Yuán*), my feet stride the **Four Cardinal Directions** (*Sì Xiàng*).*
*My crown binds the **Nine Breaths** (*Jiǔ Qì*), my robes weave their essence.*
*The sun is my **Circular Symbol** (*Yuán Xiàng*), the moon my **Circular Light** (*Yuán Guāng*).*
*My body is clad in the **Northern Dipper** (*Běi Dǒu*),*
*with **Six Jia** (*Liù Jiǎ*) and **Nine Chang** (*Jiǔ Zhāng*).*
*Left, I dominate the **River Chief** (*Hé Kuí*),*
*right, I lean on the **Heavenly Cauldron** (*Tiān Gāng*).*
*I can subdue malevolent ghosts,*
*and dispel all ill omens.*
*One decree from the **Divine Ding** (*Shén Dīng*),*
*and the **Yao-Qi** (*yāo-xiè*) vanish.*
*Urgent, as the Law decrees.*

**Next, to the northwest, call upon the **True Martial General** (*Zhēn Wǔ Jiāngjūn*) and recite the incantation:**
*"The **True Martial** (*Zhēn Wǔ*) dwells to the right,*
*the **Black Slayer** (*Hēi Shà*) to the left.*
*The **Supreme Yin** (*Tài Yīn*) generates life,*
*the **Water Position’s** (*Shuǐ Wèi*) refined essence.*
*In perilous emptiness, I ascend in response,*
*the **Tortoise and Serpent** (*Guīshé*) merge in form.*
*I traverse the **Six Harmonies** (*Liù Hé*),*
*commanding all spirits with awe.*
*No hidden realm escapes my gaze,*
*no wish remains unfulfilled.*
*At the end of the **Kālpa** (*Jié*),*
*and its beginning, I sever demonic essences.*
*I rescue and protect all beings,*
*bringing peace to families and nations.*
*Should any minor ghost dare to approach,*
*to witness my form—*
*my gaze alone can topple the **Five Sacred Peaks** (*Wǔ Yuè*).*
*Urgent, as the Law decrees.*

**Next, to the northeast, call upon the **Black Slayer General** (*Hēi Shà Jiāngjūn*) and recite the incantation:**
*"The **Black Slayer** (*Hēi Shà*) of the North,*
*the **Five-Qi Celestial Sovereign** (*Wǔ Qì Tiān Jūn*),*
*my radiance matches the sun and moon,*
*my might secures **Qian** and **Kun**.*
*With **moving talismans** (*Zǒu Fú*) and **spirit-binding records** (*Shè Lù*),*
*I sever all **ghostly gates** (*Guǐmén*).*
*Deploying **spirit-force** (*Xíng Qì*),*
*I repel the **Five Plagues** (*Wǔ Wēn*).*
*The **left and right officers** (*Zuǒyòu Lìshì*) and **Thirty-Five Generals** (*Sān Wǔ Jiāngjūn*),*
*the **Thunder Lord’s** (*Léi Gōng*) **claps** (*Pī Lì*),*
*the **Lightning’s** (*Diàn Zhé*) swift strike,*
*the **Wind’s** (*Fēng Bèn*) relentless charge,*
*blades and axes descend like rain,*
*processions and formations swell like clouds,*
*grasp the **Imperial Bell** (*Dì Zhōng*),*
*and wear the **Kunlun** (*Kūnlún*) upon my head.*
*I march around the world,*
*capturing ghosts and spirits.*
*The **Ninefold Regions’** (*Jiǔ Zhōu*) **community officials** (*Shè Lìng*),*
*the **blood-sacrificed soldiers** (*Xuè Sì Bīng*),*
*shall not dare resist—*
*should any **raise scales** (*Zhāng Líng*).*
*The **Constellation Star** (*Zhèn Xīng*) binds their hands,*
*the **Northern Sovereign** (*Běi Dì*) reclaims their souls,*
*the **Three Palaces** (*Sān Tái*) and **Seven Stars** (*Qī Xīng*),*
*holding blades to sever their bodies.*
*All malevolent **Yao-Qi** (*yāo-líng*),*
*shall not hear my incantation.*
*If they hear my **dispelling spell** (*Miè Zhòu*),*
*they crumble like fine dust.*
*Urgent, as the Law decrees.*

**Next, to the southeast, recite the **Dispelling Defilement Incantation** (*Jiě Huì Zhòu*):
*"Respectfully summoning the **Eastern Sovereign** (*Qīng Dì*), the **Wood Official** (*Mù Guān*),*
*and the **Nine Dispelling Officials** (*Jiě Huì Jūn Lì Jiǔ Rén*).*
*The **Southern Sovereign** (*Chì Dì*), the **Fire Official** (*Huǒ Guān*),*
*and the **Three Dispelling Officials** (*Jiě Huì Jūn Lì Sān Rén*).*
*The **Western Sovereign** (*Bái Dì*), the **Metal Official** (*Jīn Guān*),*
*and the **Seven Dispelling Officials** (*Jiě Huì Jūn Lì Qī Rén*).*
*The **Northern Sovereign** (*Hēi Dì*), the **Water Official** (*Shuǐ Guān*),*
*and the **Five Dispelling Officials** (*Jiě Huì Jūn Lì Wǔ Rén*).*
*The **Central Sovereign** (*Huáng Dì*), the **Earth Official** (*Tǔ Guān*),*
*and the **Twelve Dispelling Officials** (*Jiě Huì Jūn Lì Shí Èr Rén*).*
*The **Celestial Rectifying Talismans’** (*Tiān Shàng Zhí Fú*) **Dispelling Officials** (*Jiě Huì Jūn Lì*),*
*and the **Earthly Rectifying Talismans’** (*Dì Xià Zhí Fú*) **Dispelling Officials** (*Jiě Huì Jūn Lì*),*
*this year, this month, this day, this hour,*
*the **Rectifying Talismans’** (*Zhí Fú*) **Dispelling Officials** (*Jiě Huì Jūn Lì*),*
*and the **boy acolytes** (*Tóngzǐ*) and **maiden attendants** (*Yùnǚ*),*
*each numbering a hundred and twenty,*
*now assemble in full rank,*
*descending to this altar,*
*to dispel all **Heavenly Displeasure** (*Tiān Yàn*) and **Earthly Defilement** (*Dì Huì*),*
*all **human displeasure** (*Rén Yàn*) and **ghostly defilement** (*Guǐ Huì*),*
*and the unclean **Six Livestock** (*Liù Chù*) and **beasts, insects, and vermin** (*Qín Chóng*).*
*Breaking the **Defilement-Phoenix** (*Huì Fènghuáng*) from front to back,*
*from east to west,*
*one by one, I dispel all uncleanness,*
*revealing purity unseen.*
*None may linger or halt.*
*Urgent, as the Law decrees.*

**Next, face east while standing in the west, and call upon the **Green Sovereign** (*Qīng Dì Jūn*), reciting the eastern incantation:**
*"The **Five Sovereigns** (*Wǔ Dì*) and **Five Spirits** (*Wǔ Líng*),*
*the **Five Elders** (*Wǔ Lǎo*),*
*protect the nation and cultivate the Dao/Way.*
*The incantation comes from the **Divine Cauldron Scripture** (*Dòngyuān Shénzhòu Jīng*)—*
*the **‘Eliminating Disasters’** (*Xiāo Zāi*) section.*
*The **Primordial Essence** (*Yuán Jīng*) mingles in chaos,*
*the **Green-Qi** (*Qīng Qì*) disperses and divides.*
*The **Twelve Divine Boys** (*Shén Tóng Shí Èr*) guard and steady the **liver and soul** (*Gān Hún*).*
*The **Two Seven Four Five** (*Èr Qī Sì Wǔ*) shift and transform the **cloudly camp** (*Yún Yíng*).*
*The **Nine Stoves** (*Jiǔ Zào*) and **Nine Communities** (*Jiǔ Shè*),*
*the **Elder Trees** (*Lǎo Mù*) unrefined.*
*The **Divine Tiger** (*Shén Hǔ*) spews poison,*
*the **sword** (*Jiàn*) hurls fire to consume.*
*I sweep away the **Green Plague** (*Qīng Zhèng*),*
*and illuminate the **Yao-Qi** (*yāo-fēn*)’s lurking forms.*
*Recognizing the **true spirit** (*Shén Zhēn*),*
*I safeguard the **Celestial Sovereign** (*Dì Jūn*).*
*Urgent, as the **Eastern Nine-Qi Celestial Sovereign** (*Dōng Fāng Jiǔ Qì Tiān Jūn*) decrees.*

**Next, face south while standing in the north, and call upon the **Red Sovereign** (*Chì Dì Jūn*), reciting the incantation:**
*"The **Red Brightness** (*Chì Míng*) unfolds its diagram,*
*the **Flame Essence** (*Yán Jīng*) fans its gusts.*
*The **Three Divine Boys** (*Sān Shén Tóng*) dwell in one abode,*
*their radiance blazes, floating and drifting.*
*They oversee all **brightness and loss** (*Míng Shī*),*
*and all **Sovereigns** (*Wàn Dì*) bow in reverence.*
*The **Vermilion Phoenix** (*Zhū Fèng*) spews fire,*
*the **gold and stone** (*Jīn Shí*) melt and dissolve.*
*The **flowing bells** (*Liú Líng*) and **flying lightning** (*Fēi Diàn*)*
*truly command the **ten thousand Red Demons** (*Wàn Chì Yāo*).*
*I bind and restrain the **Nine Vile Ones** (*Jiǔ Chǒu*),*
*and cover them in ash, burning them to cinders.*
*I purify the **Imperial Lineage** (*Huáng Zuò*),*
*and the **Dao/Way and Virtue** (*Dào Dé*) wander freely.*
*Urgent, as the **Southern Three-Qi Celestial Sovereign** (*Nán Fāng Sān Qì Tiān Jūn*) decrees.*

**Next, face west while standing in the east, and call upon the **White Sovereign** (*Bái Dì Jūn*), reciting the incantation:**
*"The **Metal Essence** (*Jīn Jīng*) radiates its brilliance,*
*the **Great White** (*Tài Bái*) divides in the west.*
*The **Sovereign’s** (*Dì Jūn*) **sacred talisman** (*Líng Fú*) drifts,*
*carried by **pure clouds** (*Sù Yún*).*
*I summon the **Dragon** (*Lóng*) to bear water,*
*and slay the **radiant smoke** (*Hè Yān*).*
*Long-toothed beasts,*
*hunting and capturing the **brutal horde** (*Xióng Qún*).*"*

*«The **Soul’s Vital Essence** (*Pò Líng*) is settled and tranquil,
I attain **the Way’s natural harmony** (*Dào Zìrán*).

**Urgent, as the **Western Seven-Qi Celestial Sovereign** (*Xī Fāng Qī Zhì Tiān Jūn*) decrees.**

**Next, face north while standing in the south, and call upon the **Qi Sovereign** (*Qì Dì Jūn*), reciting the incantation:**

*"The **Primordial Radiance** (*Yuán Guāng*) descends in splendor,
The **Five Qi** (*Wǔ Qì*) flow and course.
The **Double Gates of the Supreme Sovereign** (*Shuāng Què Shàng Dì*) manifest,
Ten thousand **spirits/numina** (*Wàn Shén*) transform and arise.
I steady my resolve and guard my wisdom,
And consume the **Flame Essence** (*Yán Jīng*).
The **Azure Dragon** (*Cāng Lóng*) spews lightning,
Crushing and shattering the **demonic forces** (*Mó Bīng*).
The **radiant barbarian** (*Hào Hú*) vanquishes all with crystal-sharp blade,
Hurling **flaming talismans** (*Huǒ Líng*) in flight.
The **Three-Heavenly Powerful Ones** (*Sān Tiān Lì Shì*) seize and extinguish the **ten thousand essences** (*Wàn Jīng*).

I safeguard the family and bring peace to the realm,
**The Dao/Way** (*Dào*) governs and ascends to **serenity** (*Shēng Píng*).
**Urgent, as the **Northern Five-Qi Celestial Sovereign** (*Běi Fāng Wǔ Qì Tiān Jūn*) decrees.**

**Next, face south while standing in the center, and call upon the **Yellow Sovereign** (*Huáng Dì Jūn*), reciting the incantation:**

*"Chaos and the Primordial One** (*Hùn Dùn Yuán Yī*) merge,*
The **Yellow Qi** (*Huáng Qì*) intertwines in motion.
I awaken the **True Elder** (*Zhēn Lǎo*),*
And transform like the **Infant of Change** (*Yīng’ér*).
I nourish and cultivate the **Primordial Qi** (*Yuán Qì*),*
And sustain the **Two Principles** (*Liǎng Yī*) within the womb.
The **Sun and Moon** (*Rì Yuè*) ascend in splendor,*
The **stars and constellations** (*Xīng Chén*) descend in order.
The **winds and fires** (*Fēng Huǒ*) clash in battle,*
Lances and blades cross in combat.
The **Six-Heavenly and Nine Brutal Ones** (*Liù Tiān Jiǔ Chǒu*) are dispelled,
Their **rebellious hearts** (*Xīn Lí*) shattered.
The **Supreme Celestial Talisman** (*Tài Shàng Fú*) commands—
How dare they not obey?

All beings find **tranquil ease** (*Ān Lè*),*
Those who enter the **Way** (*Dào*) know **non-action** (*Wú Wéi*).
**Urgent, as the **Central One-Qi Sovereign** (*Zhōng Yāng Yī Qì Tiān Jūn*) decrees.**

**Next, I elevate the **Celestial Venerable** (*Tiān Zūn*)’s command to my body.**
If **transferred or removed** (*Ruò Qiān Bá*),*
I may **shave the priest’s sleeves** (*Duó Fǎ Shī Xiù Jiàn*) and store my **spirit** (*Shén*),*
Gazing toward the **fasting officials** (*Zhāi Guān*).
The **spitting-water incantation** (*Wǎn Shuǐ Zhòu*) is spoken:

*"Water has no fixed form,
Yet with the incantation, it is defined.
In my hands, it is named **Divine Water** (*Shén Shuǐ*).
Spit to clear the heavens,
Spit to bring eternal peace to the earth,
Spit to grant longevity to mortals,
Spit to annihilate the **ghostly forms** (*Guǐ Xíng*).
The first spit like frost,
The second spit like snow,
After the third spit—
All **malevolent influences** (*Wàn Xié*) are severed.

**Ghosts and specters** (*Guǐ Mèi*) retreat in hiding,
**Calamities and disasters** (*Zāi Yāng*) vanish utterly.
The **Southern Dipper** (*Nán Dǒu*) ascends in life,
Its **lifespan** (*Shòu*) like the **Sun and Moon** (*Rì Yuè*).
**Urgent, as the command decrees.**

Next, I recite the **command-to-body incantation** (*Chì Shēn Zhòu*),*
Visualizing my **disciples’ spirits** (*Dì Zǐ Shēn*)*
And their **spirit-forms** (*Shén Zhuàng*)*
Each guarding their **palaces** (*Guān Shì*).

For those who wish to **pay homage to the True and worship the Holy** (*Cháo Zhēn Yè Shèng*),*
First, they must **purify themselves and dissolve defilements** (*Jiě Huì Jìng Shēn*),*
So that **form and qi** (*Xíng Qì*) may be **cleansed and tranquil** (*Sù Qīng*),*
And **heaven and humanity** (*Tiān Rén*) may be **moved and harmonized** (*Gǎn Gé*).

The **fasting officials** (*Zhāi Guān*) of such-and-such rank,
The **Five True Officials** (*Wǔ Zhēn Guān*) within my body—
The **liver, lungs, heart, spleen, kidneys** (*Gān Fèi Xīn Pí Shèn*),*
The **six viscera and twelve bowels** (*Liù Zàng Shí Èr Fǔ*),*
The **seven stars and nine palaces** (*Qī Zhèng Jiǔ Guōng*),*
The **twelve spirit-forms** (*Shí Èr Shén Shì*),*
The **four limbs and five members** (*Sì Zhī Wǔ Tǐ*),*
**Tendons, bones, marrow, and brain** (*Jīn Gǔ Suǐ Nǎo*),*
**Skin, flesh, blood, and vessels** (*Pí Fū Xuè Mài*),*
The **nine orifices and twelve meridians** (*Jiǔ Qiào Róng Wèi*),*
The **one hundred and eighty spirit-passages** (*Bǎi Bā Shí Jīng Guān*),*
The **three hundred and sixty bone-joints** (*Sān Bǎi Liù Shí Gǔ Jié*),*
The **one thousand two hundred shadows** (*Qiān Èr Bǎi Xíng Yǐng*),*
The **ten thousand two thousand luminous essences** (*Wàn Èr Qiān Jīng Guāng*),*
The **left Three Souls** (*Zuǒ Sān Hún*),*
The **right Seven Spirits** (*Yòu Qī Pò*),*
The **three divisions and eight vistas** (*Sān Bù Bā Jǐng*),*
And the **twenty-four spirits** (*Èr Shí Sì Shén*).

I am a **child of the Supreme Celestial** (*Tài Shàng Zhǐ*),*
A **grandchild of the Primordial Sovereign** (*Yuán Huáng Sūn*).
My head is crowned by the **Vermilion Bird** (*Zhū Què*),*
My feet tread upon the **Dark Warrior** (*Xuán Wǔ*).
To my left, the **Green Dragon** (*Qīng Lóng*) attends,
To my right, the **White Tiger** (*Bái Hǔ*) abides.
The **Green Dragon** (*Qīng Lóng*) supports and escorts me forward,
The **White Tiger** (*Bái Hǔ*) supports and sends me back.
The **Vermilion Bird** (*Zhū Què*) guides ahead, bearing **standard and banner** (*Zhuàng Fān Fān*),
The **Dark Warrior** (*Xuán Wǔ*) follows behind, carrying **bell and drum** (*Zhōng Gǔ*).
Thus, the **fasting official** (*Zhāi Zhǔ*)’s heart is free from **malevolence** (*Xié*),*
The **liver** (*Gān*) is free from **illness** (*Bìng*),*
The **lungs** (*Fèi*) are free from **deceit** (*Jiān*),*
The **kidneys** (*Shèn*) are free from **obscurity** (*Hūn*),*
The **spleen** (*Pí*) is free from **premature death** (*Sǐ*),*
The **gallbladder** (*Dǎn*) is free from **fear** (*Bù*),*
The **stomach** (*Wèi*) is free from **filth** (*Huì*).

My body is **pure and cleansed** (*Yī Shēn Qīng Jìng*),*
No **malevolent influences** (*Wàn Xié*) may touch it.
The **officials and soldiers** (*Lì Shēn*) lead and guide,
The **Five Spirits** (*Wǔ Shén*) attend at my side.
**Urgent, as the command decrees.*»

Next, recite the *Huángtíng Jīng* **Five Viscera Incantation** to rescue the fasting official’s body within:
The **heart spirit**, *Dān Yuán Shǒu Língjūn*;
The **lung spirit**, *Hào Huá Xūchéng Jūn*;
The **liver spirit**, *Lóng Yān Hán Míng Jūn*;
The **kidney spirit**, *Xuán Míng Yù Yīng Jūn*;
The **spleen spirit**, *Cháng Zài Hún Tíng Jūn*;
The **gallbladder spirit**, *Lóng Yào Wēi Míng Jūn*.

The **Twelve True Persons of the High Tower** govern the **spirits, bodies, and essences** of the Five Viscera and Six Fu.
All dwell within the heart, circulating the **Celestial Canons**—preserved day and night for eternal life.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

Next, recite the *Huángtíng* **Facial Region Incantation** to rescue the fasting official’s body within:
The **hair spirit**, *Cāng Huá Tài Yuán Jūn*;
The **brain spirit**, *Jīng Gēn Ní Huán Jūn*;
The **eye spirit**, *Míng Shàng Yīng Xuán Jūn*;
The **nose spirit**, *Yù Lǒng Líng Jiān Jūn*;
The **ear spirit**, *Kōng Xián Yōu Tián Jūn*;
The **tongue spirit**, *Tōng Mìng Zhèng Lún Jūn*;
The **tooth spirit**, *Zhuó Fēng Luó Qiān Jūn*.

The spirits of the face guard one another,
Retrieving the soul and returning the *pò* to eternal stability.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

Next, recite the **Northern Dipper Grand Officer’s Disaster-Dispelling Incantation**, placing the Northern Dipper upon the fasting official’s head, visualizing the *Kuí* star at the crown, its handle pointing forward.

The **Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper**, the **Great Gods of Heaven’s Center**,
Above, they attend the **Golden Gate of the Celestial Court**,
Below, they shelter **Kūnlún Mountain**.
They regulate the **cosmic order** and command the **Heaven and Earth**.
*Tān Láng* and *Jù Mén* store blessings in *Wén Qǔ*,
*Lián Zhēn* and *Wǔ Qū* assist with *Pò Jūn*’s destruction.
*Dà Tóng Shā Jiè* penetrates to the finest dust.
What disaster cannot be extinguished? What blessing cannot be attained?
The **Primordial Sovereign’s Pure Qi** descends to cover the disciple’s body.
The **Heavenly Ganges** points day and night in its great wheel.
Those of low station, seeking the Dao for its mysteries,
Ever behold the honored forms—grant eternal life.
**Most High Jade Emperor, Purple Micro Emperor**,
Protect the disciple in this world, granting perpetual peace.

*Three Platforms, Three Platforms*, give birth to the disciple.
*Three Platforms, Three Platforms*, nourish the disciple.
*Three Platforms, Three Platforms*, shield the disciple.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

May the fasting official, after purification,
Have **unobstructed qi and clear spirit**, with **settled soul and unrestrained *pò***.
The **Hundred Passes** are cleansed, the **Flower Pool** overflows,
All **leaks** vanish, the **Cinnabar Field** radiates.
Prosperous and harmonious with Heaven’s blessings,
Hidden afflictions of the world are dispelled—
All undertakings are auspicious, all actions succeed.
I bow and take refuge in the **Boundless Great Dao**.

Next, brandish the sword and march to the **southwest corner**, reciting the **Incantation to Seal a Hundred Monsters’ Mouths and Tongues**.

*Six Jia, Nine Chapters*, Heaven round, Earth square.
The **Four Seasons and Five Phases**, Sun and Moon as light.
*Ayú’s Step* aligns with the Dao, *Chīyóu* repels armies.
The **Green Dragon** clutches my axle, the **White Tiger** supports my stride.
*Yīng Huò* leads ahead, dispelling all inauspiciousness.
The **Northern Dipper** slays evil, annihilating calamity.
The **Five Spirits** guard as I traverse the four quarters.
Left *Shè*, right *Jì*—bind them with my bells.
Ten thousand mouths, ten thousand tongues,
Evil men, evil ghosts, tigers, wolves, thieves, and robbers—
Sealed, suppressed, and hidden away.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

Next, proceed to the **northwest** and recite the **Ayú’s Step Eight Trigrams Incantation**, drawing forth the **Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl**. Reflect on the **Four Spirits**, then chant the incantation while stepping in *Ayú’s Step*.

The **Three Steps, Nine Traces** are thus:
Right foot eight, right foot six, right foot two—*right couple*;
Left foot seven, right foot four, left foot one;
Left foot nine, left foot five, left foot three—*left odd*.

*Qián* is exalted, *Kūn* is yielding within.
The **Two Principles** harmonize, the **Six Extremes** bring prosperity.
Aligned with Heaven, enjoying Earth, eternal peace and purity.
Responding to the **Primordial Yellow**, upper garments and lower robes.
*Zhèn* ascends, *Gèn* flourishes, *Kǎn* is abundant, *Lí* is bright.
*Xùn* thrives, *Duì* generates—**Tiger’s Step, Dragon’s Stride**.
*Yáng*’s foundation is thus *Qián* and *Kūn*, *Gèn* and *Xùn*—
**Tiger’s Step, Dragon’s Stride**.
*Zhèn*, *Lí*, *Kǎn*, *Duì*—their wings assist and uphold.
*Dù Běn* and *Zhāng Běn* thus: Heaven’s Gate, Earth’s Door,
Human Gate, Ghost Gate—who serves me?
**Boundless Heaven, Profound Azure**.
Today’s *Ayú’s Step* aligns with the **Heavenly Ganges**,
Ghosts and spirits submit; below, all inauspiciousness is repelled.
All petitions are granted, ten thousand spirits dare not resist.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

Next, establish the **boundary**, chanting the incantation while stepping the **Nine-Step Ding**. From the **northwest**, step to the **northeast**, facing east and spitting water.
Respectfully summon the **Eastern Green Boy Lord** and his officials and soldiers,
*—Dù Běn*—with **nine million men** riding the **true qi of the Eastern Year Star**, descending from the void to the altar site, deploying spirit and qi, searching out malevolent essences, driving away ghosts and demons—**no mercy for the guilty**.
I proceed from the **northern corner** to establish the boundary, reaching the **southeast**.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*
*—Dù Běn*—: Descending to the altar below, I proceed from the **northeast corner** to establish the boundary, reaching the **southeast** to deploy spirit and qi, and so on.
*—Zhāng Běn*— follows *Yáng Běn*, except for the **southeast corner**, where it adds:
*"All impurities, motionless and inactive."*

Next, chant the incantation, stepping the **Ding Step** to the **southeast**, facing south and spitting water.
Respectfully summon the **Southern Red Boy Lord** and his officials and soldiers,
Riding the **true qi of the Southern *Yīng Huò* Star**, descending from the void to the altar site, deploying spirit and qi, searching out malevolent essences, **burning ghosts and demons**—**no mercy for the guilty**.
I proceed from the **southeast corner** to establish the boundary, reaching the **southwest**.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

Next, chant the incantation, stepping the **Ding Step** to the **southwest**, facing west and spitting water.
Respectfully summon the **Western White Boy Lord** and his officials and soldiers,
Riding the **true qi of the Western *Tài Bái* Star**, descending from the void to the altar site, deploying spirit and qi, searching out malevolent essences, **slaying and beheading ghosts and demons**—**no mercy for the guilty**.
I proceed from the **southwest corner** to establish the boundary, reaching the **northwest**.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

Next, chant the incantation, stepping the **Ding Step** to the **northwest corner**, facing north and spitting water.
Respectfully summon the **Northern Black Boy Lord** and his officials and soldiers,
Riding the **true qi of the Northern *Chén* Star**, descending from the void to the altar site, deploying spirit and qi, searching out malevolent essences, **drifting away ghosts and demons**—**no mercy for the guilty**.
I proceed from the **northwest corner** to establish the boundary, reaching the **northeast**.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

Next, chant the incantation, stepping the **Ding Step** to the center of the altar, facing the **northwest** and spitting water.
Respectfully summon the **Central Yellow Boy Lord** and his officials and soldiers,
Riding the **true qi of the Central *Zhèn* Star**, descending from the void to the altar site, deploying spirit and qi, searching out malevolent essences, **burying and concealing ghosts and demons**—**no mercy for the guilty**.
I proceed from the **upper boundary** to establish the boundary, reaching the altar site.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

Next, stand at the earthly door and ascend the Seven Stars of the Dipper, facing the *jiàn* (建) and *pò* (破) directions—
that is, in the first month when *jiàn* is in the *yín* (寅) direction, turn your back to *yín* and step upon the first star.
Turn your body to enter the Dipper’s enclosure, visualizing the Celestial Official, the Sun and Moon, and the Five Peaks and Four Legions of Soldiers arrayed before you,
while the Four Spirits align in order at your left, right, front, and rear.

Then chant the incantation of the **Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper Lords**:

*"O radiant Seven Stars, the Dipper’s handle shines bright.
Acquisitive Wolf wields evil, devouring Ghost consumes essence.
Mighty Gate blazes red, illuminating the dawn’s light.
Luck Store gallops swift, commanding celestial armies.
Scarlet Trumpet’s grace, its brilliance pierces the Pure and Chaste.
Majestic Threat looms, the True Person’s guiding star.
The Heavenly Marshal commands—Break Army Star Lord, seal the Four Gates,
and let turbid *qi* surge forth.
Ever wielding axe and halberd, seizing Heaven’s *Dīng* (丁),
a single shout to the south—terror strikes, hearts shatter.
Summon the Patrol Inspector, heed the voices sought,
the Nine Regions’ community officers—none escape uncalled by name.
Slay the wicked, punish the guilty—no crime is light.
The rebellious perish, the merciful live on.
Heads severed, limbs chopped, bodies crushed to dust—
demons and monsters purged, humanity at peace.
Healing sickness, banishing malevolence—
by imperial decree, this is to be carried out.
*Urgent, as the command decrees."*

「Next, the invocation of officials by rank.
With all ranks now humbly petitioning, I respectfully request this below for the construction of a grand ritual hall (*dàzhāi*) for my family, following the prescribed rites.

Conveniently, as the patrol progresses to the Ghost Gate (*guǐmén*), I humbly invoke:
- **Heavenly Immortal** armies and cavalry (*tiānxiān bīngmǎ*),
- **Earthly Immortal** armies and cavalry (*dìxiān bīngmǎ*),
- **Flying Immortal** armies and cavalry (*fēixiān bīngmǎ*),
- **True Person** (*Zhēnrén*) armies and cavalry,
- **Sun and Moon, Star Host** (*rìyuè xīngxiù*) armies and cavalry,
- **Nine Palaces, Five Emperors** (*jiǔgōng wǔdì*) armies and cavalry,
- **Three Rivers, Four Seas** (*sānhé sìhǎi*) forces,
- **Five Mountains, Four Great Waterways** (*wǔyuè sìdú*) armies and cavalry—
each is respectfully summoned in full array, to proceed in orderly succession to the ritual platform (*tánchǎng*).

Circumambulate the platform three times, first observing its breadth and narrowness, then reciting the incantation (*niàn zhou*).

At each invocation of full array, when the feet reach the Ghost Gate, strike the earth with the sword’s tip, then turn left three times.

Cover the platform threefold:
- Above, deploy the **Heavenly Net** (*tiānluó*), drawing seven strokes horizontally,
- Below, spread the **Earthly Net** (*dìwǎng*), drawing seven strokes vertically.

All fallen corpses and lingering *qi*, earthly and wooden spirits (*tǔmù bǎi jīng*), those who obstruct the Dao—
collect and consign them beneath the **Pole Star Marshal** (*kuígāng*), descending into the earth ten thousand *zhang*, motionless and inert.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

Write the **Ghost Character** (*guǐzì*), plant the sword at the Ghost’s Heart, and spray water while reciting the incantation:
*"The Five Phases (*wǔxíng*) mutually propel, the Pole Star Marshal holds supreme authority.
The Six Celestial Periods (*liùjì*) aid me, the Three Sovereigns (*sāntái*) banish the unrighteous.
Heaven revolves, Earth turns—yin and yang [?] open.
Eternal life transcends the world, Sun and Moon shine together.
*Urgent, as the command decrees."*

Heaven’s amnesty shines resplendently, Earth’s amnesty extends squarely.
With the **Yú Steps** (*yǔbù*) performed, all ghosts submit in hiding.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

Spray water and chant the **Summoning Incantation** (*shè*), then turn right, circling the body while exiting the **Fighting Formation** (*dǒu*), avoiding the **Star Host’s Ranks** (*xīngxiù jīngyīn*) and the **Pole Star Seal** (*tīngyìn*), and recite:
*"All malevolent and impure forces—
motionless and inert, strike the teeth three times, then return to their positions.
Turn right and draw the Ghost Character, overlapping it repeatedly—
this is called the **Seal of All Malevolent Impurities** (*shōu yīqiè xiéjì yìn*)."*

**Du Tianxiān’s (杜天师) Sword-Killing Incantation**
By the **Supreme Emperor’s** (*Tàishàng*) decree, I universally proclaim to all spirits (*wànlíng*).
Hurry the **Heavenly True Ones** (*tiānzhēn*), all convene at the Imperial Court (*dìtíng*).
With a single command, the **Double Sovereigns** (*shuānghuáng*) descend, their essence refined.
Overseeing and inspecting, repelling evil, regulating *qi*, and summoning life.

If any omen is unauspicious, testing the divine—
the Seven Gods (*qīshén*) wield their axes, the **Heavenly Thunderbolt** (*tiānfēng*) strikes rightward.
Brandishing the sword to lead the charge, hurling the **Fire Bell** (*huǒlíng*), summoning the **Divine Armor** (*jiàmìng jiǎzhōu*), and the **Tiger Soldiers** (*hǔzú tiāndīng*).
Wind and fire wage battle together, slaying evil and binding spirits.
Above, they threaten the Six Heavens (*liùtiān*), below, they subdue demonic spirits (*móolíng*).
Once demonic spirits are subdued, all ten thousand malevolent forces perish—
lances strike, lightning sweeps, no wicked demon survives.

The **Former Emperor** (*xiānhuáng*) established the decree—
who dares defy it? Those who resist the decree shall be exterminated.
Each must respect and be cautious, safeguarding this **Yellow Peace** (*huángníng*).
The Nine Heavens decree, all spirits heed.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

**Deploy the Endless Golden Talisman Rite (*wújìn jīnluó yí*) to Subdue the Sword-Killing Incantation** (*zhōngjiàn*)
By the **Supreme Emperor’s** decree, I universally proclaim to all spirits.
Command the **Heavenly Generals** (*tiānjiāng*), lead the **Heavenly Soldiers** (*tiāndīng*), strike the **Heavenly Drum** (*fátiāngǔ*), raise the **Heavenly Banners** (*yáng tiānjīng*), brandish the **Golden Star** (*huáng jīnxīng*), hurl the **Fire Bell**, capture the **Shadowless** (*wúyǐng*), search the **Soundless** (*wúshēng*), align at the **Tranquil Stage** (*zhèngtàijiē*), sweep away the **Interfering Bandits** (*sǎochāndiào*), and disperse the **Evil Wind** (*yáng xiéfēng*) at the **Ten Extremes** (*shíjí*), spreading **True *Qi*** (*zhēnqì*) across the **Eight Strings** (*bāxián*).

The **Heavenly True Ones** descend, their威光 ascending pure.
All demons vanish, ten thousand monsters obliterate—
the Nine Heavens proclaim the decree, all spirits obey.
*Urgent, as the command decrees.*

**Yang Zigong’s (杨次公) Imperial Edict to Water for Summoning the White** (*shuǐqǐ bái*)
The **River Chart** (*Hétú*) ascends as an auspicious sign, revealing Heaven’s bright intent.
The **Golden Talisman’s** grand rites (*jīnluó hóngyí*) are established in the sacred age.
I, the subject, humbly emulate the **True Transformation** (*zhēnhuà*), presuming to be a **Ritual Officer** (*zhìguān*).
What I pray for is truly answered—how dare I forget to report my gratitude?
*[My intent is as follows:]* The rest is the same as above.

**Deploy the Endless Summoning Edict** (*zhāng wújìn qǐbái*)
The **Supreme Ultimate** (*Tàijí*) contains the Three (*sānhé*), indistinct and formless.
The **Great Uncarved Block** (*Dàkuài*) breathes forth ten thousand, uneven and disordered.
Numbers come and go—Dao ever rescues.
**Yuan Shi** (*Yuánshǐ*) issued the **Jade Writing** (*yùwén*), **Zǐhuáng** (*Zǐhuáng*) bestowed the **Golden Talisman** (*jīnluó*).
I, the subject, presuming to be a **Ritual Officer**, carry out the **True Teaching** (*zhēnjiào*).
Receiving words to pray and supplicate—how dare I not report them?
*[My intent is as follows:]* The rest is the same as above.

Again...」

**True Riding Descends and Soars Below** (*Zhēnyù xià xiáng*)
The **Dao’s Sovereign** (*Tàijí*) rests the **Divine Wind** (*shénfēng*), calming all into stillness;
The **Fragrant Field** (*xūncháng*) spreads open in the center, sweeping away the **impure qi** (*jìqì*) in its chaotic dispersion.

Ten directions radiate with the **jewel-like clarity** (*yùguāng*) of the void,
The Four Seasons reveal the **serene expanse** (*chéngqīng*) of the heavenly firmament.

How could I allow malevolent forces to persist?
I dare not let them linger unchecked.

I shall summon the **Sword-Wielding Spirit of Water** (*jiànshuǐ shén*) to purify the **ritual grounds** (*táncháng*).

Thus, the **tempestuous miasma** (*biāojǐng*) may recede,
And the **divine inspection** (*jiàn*) descend upon the clear and bright.

**My intent is as follows:** The subjects, how dare we not **refine our form and qi** (*dǎoliàn xíngqì*), **dispel our turbid spirit** (*shūluán jīngshén*), **cleanse impurities and dispel the thick haze** (*jiěhuì chú fēn*), and **invite the True and Descend the Sacred** (*yánzhēn jiàngshèng*)?

The **Grace of the Most High** (*Tàishàng*) is the **New Edict** (*Bùxīn*), the **Heavenly Venerable** (*Tiānzūn*) bestows the **Great Benevolence** (*Zhìdà*).
The **True Teaching** (*Zhēnjiào*) is proclaimed, and **Divine Officers** (*Jiàngguān*) are dispatched to **Descend and Inspect** (*Jiàngjiàn*).
Thus, Heaven remains free of **thick miasmas** (*fēn*), Earth free of **malevolent dust** (*yāochén*).
The **yin mists** (*yīnyǎ*) are dispelled, the **yang light** (*yángguāng*) shines pure and clear;
The **Wind Master** (*Fēngshī*) restrains all movement, so not even the finest specks stir,
The **Luminous Clouds** (*Léimài*) rise to **exalt their brilliance** (*yánghuī*), and **auspicious qi** (*ruìqì*) floats through the sky.

Thus, the **sincere and earnest** (*chéngqūn*) may ascend in prayer,
And the **divine response** (*shén*) will come as if in answer.

The subject, prostrate in thought, **focuses the mind** (*shénniàn*) upon the **True Dao** (*Zhēndào*).
Humbly awaiting the **retribution of response** (*bàoyìng*).

---

**The Source of the Ultimate Dao** (*Zhìdào zhōng*)
Its **hidden mysteries** (*yǐnmiào*) are found in the **formless origin** (*hùn máng shǒu*);
Its **divine virtue** (*shénzhēn*) manifests the **sacred transformation** (*dé*) before the **beginning of creation** (*kāipì zhī qián*).

From this stem the **models for all sovereigns** (*mófàn bǎiwáng*), the **birth of myriad things** (*shēngchéng wànhuì*).
As the **Ancestor of the Void and the Perfect** (*Chōngxū Dàodé*), it **bestows the Eight Auspicious Signs** (*chuí bājǐng*) with **luminous scriptures** (*zhì língwén*);
As the **Heir to the Mysterious Origin of Purity** (*jì xuānyuán qīngjìng*), it **descends the Precious Talismans** (*jiàng sāntiān bǎoluó*) of the **Three Heavens** (*Sāntiān*).

The **Dao** is transmitted through the **Zhèngyī** (正一) lineage,
Its duty lies in **Yángpíng** (阳平) governance,
Thus it aids the **Xuānyuán** (玄元) transmission of the **Teaching** (*jiào*),
The **Celestial Master** (*Tiānshī*) receives it,
And **subdues the perverse** (*shè yé*) to return to the **Way**.

Water is the **first of the Five Phases** (*Wǔxíng*),
And all impurities are removed;
The sword is the **refined strength of a hundred forges** (*Bǎiliàn zhī gāng*),
And no malevolent force (*miǎo* 妖) remains unsevered.
Your servants have long awaited the **hosted blessings** (*sùqìng* 宿庆),
And now follow the **true wind** (*zhēnfēng* 真风).

The **yellow silk** (*Huángsū* 黄素) bears the **flying scriptures** (*fēizhāng* 飞章),
Transmitting the **Precious Talismans** (*bǎoluó* 宝箓) of the **Nine Auspicious Dragons** (*Jiǔfèng pòhuì* 九凤破秽);
The **green thread** (*Qīngsī* 青丝) binds the **sacred knots** (*jiéniǔ* 结纽),
Receiving the **scriptures** (*wén* 文) of the **Ten Heavens** summoning the **Dragon** (*Shí Tiān zhāo Lóng* 十天召龙).

Bound by **conduct** (*xíngchí* 行持) and **pledged to benefit beings** (*jìwù* 济物),
We have accepted the **urgent words** (*lái cí* 来词) with sincerity,
And dare not neglect the **broken oath** (*liè quàn* 裂券) of our **vows**.

Entering the heart, Your servants refine the **water of the Jade Pool** (*Huápí* 华池),
And spread the **great Teaching’s** (*Dàjiào* 大教) **wind** (*fēng* 风).
With reverence, we uphold the **feathered standards** (*yǔyí* 羽仪),
Clearing away the **malevolent qi** (*miǎoqì* 妖氛) that disrupts;
Purifying the **cloud paths** (*yúnlù* 云路), we **forebearingly await** (*qián zhān* 前瞻) the **shattered and solemn** (*suīmù* 碎穆) **form**.

Greatly, the **Highest Dao** (*Dà Yǒu* 大有) and **Most Exalted Truth** (*Gāozhēn* 高真)
The **Ultimate None** (*Tài Wúshàng* 太无上) and **Most Holy Sage** (*Shèngshèng* 上圣)
**Gather the clouds and rainbows** (*guà yún ní* 廓云霓),
And **descend upon the gathered** (*fù jí* 俯集) to **oversee the opening** (*pì Chānghé* 辟阊阖);
They **admonish their appointed officers** (*shēn yōushī* 申饬攸司),
And **purify the sacrificial altars** (*sù qīng tán lǘ* 肃清坛驴),
So that **heaven and humanity may harmonize** (*shù Tiānrén* 庶天人),
And the **profound and manifest may communicate** (*bǐ yōuxiǎn* 俾幽显),
Thus fulfilling the **ordinary expectations** (*shì fù fánqíng* 式副凡情)
And **making clear the Dao of Heaven** (*Kǒngzhāo Tiāndào* 孔昭天道).

Your servants concentrate our **spirit** (*shén* 神) in the **Emerald Deeps** (*Bìluò* 碧落),
And focus our **aspirations** (*zhì* 志) in the **Crimson Expanse** (*Dānxiāo* 丹霄),
Humbling ourselves in **spiritual contemplation** (*sī shén* 思神),
And **reverently awaiting** (*gōngsì* 恭俟) the **radiant response** (*zhāobào* 昭报).

**Newly composed** (*Xīnxiū* 新修).

With deepest reverence, we acknowledge that the **Celestial Chariot** (*Dìchē* 帝车) descends—how could we tolerate any defilement lingering?
Our **inner chambers** remain unemptied; how could external malevolence dare intrude?

We **align with Heaven** (*shì Tiān* 事天) to **nurture our nature** (*yǎngxìng* 养性), and dare to clear the earth as our altar.
Though we profess reverence without exception, we still fear our devotion may fall short.

To **honor the Venerable Ones** (*Chóngzhēn* 崇真), we first **perform the rites of purification** (*jiěhuì* 解秽).
Where the **spiritual incantations** (*shénzhòu* 神咒) are invoked, the **malevolent qi** (*yāofēn* 妖氛) is utterly dispersed.

In accordance with this intent, the subsequent text follows as before.

We dare not fail to **purify our hearts and minds** (*xǐqīng xīndì* 洗清心地) and establish an altar **akin to the Sovereign’s** (*lèidì* 类帝).
We **cleanse and refine** (*quánjié* 蠲洁) the ritual implements, and **properly display** (*shìzhǎn* 式展) the rites to Heaven.

We greatly fear that **malevolent dust** (*yāochén* 妖尘) may obstruct, making it difficult to approach the **sudden divine descent** (*biāoxū* 飙欻).
With deepest humility, we pray that the **Most High** (*Tàishàng* 太上) may **reiterate commands** (*shēnchì* 申敕) to the **thousand officials** and **warn** (*jiéyán* 戒严) the **ten thousand cavalry**.

Let the **four boundaries be cleared** (*guòqīng sìjiè* 廓清四界), and the **auspicious formations** (*sēnzǎo* 森藻) stand guard at the **fragrant ritual grounds** (*xūncáng* 熏场).
Let the **exorcisms** (*zhènfú* 振祓) subdue the **malevolent forces** (*tánxiōng* 覃凶), and the **divine winds** (*biāo* 飙) descend upon the **embroidered seat** (*fǔzuò* 黼座).

May the **howling winds, rain, and thunder** (*língyǔzhènfēng* 凌雨震风) cease at dawn and dusk,
And may we behold the **auspicious stars and luminous sun** (*jǐngxīngruìrì* 景星瑞日) in darkness and light.
Thus may **flourishing virtue** (*màoduì* 茂对) answer to **manifest authority** (*míngwēi* 明威),
And may our **ritual endeavors** (*lící* 厘事) be fulfilled.

We, your servants, **direct our hearts to the Crimson Steps** (*Dān Bì* 丹陛),
And **still our breath at the Purple Altar** (*Zǐ Tán* 紫坛),
Humbling ourselves in **spiritual contemplation** (*sī shén* 思神),
And **reverently awaiting** (*gōngsì* 恭俟) the **radiant response** (*zhāobào* 昭报).

**The Daoist Canon’s Universal Teachings** (*Dàomén Tōngjiào* 道门通教) must employ **Volume Seven** (*Jíjuàn zhī qī* 集卷之七竟) and **Volume Eight** (*Jíjuàn zhī bā* 集卷之八).

**The Daoist Master Lü Taigu of Hèlín’s Collection**
**Chapter on Ritual Dignity**
**Yellow Talisman Nine-Hour Invocation Scripture**
**First Hour**
*With this first recitation today,*
We **divine auspicious omens for the realm** and **pray for the sovereign’s eternal life.**

**Gathered Daoists ascend the altar**, holding in mind the **Celestial Worthy’s sacred name**,
And **recite in rotation** the *Supreme Daoist Classic of the Primordial Origin and Supreme Virtue: The Dao and Its Power*,
**The True Scripture of the Yellow Emperor**.

For this Scripture—
From the **Five Phases’ inception**, before **Heaven and Earth were divided**,
When **spiritual winds gathered in mystery** and **void and substance congealed in brilliance**,
When **precious texts formed in the Primordial Mixture** and **jade characters emerged from Solitary Transformation**,
When it **stood forth in the depths of obscurity** and **shone before the Dark and Yellow**,
The sun and moon **received it to illuminate**, and **Heaven and Earth relied upon it to move**.

Thus, the **Emperor of the Void** commanded **Lord of the Primordial Beginning** to
**Inscribe it upon jade tablets**, **compile it in jade slips**,
**Store it in a treasure chest**, **gather it in a jade terrace**,
**First concealing it in the Upper Primordial**, then **flowing it to the lower lands**,
**Descending to enlighten the virtuous**, and **bestowing this culture**.

**Fu Xi received the Spiritual Diagram**, **Huangdi received the Symbolic Talisman**,
**Emperor Shao received the Sacred Edicts**, **Yu the Great received the Luo Book**.
Thus, **the Dao’s teachings were established**, and **cultural texts descended from this moment**.

When the **Primordial Origin descended as Sage**,
And **served as imperial preceptor**,
Yet **the Great Dao was not practiced**, and **human morals grew corrupt**,
He **proclaimed the Five-Thousand-Word Doctrine of Dao and Virtue**,
To **restore the source of purity and simplicity**.

Its words—
**Boundless yet encompassing all**, **minute yet including all**,
**Exhausting all mysteries in principle**, **harmonizing with the Void in meaning**,
**Internally governing the body**, **externally ordering the state**,
When **studied, resonate with the Supreme Ultimate**,
When **practiced, bring peace and prosperity to the land**,
**As the ancestral root of all things**, **the origin of Heaven and Earth**.

This Scripture’s **sublime excellence** is **beyond full praise**,
Yet we **assemble these extraordinary merits** in reverence,
And **pray for the longevity of the present Emperor**.

May the **Sovereign’s person be at ease and flourishing**,
May **years match the celestial poles** in length,
May **Heaven’s writ descend** and **great undertakings prosper**,
May **imperial reigns extend** and **the nation’s foundations deepen**,
May **weapons rest** and **the world be tranquil**,
May **pure customs revive** and **the age of peace prevail**,
May **rains be timely and winds harmonious**, **wealth abundant for families and state**.

All **sentient beings** shall **align with the Dao’s truth**,
And **distant lands and remote regions** shall **return to the Right Path**.

«We now rely upon the **Pure and Numerous** [清眾 *Qīngzhòng*],
Each **invoking sincerity** [各運誠心 *gè yùn chéngxīn*],
First **reciting the incantations** [先持誦 *xiān chí sòng*] of the **Pure Heaven and Earth Deities** [净天地神 *Jìng Tiāndì Shén*],
The **Pure Heaven and Earth Incantation** [净心口神 *Jìng Xīnkǒu Shén*],
And the **Incantation for Peace of the Land Deities** [安土地神 *Ān Tǔdì Shén*].

We invoke the **Jade Purity Primordial Sovereign Lord** [玉清元始天尊 *Yùqīng Yuánshǐ Tiānzūn*],
The **Supreme Purity Lord of the Spirit Treasure** [上清靈寶天尊 *Shàngqīng Língbǎo Tiānzūn*],
The **Great Purity Sovereign Lord of Descending Life** [太清降生天尊 *Tàiqīng Jiàngshēng Tiānzūn*],
The **Supreme Jade Emperor of the Celestial Vault** [昊天玉皇上帝 *Hàotiān Yùhuáng Dàdì*],
The **Great Sovereign Emperor of the Upper Palace** [上宮天皇大帝 *Shànggōng Tiānhuáng Dàdì*],
The **Sovereign Emperor of the Northern Dipper of the Middle Heaven** [中天北極天帝 *Zhōngtiān Běijí Tiāndì*],
The **August Earth Deity of the Later Soil** [後土皇地祇 *Hòutǔ Huángdìzhǐ*],
The **Jade Purity Sovereign Lord of the Void** [玉清虛無天尊 *Yùqīng Xūwú Tiānzūn*],
The **Jade Purity Sovereign Lord of Great Compassion** [玉清大慈天尊 *Yùqīng Dàcí Tiānzūn*],
The **Jade Purity Sovereign Lord of Great Mercy** [玉清大悲天尊 *Yùqīng Dàtī Tiānzūn*],
The **Jade Purity Sovereign Lord of the Great Emperor and the Void** [玉清大帝虛皇天尊 *Yùqīng Dàdì Xūhuáng Tiānzūn*],
The **Jade Purity Sovereign Lord of the Later Sage of the Golden Gate** [玉清後聖金闕天尊 *Yùqīng Hòushèng Jīnkuàng Tiānzūn*],
The **Jade Purity Sovereign Lord of the Later Sage of the Azure Gate** [玉清後聖琼玉闕天尊 *Yùqīng Hòushèng Qióngkuàng Tiānzūn*],
The **Jade Purity Sovereign Lord of the Later Sage of Great Peace** [玉清後聖太平天尊 *Yùqīng Hòushèng Tàipíng Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of Great Peace and Protection of the Realm** [太平護國天尊 *Tàipíng Hùguó Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of Prospering the Realm and Transforming the People** [昌國化人天尊 *Chāngguó Huàrén Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of Perfecting the Realm and Land** [成就國土天尊 *Chéngjiù Guótǔ Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of Great Peace and Prospering the Realm** [興國太平天尊 *Xīngguó Tàipíng Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of the Mysterious Capital and Ten Thousand Longevities** [玄都萬壽天尊 *Xuándōu Wànshòu Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of Preserving the System and Managing the Eon** [保制劫運天尊 *Bǎozhì Jièyùn Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of the Inconceivable Sacred Virtue** [難思聖德天尊 *Nánsī Shèngdé Tiānzūn*],
The **True Person of the Ocean-Space Wisdom** [海空智藏真人 *Hǎikōng Zhìcáng Zhēnrén*],
And the **True Person of the Universal Virtue and Marvelous Conduct** [溥德妙行真人 *Pǔdé Miàoxíng Zhēnrén*],
Whose **inconceivable merits** [不可思議功德 *Bùkě Sīyì Gōngdé*] are profound.

Next, we **each recite** [各轉 *gè zhuàn*] the **Scripture of the Supreme Virtue of the Mixed Primordial Emperor** [《混元上德皇帝道德真經》 *Hùnyuán Shàngdé Huángdì Dàodé Zhēnjīng*].

In the **second recitation** [第二時 *dì èr shí*],
We now **recite this third time** [以今第三遍 *yǐ jīn dì sān biàn*],
To **bestow celestial blessings** [正天分度 *zhèngtiān fēndù*] upon all under the **universal canopy** [溥天之下 *pǔtiān zhīxià*],
To **ward off and resolve** [解禳 *jiěráng*] the **solar calamities of the Nine Yang** [陽九 *yáng jiǔ*] and the **terrestrial calamities of the One Hundred and Six** [百六 *bǎiliù*],
Including **wars and weapons** [兵戈 *bīnggē*], **epidemics** [疾疫 *jíyì*],
**Floods, fires, droughts, and locust plagues** [水火旱蝗 *shuǐhuǒ hànhuáng*],
And the **sufferings of famine and pestilence** [饥馑之厄 *jījǐn zhī è*].

We rely upon the **converged Daoist assembly** [坛道眾 *tándào zhòng*],
**Invoking the sacred titles** [持念天尊聖號 *chíniàn Tiānzūn shènghào*] of the Celestial Sovereigns,
And **recite in succession** [轉誦 *zhuàn sòng*] the **Scripture of the Great Incantation for Disaster Elimination by the Supreme Lord of the Eleven Luminaries** [《太上十一曜大消災神咒經》 *Tàishàng Shíyīyào Dàxiāozāi Shénzhòu Jīng*],
And the **Scripture of the Spirit Treasure Sovereign Lord for Disaster Warding and Eon Salvation** [《靈寶天尊禳災度厄真經》 *Língbǎo Tiānzūn Rángzāi Dùè Zhēnjīng*].

For within the **four seas** [四海 *sìhǎi*] and the **nine lands** [九地 *jiǔdì*],
From the **highest ranks of imperial lords and nobles** [帝王侯伯 *dìwáng hóubì*] to the **lowest of common folk and all things** [人民品物 *rénmín pǐnwù*],
All are governed by the **cyclic interplay of the Five Phases** [五行推運 *wǔxíng tuīyùn*],
And illuminated by the **radiance of the Eleven Luminaries** [眾曜照臨 *zhòngyào zhàolín*].
When **virtue or vice arise** [善惡一興 *shàn'è yīxīng*],
Then **calamities or blessings manifest accordingly** [祸福應見 *huòfú yìngjiàn*].

The **Nine Yang Solar Calamities** [陽九 *yáng jiǔ*] and the **One Hundred and Six Terrestrial Calamities** [百六 *bǎiliù*]
Cause the **eclipse of the sun and moon** [日月失昏 *rìyuè shīhūn*],
And the **erratic movement of the stars and constellations** [星宿錯度 *xīngxiù cuòdù*].
The greater disasters **imperil the august sovereign** [忧形帝主 *yōuxíng dìzhǔ*],
While the lesser afflict **all living beings** [災及生靈 *zāi jí shēnglíng*].
Or they **ignite fourfold wars** [兵革四興 *bīngé sìxīng*],
Or **spawn calamities and omens in competition** [災祥競起 *zāixiáng jìngqǐ*],
Bringing **the sufferings of famine, epidemics, insects, and locusts, floods, and fires** [饥荒疾疫之苦 *jīhuāng jíyì zhī kǔ*],
And **the perils of plagues, droughts, and conflagrations** [虫蝗水火之虞 *chónghuáng shuǐhuǒ zhī yú*].

To **eliminate disasters and dispel evil** [兔災以除凶 *tìzāi yǐ chúxiōng*],
One must **recite the scriptures and practice the Dao** [當誦經而行道 *dāng sòngjīng ér xíngdào*].

In ancient times, upon the **Great Luo Celestial Realm** [大羅天上 *Dàluó Tiānshàng*],
The **Primordial Compassionate Sovereign** [元始慈尊 *Yuánshǐ cízūn*] sounded the **law-drum** [法鼓 *fǎgǔ*],
And struck the **jade chimes** [琼钟 *qióngzhōng*],
Summoning the **ten directions** [十方 *shífāng*] and gathering the **multitude of saints** [眾聖 *zhòngshèng*],
To expound upon the **retribution of virtue and vice** [善惡之報應 *shàn'è zhī bàoyìng*],
And demonstrate the **causes of sin and blessings** [罪福之因緣 *zuìfú zhī yīnyuán*],
Displaying this scripture, **compassionate toward those yet unaware** [愍兹未悟 *mǐn zī wèi wú*],
With **merits profound and weighty** [功德深重 *gōngdé shēnzhòng*],
Whose **joy and celebration are beyond expression** [喜慶難言 *xǐqìng nányán*].

All who **aspire to cultivation and reverence** [有修崇 *yǒu xiūchóng*]
Should **diligently recite** [當勤訓誦 *dāng qín xùnsòng*].

May the **Seven Celestial Officials** [七政 *qīzhèng*] align in harmony,
And the **sovereign’s sacred deeds** [聖功 *shènggōng*] manifest in splendor,
May the **Five Stars** [五星 *wǔxīng*] converge,
And the **national fortune** [國祚 *guózhuó*] flourish in prosperity,
May **latent solar calamities** [潛消災變 *qiánxiāo zāibiàn*] be dispelled,
And the **radiant virtues of celestial illumination** [丕顯照臨之德 *pǔxiǎn zhàolín zhī dé*] shine forth,
May **auspicious clouds** [景雲 *jǐngyún*] present **divine omens** [呈瑞 *chéngruì*],
And **malevolent energies** [妖氣 *yāoqì*] be **banished** [屏收 *píngshōu*],
May the **world attain the utmost peace and order** [世臻極治之安 *shì zhēn jíjì zhī ān*],
And all **sentient beings recognize the joy of life** [人識有生之樂 *rén shí yǒushēng zhī lè*].

We now rely upon the **Pure and Numerous** [清眾 *Qīngzhòng*],
Each **invoking the sacred titles** [各持念 *gè chíniàn*] of the **Supreme Sovereign Lord of the Upper Eon’s Solar Palace** [上元日宮皇極天尊 *Shàngyuán Rìgōng Huángjí Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of the Middle Eon’s Lunar Palace** [中元月宮正一天尊 *Zhōngyuán Yuègōng Zhèng Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of the Lower Eon’s Stellar Palace** [下元星宮眾妙天尊 *Xiàyuán Xīnggōng Zhòngmiào Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of the Illuminating Clarity** [運明廣照天尊 *Yùnmíng Guǎngzhào Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of the Radiant Opening and Preservation of Life** [開輝保生天尊 *Kāihuī Bǎoshēng Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of the Luminous Sun and Moon** [日月光明天尊 *Rìyuè Guāngmíng Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of the Pure and Flowing Light** [清淨流光天尊 *Qīngjìng Liúguāng Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of Subduing Demons and Quelling Disturbances** [收魔滅惱天尊 *Shōumó Miènǎo Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of the Congealing Colors and Radiant Splendor** [凝彩光華天尊 *Níngcǎi Guānghuá Tiānzūn*],
The **Sovereign Lord of Eternal Protection of the Realm** [護國永安天尊 *Hùguó Yǒngān Tiānzūn*],
The **True Person of the Solar Light** [日光真人 *Rìguāng Zhēnrén*],
The **True Person of the Lunar Light** [月光真人 *Yuèguāng Zhēnrén*],
And the **True Person of the Stellar Light** [星光真人 *Xīngguāng Zhēnrén*],
Whose **inconceivable merits** [不可思議功德 *Bùkě Sīyì Gōngdé*] are profound.

Next, we **each recite** [各轉 *gè zhuàn*] the **Scripture of the Great Incantation for Disaster Elimination by the Eleven Luminaries** [《十一曜大消災神咒經》 *Shíyīyào Dàxiāozāi Shénzhòu Jīng*],
And the **Scripture of the Spirit Treasure for Disaster Warding and Eon Salvation** [《靈寶禳災度厄真經》 *Língbǎo Rángzāi Dùè Zhēnjīng*].

In the **third recitation** [第三時 *dì sān shí*],
We now **recite this third time** [以今第三遍 *yǐ jīn dì sān biàn*],
To **offer reverence to all beneath the universal canopy** [溥天之下 *pǔtiān zhīxià*],
Who have **contributed to the realm** [有功於國 *yǒugōng yú guó*],
And **should be honored with sacrificial rites** [應當祀典 *yìngdāng sìdiǎn*],
To the **divine officials of merit and virtue in all temples** [諸廟福德正神 *zhūmiào fúdé zhèngshén*],
To **augment their sacred radiance** [增助威光 *zēngzhù wēiguāng*],
And **secure the peace of the national borders** [保寧國界 *bǎoníng guójiè*].

We rely upon the **converged Daoist assembly** [坛道眾 *tándào zhòng*],
**Invoking the sacred titles** [持念天尊聖號 *chíniàn Tiānzūn shènghào*] of the Celestial Sovereigns,
And **recite in succession** [轉誦 *zhuàn sòng*] the **Scripture of the Supreme Ascension to the Mysterious for Disaster Elimination and Protection of Life** [《太上升玄消災護命妙經》 *Tàishàng Shēngxuán Xiāozāi Hùmìng Miàojīng*],
And the **Scripture of the Yellow Emperor’s Dark Sympathy** [《黃帝陰符經》 *Huángdì Yīnfǔ Jīng*],
To **extend reciprocal kindness** [以伸回施 *yǐ shēn huíshī*].

The **sweating wooden horse** manifests the **Divine General of Jin’s** extraordinary merit.
**Civilization flourishes in the realm**, and **sovereign majesty extends to the four seas**—
the **nation relies upon this for stability**, while **scholars and commoners alike turn to it in prayer**.

Now, the **Yellow Altar is erected**, and **reverently unveiled are the purple scrolls**—
**trusting in the Dao’s power**, we **aspire to exalt the sacred radiance**.

May **blessings perpetuate the imperial vision**, ensuring **eternal peace for all lands**;
may **names be inscribed in the Celestial Register**, ever **witnessing the boundless transformations of virtue**.

Then, **bestow blessings upon the ritual officers**, let **auspiciousness flow through the household**—
**no calamity shall remain unresolved**, and **every wish shall be fulfilled**.
**Relying upon this grace**, we **pledge with solemn devotion to repay with reverence**.

With **deepest reverence**, we **invoke the Pure-Origined Celestial Sovereign of Revealed Teaching**,
the **Celestial Sovereign of Great Auspicious Virtue**,
the **Celestial Sovereign of Compassionate Salvation Across Kalpas**,
the **Celestial Sovereign of Universal Liberation from Suffering**,
the **Celestial Sovereign of Boundless Spiritual Response**,
the **Celestial Sovereign of Transformed Manifestation Without Limit**,
the **Celestial Sovereign of Unobstructed Divine Power**,
the **True Person of Marvelous Conduct**,
the **True Person of Broad Faith**—
**inconceivable merit and virtue**.

Next, **recite in succession** the *Scripture of the Supreme Ascension to the Mysterious for Disaster Elimination and Protection of Life*,
and the *Scripture of the Yellow Emperor’s Dark Sympathy*.

**Fourth Session**
With this **fourth recitation**, we **offer on behalf of the ritual officer’s family**—
for **ancestors and departed kin**—
to **transmigrate and elevate their spirits**, ascending to the **Pure Realms**.

**Relying upon the assembled Daoist congregation**, we **invoke the Celestial Sovereigns’ sacred titles**,
and **recite in succession** the *Supreme Scripture of the Mysterious Treasure’s Boundless Liberation of Beings (Upper Grade)*.

For **Mysterious Treasure** is **one division of the Three Caverns**,
and **Boundless Liberation of Beings** is **one scroll of that division**.
Its **practices encompass many gates**,
while **its hymns commence with this volume**.

In ancient times, within the **True Realm of Floating Reeds**,
it was **first transmitted by the Sage of Memorized Discourse**,
initially **concealed in the Purple Micro Palace**,
its **manifest traces sealed away**—
a **hidden verse of the Celestial**, a **great scripture of the Dao**.
**Eight-cornered with radiant spikes**, it **originates from the Sovereign’s decree**;
**thousands of divine attendants** **universally guide humanity**.

Those who **nurture innate purity and rectitude**, harmonizing **heaven and earth**,
with **few desires and sincere thoughts**, abandoning **deceit for authenticity**,
**cleansing their minds through fasting**, **reciting with pure devotion**,
**accumulating inner concentration**, **radiating outer purity**—
**they may thus transform obscurity into clarity**, illuminating even the deepest darkness.
Like **white generated in an empty chamber**, or **evil dispelled by the Warm Springs**,
they **ascend joyfully to the Spring Terrace**, **crossing to the Realm of Longevity**.
**Sincerity’s reach knows no limit**; **auspiciousness is boundless**.

The *Scripture of the Treasure’s Liberation* **praises beyond measure**—
**gathering these wondrous virtues**, we **universally liberate the departed souls**.

May the **ancestors of past generations**, hearing this Scripture,
**pierce the True Principle**, **never forgetting their origin**,
soaring through the **forest of merit**, **freed from the duality of darkness and light**.

**Sacred texts transmute fate**; **alchemical fire refines the form**,
dwelling in **rewarding bodies within the Dao’s domain**.
Then, **ascending to the Azure Void**, **descending to the Golden Wheel**—
**all sentient beings alike attain the Dao’s shore**.

**Relying upon the Daoist assembly**, we **pray as above**,
each invoking the **Pure Heavenly Sovereign of the Void**,

**inconceivable merit and virtue**.
