**In the seventh session**, with this seventh recitation, we solemnly offer prayers for the **host of the ritual** [certain family] to **alleviate disasters and escape calamities**, to **invoke blessings and prolong life**.
Relying upon the **congregation of Daoists** at the assembled altar, we invoke the **sacred names of the Celestial Sovereigns** and recite the *True Scripture of the North and South Two Luchres for Prolonging Life*, praying for **auspicious blessings**.

**Indeed, the human body is hard to obtain**, and **birth in the Central Realm is rare**; even if one is born, **encountering the True Dao is difficult**.
The **wondrous teachings of the immortals** alone can **fully grasp the Dao’s power**—once the mind of faith arises, **illumination follows from past practice**.

In antiquity, the **Daoist Ancestor of the Mixed Primordial** **compassionately surveyed the lost multitude**; the **True Person of Oneness** **personally transmitted the sacred texts**.
Some were received from the **Jade Bureau**, others descended through **Crane’s Call**—all are the **true scriptures of the Nine Heavens and Eight Assemblies**, the **highest Dao of the Three Caverns and Three Purity Realms**, benefiting all beings and serving as the **ferry for crossing the sea of existence**.

**All who witness or hear**—how could they **lightly abandon life** while **ignoring their true origin**?
**Those who diligently read and recite**—thus do they **come to know their fate and return to the True**.

Here, we establish the **precious altar** and **unveil the profound essence**.
We wish the **ritual officials** [certain names] to **follow this practice and solemnly observe**, to **devote themselves to recitation**, so that the **Northern Treasury dispels calamities**, the **Southern Palace bestows wealth**, the **Dao-heart unfolds**, the **wisdom-nature clarifies**, **dusty toil is cleansed**, and **delusion is dispelled**—gradually ascending to the **wondrous fruit**, firmly rooted in the **mysterious merit**.

**Blessings extend to the living and the dead**, **merit permeates land and water**—forever transcending the **profane net**, all entering the **Golden Gate**,** fulfilling the True Oneness’s doctrine**, and **aligning with the Hermit’s intent**.

Relying upon the **congregation of Daoists** at the assembled altar, we invoke the **sacred names of the Celestial Sovereigns** and recite the *Supreme Scripture of True Oneness for Repaying Parental恩重*, the *Scripture of the Spiritually Martial for Repaying Parental恩重*.
**Since the Primordial Unity’s judgment**, the **Nine Qi** have **formed the body**—each breath of *qi* ceases not, each life perpetuates.
**Among all things**, only **humanity is most refined**.
Though we **draw our breath from Yin and Yang**, truly we **receive our form from our parents**.
**Hair and skin, flesh and bone**—each generation **passes the torch**.
**Countless kalpas** have come and gone, **numberless beyond reckoning**.
**The self-image arises**, then **decay begins**.
**Because of the self-image**, the **Six Kinships** emerge.
**Branches spread**, the **source fades**.

**Discussing lineage**, though ancient and modern differ—
**regarding virtue and vice**, past and present are **inextricably linked**.
Like **shadows following form**, they **cannot be separated**.

In days of old, the **Celestial Sovereign of the Western Jade Realm** **expounded the hardship of repaying恩**, and in the **Kaihuang Kalpa**, the **Supreme One** **admonished the unfilial child**—
**those who come after**, how could they **fail to reflect**?

**Through the ritual of the Yellow Register**, we **formally enact the secrets of the Lingbo**.
**For the parents now in the ancestral hall**, we pray they be **granted supreme longevity**, like **pine and cypress at a thousand years old**; we pray this **face may flourish**, like **peach and plum in spring’s breeze**.
**With reverent and humble devotion to their porridge and water**, we hope to **slightly repay their toil**.

**For the parents of the past**, may their **bodies escape the Abyssal Realm**, their **ears hear the True Dharma**—
so that **beneath the Nine Springs**, no **unanswered grudge remains**, and **within the Three Realms**, they **attain unbounded joy**.
Thus, **their endless longing is fulfilled**, and **their eternal thoughts are slightly consoled**.

Relying upon the **congregation of Daoists** at the assembled altar, we invoke the **sacred names of the Celestial Sovereigns** and recite the *Supreme Scripture of the Great Purity Heavenly Child for Protecting Life* and the *Scripture of the Wisdom Observation of the Body*, to **extend our gratitude**.

**The Daoist ritual concludes with the ninth scroll of the General Teachings.**

*«The Daoist adept Lü Taigu of the Crane Forest School’s *Essentials of Refined Thought* (精思篇) – A Ritual Invocation*

**Ritual Invocation (发奏):**
Without first announcing to the Earth and Land deities (*告土地*), the adept proceeds to the **outer altar** (*外坛*) and performs the **host’s preliminary rites** (*宿启*). Later generations expanded these rites with formal compositions, reducing them to mere announcements and the placement of written petitions (*寻置文牒*).

For those who practice the ritual while seated in the **Master’s position** (*师位*), additional **seals, incantations, and talismans** (*印诀符咒*) are employed, summoning the Earth and Land deities (*土地诸神*)—this tradition stems from the *Heavenly Heart Orthodoxy* (*天心正法*).

Now, this has become established practice: once the deities are seated, the adept must **invoke the talismans for divine transformation** (*如法文变神搯诀*) in accordance with the prescribed rites before proceeding.

As recorded at the beginning of this section:
**Ritual Invocation (发奏):**
The adept arranges the Earth and Land deities (*土地等神*) at the **Celestial Gate** (*天门*), and the **Daoist Master** (*法师*) sits at the **southeast corner** (*东南隅*).

Upon taking his seat, the Master first **harmonizes his own person** (*存己身*), donning the **Fish-Tail Crown** (*鱼尾冠*), wrapping himself in the **Fish-Mane Robe** (*鱼鬣衣*), and wearing **crimson shoes** (*朱履*), as prescribed by the **Celestial Master** (*天师*).

Then, he performs the **talismans for divine transformation** (*搯变神诀*):
With the **left hand’s ring finger** (*左手小指*), he curves it backward from the **fourth finger** (*四指*), bending it into the **root of the middle finger** (*中指根*). The **fourth finger** (*四指*) is curled inward toward the **palm** (*掌心*), while the **middle finger** (*中指*) hooks and secures the **ring finger** (*小指*). The **thumb** (*大指*) then presses against the **middle joint of the middle finger** (*中指中节*). After releasing the **thumb** (*弹了大指*), he presses the **root of the second finger** (*第二指根*).

This is the **original Master’s seal and talisman** (*本师印诀*), invoking the **Six Jia and Six Ding** (*六甲六丁*), the **Four Celestial Gate Kings** (*四天门王*), the **Azure Dragon and White Tiger** (*青龙白虎*), and the **Vermilion Bird and Dark Tortoise** (*朱雀玄武*), arrayed in concentric ranks around him. Next, he invokes the **Earth and Land officials** (*土、地申奏官属*), who stand at the **Celestial Gate** (*天门*) awaiting command, each distinctly recognized.

Afterward, he **proclaims the summons** (*宣召*), directing them with his intent (*入意指挥*), and concludes with the **dismissal and farewell invocation** (*发引遣表*).

The Master, with his **left hand forming the talisman** (*搯印诀*), raises his **two fingers** (*二指*) to summon the scripture. With his **right hand wielding the Threefold Fire** (*仗三昧火*), he strikes the **roots of his four fingers** (*四指根节*) and recites the **Sword-Water Incantation** (*剑水咒*). Upon finishing the incantation (*噀水讫*), he **plants the sword** (*卓剑*).

At the **right side of his seat** (*坐右*), he forms the **Sword Talisman** (*卓剑诀*), striking the **root of his middle finger** (*右手中指根节*) toward the sword. Next, he **burns incense** (*焚香*), repeating the earlier **talisman for divine transformation** (*仍搯前变神诀*), visualizing the **Three Platform Stars** (*三台星*) upon the **back of his thumb** (*大指背*), known as the **Seven-Star Talisman** (*七星诀*).

After reciting the scripture and proclaiming the petitions (*念文宣牒讫*), he **dismisses the deities with incantations** (*遣牒诵咒*), invoking the **True Qi of the Great Sun** (*太阳赤气*), the **True Qi of the Great Moon** (*太阴白气*), and the **Three Platform Seven-Star True Qi** (*三台七星真气*), channeling them into the water (*流注水中*), and **drawing the qi with the sword** (*执剑取气*).

Upon finishing the incantation (*噀水讫*), the Master **directs his tongue to the upper palate** (*以舌主上腭*), transforming it into a **Golden Bridge** (*化为金桥*), allowing the Earth and Land officials to **deliver their petitions directly to the Celestial Gate** (*令土地申奏，从桥上径达天门*).

When the ritual is complete (*事讫*), he **restores the deities and offers repentance** (*还神回向*).

Extracted from the *Heavenly Heart Orthodoxy* (*天心正法*), recorded as *White Announcement of the Deities* (*白事*).»

The **Master of Qingdu Dao**, Zhang Wanfu, states:

*"The Daoist ritual of fasting is strict and exacting; all celestial deities and sages descend to observe. Every matter must conform to proper ritual standards, without neglecting or abandoning the prescribed rites and procedures."*

The **Great Cavern Master**, Xie Fanglai, further says:

*"When performing high-level petitionary rites, one must face east and stand upright. Below the rank of *Dujian* (都讲), all should face west to form a single rank. Standing upright, holding the tally tablet and bowing respectfully, one must regulate one’s breath and steady one’s *qi*, speak in measured, modest words, and maintain simplicity in ritual language. One must not raise one’s voice harshly, nor indulge in excessive ornamentation. Words should be concise, and meaning must be clear—avoid artificial embellishments, lest sincerity be lost."*

*"In all supplications, one must first repent of one’s transgressions before reporting the matter."*

Zhang Wanfu again says:

*"When ascending the platform to practice the Dao, one must first purify with incense and water, known as *Dangji* (荡秽). To draw forth and seal the *qi*, one must also purify, known as *Bizhenqi* (闭真气). When ascending the platform, one must strictly follow the ritual procedures established by the two Masters Zhang and Du. Before performing any rites, one must first go before the **Mysterious Master** (*玄师*), arrange the ranks, and chant the Dao. Upon reaching the platform’s entrance, one must hold the incantation and circle counterclockwise before ascending the **Celestial Gate** (*天门*) and offering incense to the Ten Directions. Then, one proceeds to the uppermost rank and performs the rites there—never omitting the proper announcement at the base of the platform, for such an omission is unknown in the original traditions and deviates from their intent.*

*"Indeed, from the **Ritual Master** (*礼师*), the **Qi-Storing Master** (*存神*), and the **Furnace-Opening Master** (*发炉*), all are meant to harmonize the inner and outer *qi*. Only after the **Spirit Official** (*灵官*)’s solemn rites are completed does one then invoke the **Daoist rank** (*法位*) and petition the **True Saints** (*诸真圣*). The logic of the announcement is clear and direct—omitting the base-platform announcement leaves no room for doubt or confusion.*

**Nighttime Entrance Incantation** (*夜入户咒*):
*"Standing to the left of the earthly entrance, thrice strike the teeth in reverence, and in secret invoke the **Four Bright Officials** (*四明功曹*), the **Dragon-Tiger Envoys** (*龙虎使者*), the **True One Originating Qi** (*正一生气*), and the **Attendant Pure Maiden** (*侍靖素女*). If there are matters to be reported at night, I pray for the **Open-Mind Child** (*开明童子*) and the **Upper Primordial Maiden** (*上元少女*) to accompany me into the hall and platform, conveying my petitions so that they may be heard above."*

**Nighttime Exit Incantation** (*夜出户咒*):
*"Exit the **Great Cavern** (*大洞*), ascending the **Great Yin** (*太阴*), the eight windows of illumination open, and all that has been presented is conveyed by the Pure Maiden."*

*"After the rites are finished, return to one’s proper station, and all the deities retreat in solemn rest. In the morning, the **Entrance Incantation** (*入户咒*) is:*
*'Four Bright Officials, the **Pure Truth Envoys** (*通真使者*), the **Jade-Tongued Youth** (*传言玉童*), and the **Attendant Pure Maiden**, I pray that you convey my petitions to the **True Deities** (*正神*) of the hall and platform, the **Primordial Originating Qi** (*上元生气*), and that they descend into my body.'*

**Morning Exit Incantation** (*朝出户咒*):
*'Exit the **Great Yin** and enter the **Great Yang** (*出阴入阳*), and all the deities are opened and communicated.'"*

Extracted from the *Heavenly Heart Orthodoxy* (*天心正法*), recorded as *White Announcement of the Deities* (*白事*).

After the rites are completed, the **Yellow Chamber** is closed. The **Attendant Pure Maiden** (*侍靖玉女*) stands vigilant in the sacred hall.

From the *Clarified Truth Rites* (*明真科*) of **Lu Tian师**, preserved by **Jianji Lu Tian师**:

*"The Dao begins with fasting; fasting begins with scripture. In observing fasting rites, one must first focus the mind with precision. In honoring the scriptures’ authority, one must ground oneself in stillness of thought. If the foundation is not upright, the ritual decorum will falter, failing to align with the scriptures—how then could one invoke the Mysterious Saints and attain virtue and wisdom? Drawing from myriad scriptures, I have marked their essential truths, following the ancestral traditions to aid practitioners.

Here is the **Essential Method for Concentrated Dao Practice and Spirit-Nurturing** (*道法精思存神诀*). Each practitioner must observe the teacher’s presence in accordance with the method.

Stand upright, close the eyes, and focus the spirit.

First, focus on the **Three Supreme Sovereigns** (*太上三尊*), seated upon the **Celestial Treasure Platform** (*天宝台*). To their left stand the **Thirty-Six Departments of Venerable Scriptures** (*三十六部尊经*), and to their right, the **Grand Master of the Mysterious Middle** (*玄中大法师*), the **Ten True Ones and Five Emperors** (*十真五帝*), with the assembled immortals and celestial attendants arrayed as in a grand court audience.

Next, focus on the **Scripture Master’s** presence, bowing inwardly three times, honoring the master’s lineage. Then focus on the **Transmission Master’s** presence, bowing inwardly three times, honoring the master’s lineage. Then focus on the **Initiation Master’s** presence, bowing inwardly three times, honoring one’s own lineage.

May my three masters ascend to the heights of the immortals, opening the way for my seven ancestral parents to swiftly attain the Celestial Hall, and may my name be inscribed among the immortals, forever as a **True Person** (*真人*).

At dawn, the **Yin Hour** (*寅时*), visualize **Green Qi** (*青气*) rising from the liver, ascending like clouds, encircling the altar hall. The **Azure Dragon** and **Lion** guard the fore and aft.

The **Celestial and Earthly Immortals**, **Heavenly Maidens and Jade Boys**, the **Solar, Lunar, and Stellar Hosts**, the **Five Emperors’ Armies**, each numbering ninety million, along with the **Supervising Officials of the Fast** and the **Three Realms’ Attendants**, array themselves on either side, enveloping the disciple’s dwelling—great and small—with cloud-mist.

At noon, the **Yang Hour** (*午时*), visualize **Red Qi** (*赤气*) rising from the heart, ascending like clouds, raining down upon the altar hall. The **Vermilion Bird** and **White Crane** guard the fore and aft.

The **Celestial and Earthly Immortals**, **Heavenly Maidens and Jade Boys**, the **Solar, Lunar, and Stellar Hosts**, the **Five Emperors’ Armies**, the **Supervising Officials of the Fast**, and the **Three Realms’ Attendants** array themselves on either side, enveloping the disciple’s dwelling—great and small—with cloud-mist.

At nightfall, the **Hai Hour** (*戌时*), visualize **White Qi** (*白气*) rising from the lungs, ascending like clouds, encircling the altar hall. The **White Tiger** and **Qilin** guard the four quarters.

The **Celestial and Earthly Immortals**, **Heavenly Maidens and Jade Boys**, the **Solar, Lunar, and Stellar Hosts**, the **Five Emperors’ Armies**, the **Supervising Officials of the Fast**, and the **Three Realms’ Attendants** array themselves on either side, enveloping the disciple’s dwelling—great and small—with cloud-mist.

Further, visualize the **Five Stars**, **Five Sacred Peaks**, and **Five Emperors** guarding one’s form. The **Five Zang Qi** ascend in radiant disorder, crowning the body like mist, as if enshrouded in vapor. A **Golden Radiance** (*金华*) crowns the head, transforming the body into gold, first emerging from the lungs, with a round luminous orb atop the crown—like the sun’s symbol—illuminating the ten directions. Within the body, all is clear, both inner and outer, fully revealed.

Then, practice the **Mysterious Observations**, penetrating the **Void and Profound**. This method is to be employed day and night, at the three critical hours."

Next, strike the **Law Drum** twenty-four times. The **Law Drum**—by gathering inner **qi** and aweing external spirits—is the first act of ritual. When striking the door’s upper and lower beams in rhythm, this is called the **Law Drum**. After every eight strikes, pause briefly, symbolizing the twenty-four **qi** phases of the cosmos.

Master Wanfu of the Celestial Masters said: *"The scriptures state that the Law Drum has three methods. First, strike silently without sound; second, strike so that it is heard; third, strike with an open mouth and relaxed cheeks, producing a deep, resonant sound—this is the method of self-cultivation. If the ritual assembly is large and noisy, striking silently is best, for then one’s mind may focus with precision, and the **qi** remains tranquil."*

The above method of **mindful striking** is recorded in the *Treatise on Natural Etiquette* and the *Golden Talisman Simplified Texts*.

According to the **refined contemplation** decreed by Master Lu, now called **"commanding demons through visualization"**—this is specifically for **Stepping Through the Void** (*bùxū*). Since **Stepping Through the Void** follows **commanding demons**, one first visualizes, then commands the demons, and proceeds to **Stepping Through the Void**. Indeed, all matters within **Stepping Through the Void** align with the *Jade Capital Stepping Through the Void Scripture*, hence the reliance on Master Lu’s teachings, detailed here.

**Refined Contemplation for Stepping Through the Void**
Master Lu said: *"When reciting the Stepping Through the Void Scripture, first strike the teeth three times, swallow saliva three times, and visualize the sun and moon upon your face. Let them enter through your nostrils into the Golden Flower Palace of the Inner Chamber, their radiance emerging from the nape, forming a nine-colored circular luminosity that descends into the Jade Pillow, illuminating the ten directions. As you circle the scripture in rotation, complete the practice, then strike the teeth three times and swallow saliva three times."*

*(Excerpted from the *Supreme Jade Scripture’s Hidden Commentary*)*
*The explanation of this method is also by Master Lu.*

**Refined Contemplation for Stepping Through the Void** *(continued)*

*"Visualize the sun and moon upon your own face. The sun’s hue is red, with a purple radiance of nine rays. The moon’s hue is yellow, with a white radiance of ten rays. The sun stands to your left, the moon to your right, nine chi distant from your face. The sun’s rays descend straight from the left, entering through the left nostril. The moon’s rays descend straight from the right, entering through the right nostril. Together, they penetrate into the Golden Flower Palace of the Inner Chamber. The Golden Flower Palace is the point five cun directly inward from between the brows. Their radiance then descends into the Jade Pillow, emerging from the nape. The entire head is called the Níhuán Palace; one cun inward from the brows is the Míngtáng Palace, two cun the Dòngfáng Palace, three cun the Dāntián Palace, four cun the Liúzhū Palace, and five cun the Jīnhuá Palace—also known as the Inner Chamber of the Female Golden Flower. It is also called the Palace of the Jade Emperor, each palace being one cun in depth, thus forming the Níhuán Dòngmíng Mirror, which completes the likeness of the Golden Flower Immortal. Once the visualization is complete, then recite the verses of the Stepping Through the Void Scripture.*

*According to Master Dù’s established ritual, the Daoist Master of Exorcism is stationed at the Ghost Gate, facing west. The Grand Master is stationed at the Heavenly Gate, facing east, and each chants while visualizing the nine-colored circular luminosity and swallowing saliva to invoke the secret exorcism spells. From the High Functionary downward, each performs the visualization in turn. Since Master Yáng’s establishment of the Golden Talisman Ritual, the Master of Exorcism has been stationed at the Heavenly Gate. Now, no further changes are made; instead, each follows the prescribed method as recorded in the scripture. The Exorcism Spell reads:*

*'Huángzhōng cè qì zhǎn yāo zōng,*
*Chá zhì qiáng jīng duàn xié wēng.*
*Tàishàng yǒu mìng Tàishàng fáng,*
*jí chào běi dì yì yù gōng.*
*Shòu chéng wēi lìng xuān máo wáng,*
*wǔ qì wěng yù yǔ mìng chōng.*
*Bì cáng yù wén fāng jiù lóng,*
*sān tiān yùn míng liù tiān zhōng.*

*Master Dù said: ‘This spell must be recited silently; do not let your own ears hear it. Violating this brings misfortune—be cautious, be cautious.’*

*From the *Wǔ Fú Rén Niǎo Jīng*, Master Zhào Míngjǔ states: ‘Though divided into nine colors, the essence remains the Primordial Xuan Yuan alone. For the nine colors originate from the Three Qi—Qīng, Huáng, and Bái. If further divided into colors like Zǐ and Bǐ, it becomes overly complex and loses its simplicity. Thus, the Three Qi are divided into Nine Qi for the exorcism.’*

**Explanation of the Exorcism Ritual**
*Master Zhāng Wànfú of the Qingdū School says: ‘Before the Celestial Venerable spoke the scripture, the demon kings of the Three Realms and Ten Thousand Worlds were the leaders of all ghosts, wielding power and poisoning the world, harming living beings. After the Celestial Venerable spoke the scripture, the demons submitted and transformed, guarding the Dao and protecting the law. They restrained the myriad demons, safeguarding those who practice genuine cultivation, thus enabling their ascension into the ranks of immortals. Hence it is said: “Any who dare to obstruct those practicing genuine cultivation shall be slain by the Golden Axe and punished by the Great Queen of the Afterworld.” It is also said: “The Great Demon King, upholding the Ascended Immortal, has fully attained the Dao and now wanders the Three Realms, entering the Golden Gate.” And again: “The Eastern Extermination of demonic essences, the beheading of the Six Ghostly Chiefs—this is the meaning.” Thus, the invocation of demons refers to summoning the demon kings of the Ten Thousand Worlds to uphold the merit of the ritual, to restrain and subdue malevolent ghosts. The *Stepping Through the Void Scripture* states: “The demon kings respectfully receive the ritual’s command, thus able to attend the Celestial Assembly. Both celestial and demonic beings respect and protect, receiving great blessings in this world and the next. The scattered flowers express my vow, the clenched talisman summons the demon kings.”*

**Refined Contemplation for Reciting the Scripture**
*According to Master Dù’s ritual guidance, when reciting the scripture’s verses, one must reach the stage of silent, lawful contemplation. Then, the Master follows the scripture’s instructions, visualizing while reciting the spells. However, the ritual text does not specify the method of visualization; thus, it is recorded here according to Master Lu’s diagrams and instructions.*

**Visualization and Spiritual Preservation from the *Dào Dé Jīng***
*The *Tàijí Yǐnzhù* states: ‘When reading the *Dào Dé Jīng* of the Celestial Venerable, first burn incense, adjust your attire, and bow three times. Visualize the Primordial Daoist Master, the Celestial Venerable Lǎojūn, who in the past was the Primordial Daoist Master of the Riverbank, Yín Xiansheng. Recite the spells while visualizing:*

*"Xuán xuán zhì dào zōng,*
*Shàng dé tǐ hóng yuán.*
*Tiān zhēn suī yuǎn miào,*
*Jìn yuán níhuán jūn.*

*Though distant, the Celestial Venerable is near in essence—*
*the Níhuán Palace, where the Jade Emperor resides,*
*is the brain’s center. Its halls are adorned with seven treasures,*
*its windows and doors self-illuminating.*
*The ever-present purity and tranquility bring forth the True,*
*ascending in the radiance, riding upon the purple clouds.*
*The sun and moon shine left and right,*
*eternal immortality is preserved within.*
*The Seven Ancestors ascend to Heaven,*
*through generations, they guard the Dao of Virtue and Power.*

*Complete the recitation with thirty-six strikes of the teeth,*
*thirty-six swallows of saliva,*
*and visualize the Azure Dragon to your left,*
*the White Tiger to your right,*
*the Vermilion Bird before you,*
*the Dark Tortoise behind,*
*the Eight Trigrams Spirit Tortoise,*
*and thirty-six lions arrayed ahead,*
*the Seven Stars of the Head bowed inward,*
*with the Dipper’s handle pointing forward.*
*The five zàng-organs’ five-colored qi*
*cover your body like a brocade pattern.*
*The Three-One True Person stands before the scripture,*
*your own Three Teachers arrayed in ten thousand chariots,*
*guarding left and right.*
*Once fully comprehended,*
*then recite the scripture.*

*The *Sìjí Kē* states: ‘When reading the scripture, let your heart and mouth move in harmony, your eyes see nothing else, your mind harbor no other thoughts. Complete each phrase without omitting or rushing the Celestial Venerable’s words—three violations bring blame.’*

*The *Tàijí Yǐnzhù* states: ‘After reciting five hundred words of the scripture, strike the teeth three times, let the tongue moist the upper and lower lips, and swallow saliva three times—this prevents exhaustion.’*

**Visualization and Spiritual Preservation from the *Dù Rén Jīng***
*The scripture states: ‘On the day of practicing the Dao, bathe in fragrant water and purify yourself in seclusion. Facing east, strike the teeth thirty-two times, invoking the thirty-two heavens above. Bow thirty-two times in your heart, swallow saliva thirty-two times. Close your eyes and sit in still contemplation, your body resting within the three-colored clouds of Qīng, Huáng, and Bái. Within and without, all is dense and mysterious. Visualize the Azure Dragon, White Tiger, Vermilion Bird, Dark Tortoise, Lions, and White Cranes arrayed to your left and right. The sun and moon shine brightly, illuminating the chamber within. A circular luminosity forms at the nape, its light reflecting in the ten directions—thus, all is clear and distinct."*

---

**Secret Incantation:**

*"Thus it is spoken."*

**Explanation of the Method:**
Strike the teeth and bow in heart—
store the thirty-two heavens in the four directions:
the Azure Dragon to the left,
the White Tiger to the right,
the Vermilion Bird before you,
the Dark Tortoise behind.
The White Crane and Lions arrayed in their places.

The sun and moon stand nine *chi* before you,
their light illuminating the ten directions.

Draw *qi* through the nose thirty-two times,
ensuring no sound escapes the ears.
Face east and recite the scripture.

---
**From the *Nán-Běi Dǒu Jīng* (Scripture of the Southern and Northern Dipper):**
**Method of Concentrated Thought and Spirit Preservation**

Face north and sit upright.
Strike the teeth twenty-four times.
In heart, store the Most High Laozi,
the Three Heavenly Masters,
and the True Persons of left and right above.
Bow three times in heart.

Next, store the Six Stars of the Southern Dipper to the right,
the Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper to the left.
With sincerity, pray and wish for the Ten Precepts of the Immortal Officials,
the Three Thousand Southern Envoys,
the Seven Thousand Northern Divine Generals,
and the attendants on either side—
all clearly manifest.

Then recite the scripture and chant the incantation:

*"In the late Eastern Han, at the start of the Yongshou era,
the Celestial Master rode a White Crane,
the Most High drove a Dragon Chariot.
Five clouds descended from heaven,
the Celestial Procession arrived in Chengdu.
Earthly gods surged forth with a jade array,
its height exceeding ten *chi*.
The Most High ascended the jade seat,
transmitting the Nine Heavenly Scriptures,
the method of cutting death and prolonging life,
and the Seven Elements governing the world.
The Scripture of Prolonging Life and Saving Others—
the Six Ministries all bear talismans.
Those who practice the Dao and cultivate,
reading this, shall have their calamities removed.
Now I recite the sacred text,
and officials and ministers aid me in secret.
I shall establish the Mysterious Merit,
and through wondrous Dao attain the Void."*

---
**Incantation of the *Dàodé Jīng* (Classic of the Way and Its Power):**

*"The Heavenly Teacher of countless eons,
the Great Sage, the Primordial Lord,
once in the Palace of Great Clarity,
wrote five thousand characters.
Shun, the filial son of Yu,
transmitted it to the Most High,
its secrets not revealed to the world,
its mysteries passed down without end.
In the late Zhou, during King Zhao’s reign,
he rode the winds on a purple cloud,
Yin Xi guarded the Gloomy Pass,
gazing to welcome the flying wheel.
Crossing the Western Sands, the Most High arrived at the Pass,
and at noon again transmitted the *Dàodé Jīng*.
Its meaning encompasses all that is great and small,
nothing too vast or minute to discuss.
Now I expound the True Scriptures,
unfolding the roots of heaven and earth.
I wish to follow the Supreme Dao,
that my family and nation may share its blessings.
May the Emperor-King preserve his ten thousand years,
ultimately ascending to the Celestial Gate."*

---
**Incantation of the *Dù Rén Jīng* (Scripture of Saving Others):**

*"Blessed be the Primordial Lord,
who in the Beginning of Azure Heaven
suspended pearls like millet grains,
drawing ten-directional immortals.
He taught the Dao to save others,
the precious chapter named *Dòng Xuán* (Mysterious and Profound).
The Thirty-Two Heavenly Emperors,
their inner names and hidden titles complete.
The Great Demons of the Three Realms,
sing only hollow verses.
The Great Brahman’s hidden speech,
the Sovereign’s own compilation.
The High True Ones descended to rescue,
transmitting the method of saving fateful souls.
For five eons, the teachings spread far,
those saved without number.
Now I face east and recite,
wishing to match the heavens in years.
May the Emperor-King preserve his peace and stability,
and the Nine Ancestors all ascend as immortals.
When merit is complete and virtue fulfilled,
I shall rise on clouds and mist."*

---
**Incantation of the *Shēng Shén Jīng* (Scripture of Nourishing the Spirit):**

*"Blessed be the Primordial Lord,
reclining in the Yellow Palace.
Qi Yi cultivated the Great Primordial,
refining the void and blending the pure.
He flew from heaven to pay homage,
laying out the end of the eon.
It is fitting to practice the Great Method,
broadly saving the ignorant and deluded.
The Heavenly Sage rescues the wise and foolish,
the jade case opens with clarity.
He revealed the *Shēng Shén* Chapter,
unfolding the Nine *Qi* Principles.
With focused heart, I bow and recite,
those saved without end.
Now I unfold the Cloud Brocade,
completing the Nine Transformations of humanity.
When merit is complete and virtue fulfilled,
I shall ride the Light and the Cloud Dragon."*

**Upon completion of the ritual:**
Concentrated thought and spirit preservation.
Strike the teeth twenty-four times.
Before opening your eyes, first store the Three Pure Ones at the crown,
the assemblies of the *Dàodé* honored ones gathered before you.
The Azure Dragon, White Tiger, Vermilion Bird, and Dark Tortoise
stand to your left, right, front, and back.
Your body grows over ten *chi* in length,
your form radiant as golden flowers.
The crimson gate of your door opens at the crown.
True officials, soldiers, and ministers
all emerge from the crown.
The Tiger General stands at the nose,
the Heavenly Laborers at the shoulders,
the Wolf Officials at the neck,
the Directing Messengers at the cheeks,
the Heavenly Steeds at the arms,
the Armored Soldiers at the fingertips,
the Deliberate Cavalry and Hooked Riders in the abdomen,
the Three Generals in the heart,
the Science Carriages and Red Talismans at the navel,
the Three Officials and Secretaries in the stomach,
the *Gāngfēng* Cavalry stationed at the knees,
the Relay Horses bearing dispatches at the calves,
the *Qi*-Collecting Officials along the twenty-four vertebrae,
the Green-Robed Village Lords before you.
The Directing Functionaries hold the tablets and staves—
each clearly manifest.
Then open your eyes and conclude the ritual.
Strike the teeth three times,
swallow saliva three times.
Proclaim the chapter,
recite the *Tàiqīng* (Supreme Clarity) text.

From *Yīn Zhēn Rén’s* *Wèn Kē Jīng* (Scripture of Questioning the Laws)
and the Celestial Master’s *Wèn Fǎ Jīng* (Scripture of Questioning the Dao):
The Celestial Master told the Most High:
*"There are those who read the *Tàiqīng* first, then report it;
or report it first, then read the *Tàiqīng*;
or read the *Tàiqīng* characters first, then report, then state their surname;
or break off and read the *Tàiqīng* last.
These differ—what is the correct method?"*

The Most High said:
*"When reporting is complete, then state your surname,
then read the *Tàiqīng*, then the year number,
each separated by three lines—
this is the unchanging method of writing the chapter.
But when proclaiming aloud,
reporting is complete, then kneel deeply and grasp the extreme,
first read the *Tàiqīng*, speaking the fine characters softly.
Do not let the voice rise sharply—
do not cough or swallow saliva.
Recite in one breath, then state your surname,
then the year number—
this is the Heavenly Emperor’s complete method."*

---
**Zhào Míngjǔ’s Master’s Method of Spreading *Qi* and Chanting the Seal:**

*"The Three *Qi* originally merge to form the body,
the Primordial Sovereign’s features now clear.
Within lies the Dao of the Mysterious and the Void,
but fear the times may lack precision in learning."*

**Seal of the Seven Elements, the Leader, the Dipper, and the True Form Talisman:**

*"The chapter’s seals and all ritual diagrams
are unseen in the scriptures—
such as the *Bǎozhāng Lì* of the Red Pine Child,
the talismans of Broad Achievement Master,
and the *Jīn Guàn* ritual diagrams—
none are recorded."*

*"One must inquire of the venerable past masters and say: 'In my youth, I still saw my predecessors, at the moment, use a red brush to inscribe this talisman upon the ritual diagrams, its height and depth forming the **Northern Dipper** constellation. Truly, this was meant to guard and protect the ritual diagrams, ensuring their efficacy must reach its fullest extent.

'Later, upon examining the **Broad Achievement Master’s Purple Court Ritual** of the Northern Obscurity, I saw the **Seven Elements Seal** inscribed upon yellow silk, wrapped around the words of the ritual, and sealed within the case. Only then did I believe the words of the venerable past masters were not false.

'With reverence, I publish this method, and further explain their reasoning: 'Nowadays, these talismans are made as seals, but this is a later private interpretation. The **True Form Talisman** of the **Heavenly Emperor’s Supreme Seal**—I bow twice to report this. Bow twice, then state your name: **"Uppermost Way" (太清上) and "Lowest Way" (太清下)**, the **True Form Talisman** of the **Heavenly Sovereign (太歲)**, and the **Three Generals Seal** are inscribed upon the right side of the ritual case.

'The **Six Celestial Stems Seal** of **Yin-Yang**—two talismans, one for each—from **Jiazi (甲子)** to **Yihou (乙丑)**, each having its own seal. The lower one must always conclude with the **Yin Seal** and the **Yang Seal**. **Jiazi** represents **Yang**, **Yihou** represents **Yin**; **Yang** governs the **Yang Realm**, **Yin** governs the **Yin Realm**.

'Now, when spreading the talisman, this involves matters of the **Yang Realm**, so one must use the **Yang Seal**. Yet, in common practice, many inscribe the **Yin Seal** upon the case and use both talismans together, with incantations beneath them. The **Yang Seal** reads:

*'**Midheaven Great Sage** (中天大聖), **Flying Heaven Swift** (飛天捷疾), seizes and apprehends the **Yang Jade Realm’s** ghosts—those within the **Yang Realm** and the lower **Yin-Yang Void**—and delivers them to the **Northern Prison of Heaven One** (天一北獄), where they are judged according to the **Dharma Law** (律). The **Tang Gezhou Generals** (唐葛周將軍) and the **True Martial General** (真武將軍) await with drawn swords.'

The **Yin Seal** reads:

*'**Midheaven Great Sage** (中天大聖), **Flying Heaven Swift** (飛天捷疾), seizes and apprehends the **Yin Jade Realm’s** ghosts—those within the **Yin Realm** and the five **Void Directions** (五方無道之鬼)—and delivers them to the **Northern Prison of Heaven One** (天一北獄), where they are judged according to the **Dharma Law** (律). The **Tang Gezhou Generals** (唐葛周將軍) and the **Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water** (天地水三官) come to their aid.

'The **Dissolving Form Talisman** follows the same structure as above: **"Midheaven Great Sage" (中天大聖), "Flying Heaven Swift" (飛天捷疾), seizing and apprehending the **Yang Jade Realm’s** ghosts—those within the **Yang Realm** and the **Yin-Yang Void**—as the **True Martial General** (真武將軍) awaits with drawn swords, up to the **Tang Gezhou Generals** (唐葛周將軍). The **Yin Seal** follows this pattern accordingly.

'The **Supine Talisman** and the **Stepfighting Dipper Diagram** (伏章步斗圖) are also included."*

At this juncture, the **Celestial Rotation** (乾旋) is invoked within the **Fighting Man** (人斗) through the **Supine Talisman** (伏章) and the **Stepfighting Dipper Diagram** (步斗歌):

*"Kàn* (坎) and *Gèn* (艮) move in paired single steps, crossing *Qián* (乾);
*Zhèn* (震) advances in double ranks, as does *Duì* (兑) likewise.
*Kūn* (坤) follows *Lí* (离) in paired single steps, while *Xùn* (巽) turns—
When the **Three Stars** (三台) return, they ascend to **Heaven** (朝天).

The **Preserved Talisman** (存章) reflects the **Divine Method** (神法), as recorded in **Master Sun’s** teachings within his collection.

This is the **Most High’s** (太上) hidden secret—though preserved in written scrolls, the **heart-method** (心法) is a self-realized mystery, beyond words.

Since **Master Sun** has already revealed it, yet instructed that my disciples should guard this doctrine, lest it be carelessly disclosed to others, I refrain from further engraving or mass reproduction, lest the **Heavenly Secrets** (天秘) be widely leaked. Future seekers who pay heed should consult **Master Sun’s** original text and inquire into its hidden meanings from those of earlier attainment.

This is the **Dao Gate’s** (道門) universal teaching, which must be found within the **Ninth Volume** (集卷之九) of its compilation.
